For elliptical, we can use:\n- Circular approximation: treat as circular at semi-major axis\n- Or use the actual velocities\n\nFor simplicity and robustness, let me use a combined metric:\n- Compute the minimum delta-V needed accounting for semi-major axis change and plane change\n\nActually, the simplest reasonable metric: |v1 - v2| (relative velocity) gives an upper bound on delta-V. But this doesn\'t account for phasing.\n\nLet me use a more principled approach:\n1. Compute circular velocity at each orbit\'s semi-major axis\n2. Use Hohmann transfer delta-V as baseline\n3. Add plane change cost\n\nFor the starting position, we treat it as another orbit from which we start.\n\nLet me think about the cost matrix:\n- We have N stations + 1 starting position\n- cost[i][j] = delta-V to go from station i to station j\n- For the starting position, cost[start][j] for each j\n- We want to find the order of visiting all N stations starting from the start position\n- The total cost is cost[start][s0] + cost[s0][s1] + ... + cost[s_{N-2}][s_{N-1}]\n- No return required\n\nSo this is an open TSP (no return to start).\n\nFor the Held-Karp DP with open TSP:\n- dp[mask][i] = min cost to visit all stations in mask, ending at station i\n- Transition: dp[mask | (1<<j)][j] = min(dp[mask][i] + cost[i][j])\n- Initial: dp[1<<i][i] = cost_from_start[i]\n- Answer: min over i of dp[(1<<N)-1][i]\n\nLet me code this up carefully.\n\n### Memory for Held-Karp\n- N=20: 2^20 * 20 * 8 bytes = ~160 MB - feasible\n- N=25: 2^25 * 25 * 8 bytes = ~6.7 GB - not feasible\n- N=22: 2^22 * 22 * 8 = ~700 MB - borderline\n- I\'ll use Held-Karp for N ≤ 20, heuristics for N > 20\n\nActually with 127 GB RAM, maybe N ≤ 22 or 23. vector\n    static double SemiMajorAxis(double[] rv) {\n        double rx=rv[0],ry=rv[1],rz=rv[2];\n        double vx=rv[3],vy=rv[4],vz=rv[5];\n        double r = Math.Sqrt(rx*rx+ry*ry+rz*rz);\n        }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    static int[] SolveTSP() {\n        if (N == 1) return new int[]{0};\n        if (N <= 20) return HeldKarp();\n        else return LargeScaleSolve();\n    }\n    \n    static int[] HeldKarp() {\n        // dp[mask][i] = min cost to visit all stations in mask, ending at station i+1 (0-indexed stations)\n        // Stations are indexed 0..N-1, corresponding to costMatrix indices 1..N\n        // Start is costMatrix index 0\n        \n        int full = 1 << N;\n        double[,] dp = new double[full, N];\n        int[,] parent = new int[full, N];\n        \n        for (int m = 0; m < full; m++)\n            for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) {\n                dp[m, i] = double.MaxValue / 2;\n                parent[m, i] = -1;\n            }\n        \n        // Initialize: from start to each station\n        for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) {\n            dp[1<<i, i] = costMatrix[0, i+1]; // cost from depot to station i\n        }\n        \n        // Fill DP\n        for (int mask = 1; mask < full; mask++) {\n            for (int last = 0; last < N; last++) {\n                if ((mask & (1<<last)) == 0) continue;\n                if (dp[mask, last] >= double.MaxValue/2) continue;\n                \n                int prevMask = mask ^ (1<<last);\n                // Try going to each unvisited station\n                for (int next = 0; next < N; next++) {\n                    if ((mask & (1<<next)) != 0) continue;\n                    int newMask = mask | (1<<next);\n                    double newCost = dp[mask, last] + costMatrix[last+1, next+1];\n                    if (newCost < dp[newMask, next]) {\n                        dp[newMask, next] = newCost;\n                        parent[newMask, next] = last;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        \n        // Find best ending station\n        int fullMask = full - 1;\n        int bestLast = 0;\n        double bestCost = dp[fullMask, 0];\n // Reconstruct path\n        int[] path = new int[N];\n        int cur = bestLast;\n        int curMask = fullMask;\n        for (int step = N-1; step >= 0; step--) {\n            path[step] = cur;\n            int prev = parent[curMask, cur];\n            curMask ^= (1<<cur);\n            cur = prev;\n        }\n        \n        return path;\n    }\n    \n    static int[] LargeScaleSolve() {\n The standard Held-Karp processes masks in order, but I need to make sure I process them correctly.\n\nActually the issue is that when I initialize dp for single-station masks, I need to then process 2-station masks, etc. Processing in order of mask value (0 to full-1) does work because smaller masks have smaller values.\n\nLet me also think about memory: for N=20, dp is 2^20 * 20 = ~20M doubles = 160MB. // cost[i,j] where 0=start, 1..N=stations\n    \n    static void Main() {\n        // Parse\n        var line1 = Console.ReadLine().Trim().Split();\n        N = int.Parse(line1[0]);\n        MU = double.Parse(line1[1]);\n        \n        var startRV = ParseVec(Console.ReadLine());\n        var stationRVs = new double[N][];\n        for (int i = 0; i < N; i++)\n            stationRVs[i] = ParseVec(Console.ReadLine());\n        \n        // Build cost matrix (N+1 x N+1, index 0 = start)\n        int sz = N + 1;\n        cost = new double[sz, sz];\n        var allRVs = new double[sz][];\n        allRVs[0] = startRV;\n        for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) allRVs[i+1] = stationRVs[i];\n        \n        for (int i = 0; i < sz; i++)\n            for (int j = 0; j < sz; j++)\n                cost[i,j] = (i==j) ? 0 : DeltaV(allRVs[i], allRVs[j]);\n        \n        int[] result;\n        if (N == 1) result = new[]{0};\n        else if (N <= 20) result = HeldKarp();\n        else result = LargeScale();\n        \n        Console.WriteLine(string.Join(" ", result));\n    }\n    \n    static double[] ParseVec(string s) {\n        return s.Trim().Split(new[]{\' \',\'\t\'}, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries)\n                .Select(x => double.Parse(x, System.Globalization.CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)).ToArray();\n    }\n    \n    static double DeltaV(double[] r1v1, double[] r2v2) {\n        // Estimate transfer delta-V between two orbital states\n        double a1 = SMA(r1v1), a2 = SMA(r2v2);\n        double i1 = Inc(r1v1), i2 = Inc(r2v2);\n        \n        if (a1 <= 0 || a2 <= 0 || double.IsNaN(a1) || double.IsNaN(a2)) {\n            // Fallback\n            double dvx = r2v2[3]-r1v1[3], dvy = r2v2[4]-r1v1[4], dvz = r2v2[5]-r1v1[5];\n            return Math.Sqrt(dvx*dvx+dvy*dvy+dvz*dvz);\n        }\n        \n        double vc1 = Math.Sqrt(MU/a1);\n        double vc2 = Math.Sqrt(MU/a2);\n        double aT = (a1+a2)/2;\n        \n        double dv1 = Math.Abs(Math.Sqrt(MU*(2/a1-1/aT)) - vc1);\n        double dv2 = Math.Abs(vc2 - Math.Sqrt(MU*(2/a2-1/aT)));\n        \n        double dvH = dv1 + dv2;\n        \n        double di = Math.Abs(i2 - i1);\n        double vMid = Math.Sqrt(MU*(2/aT - 1/aT)); // this is wrong...\n        // velocity at apoapsis of transfer (larger semi-major axis = apoapsis)\n        // For a1 < a2: transfer goes from periapsis a1 to apoapsis a2\n        // v at apoapsis = sqrt(mu*(2/a2 - 1/aT))\n        double aMax = Math.Max(a1,a2);\n        double aMin = Math.Min(a1,a2);\n        aT = (aMax+aMin)/2;\n        double vApo = Math.Sqrt(MU*(2/aMax - 1/aT));\n        double dvPlane = 2 * vApo * Math.Sin(di/2);\n        \n        return dvH + dvPlane;\n    }\n    \n    // semi-major axis\n    static double SMA(double[] rv) {\n        double r = Math.Sqrt(rv[0]*rv[0]+rv[1]*rv[1]+rv[2]*rv[2]);\n        double v2 = rv[3]*rv[3]+rv[4]*rv[4]+rv[5]*rv[5];\n        double E = v2/2 - MU/r;\n        return -MU/(2*E);\n    }\n    \n    // inclination\n    static double Inc(double[] rv) {\n        double hx = rv[1]*rv[5]-rv[2]*rv[4];\n        double hy = rv[2]*rv[3]-rv[0]*rv[5];\n        double hz = rv[0]*rv[4]-rv[1]*rv[3];\n        double h = Math.Sqrt(hx*hx+hy*hy+hz*hz);\n        return Math.Acos(Math.Max(-1,Math.Min(1,hz/h)));\n    }\n    \n    static int[] HeldKarp() {\n        int full = 1<<N;\n        var dp = new double[full, N];\n        var par = new short[full, N];\n        \n        for (int m=0; m<full; m++)\n            for (int i=0; i<N; i++) {\n                dp[m,i] = double.MaxValue/2;\n                par[m,i] = -1;\n            }\n        \n        for (int i=0; i<N; i++)\n            dp[1<<i, i] = cost[0, i+1];\n        \n        for (int mask=1; mask<full; mask++) {\n            for (int last=0; last<N; last++) {\n                if ((mask&(1<<last))==0) continue;\n                double d = dp[mask,last];\n                if (d >= double.MaxValue/2) continue;\n                for (int next=0; next<N; next++) {\n                    if ((mask&(1<<next))!=0) continue;\n                    int nm = mask|(1<<next);\n                    double nd = d + cost[last+1, next+1];\n                    if (nd < dp[nm,next]) {\n                        dp[nm,next] = nd;\n                        par[nm,next] = (short)last;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        \n        int fMask = full-1;\n        int best = 0;\n        for (int i=1; i<N; i++)\n            if (dp[fMask,i] < dp[fMask,best]) best = i;\n        \n        var path = new int[N];\n        int cur = best, msk = fMask;\n        for (int s=N-1; s>=0; s--) {\n            path[s] = cur;\n            int p = par[msk, cur];\n            msk ^= (1<<cur);\n            cur = p;\n        }\n        return path;\n    }\n    \n    // Compute tour cost (0-indexed stations, start = node 0 in cost matrix)\n    static double TourCost(int[] tour) {\n        double c = cost[0, tour[0]+1];\n        for (int i=1; i<tour.Length; i++)\n            c += cost[tour[i-1]+1, tour[i]+1];\n        return c;\n    }\n    \n    static int[] GreedyStart(int first) {\n        var visited = new bool[N];\n        var tour = new int[N];\n        tour[0] = first;\n        visited[first] = true;\n        int cur = first;\n        for (int s=1; s<N; s++) {\n            double best = double.MaxValue;\n            int bj = -1;\n            for (int j=0; j<N; j++) {\n                if (!visited[j] && cost[cur+1,j+1] < best) {\n                    best = cost[cur+1,j+1];\n                    bj = j;\n                }\n            }\n            tour[s] = bj;\n            visited[bj] = true;\n            cur = bj;\n        }\n        return tour;\n    }\n    \n    static int[] GreedyStartFromDepot() {\n        var visited = new bool[N];\n        var tour = new int[N];\n        // Start from depot (node 0)\n        int prev = -1; // -1 means depot\n        for (int s=0; s<N; s++) {\n            double best = double.MaxValue;\n            int bj = -1;\n            for (int j=0; j<N; j++) {\n                if (!visited[j]) {\n                    double c = (prev==-1) ? cost[0,j+1] : cost[prev+1,j+1];\n                    if (c < best) {\n                        best = c;\n                        bj = j;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n            tour[s] = bj;\n            visited[bj] = true;\n            prev = bj;\n        }\n        return tour;\n    }\n    \n    static void TwoOpt(int[] tour) {\n        bool improved = true;\n        while (improved) {\n            improved = false;\n            for (int i=0; i<N-1; i++) {\n                for (int j=i+2; j<N; j++) {\n                    // Current edges: (i-1 -> i, j -> j+1) or (depot -> 0, ..., i-1 -> i, ..., j -> j+1)\n                    // Reversed segment [i..j]\n                    // Cost before: cost(prev_i, i) + cost(j, next_j)\n                    // Cost after: cost(prev_i, j) + cost(i, next_j)\n                    int prevI = (i==0) ? -1 : tour[i-1]; // -1 = depot\n                    int nextJ = (j==N-1) ? -2 : tour[j+1]; // -2 = none (open TSP, no return)\n                    \n                    double before, after;\n                    int a = prevI, b = tour[i], c = tour[j];\n                    int d = (j<N-1) ? tour[j+1] : -2;\n                    \n                    double costAB = (a==-1) ? cost[0,b+1] : cost[a+1,b+1];\n                    double costCD = (d==-2) ? 0 : cost[c+1,d+1];\n                    double costAC = (a==-1) ? cost[0,c+1] : cost[a+1,c+1];\n                    double costBD = (d==-2) ? 0 : cost[b+1,d+1];\n                    \n                    before = costAB + costCD;\n                    after = costAC + costBD;\n                    \n                    if (after < before - 1e-10) {\n                        // Reverse segment [i..j]\n                        Array.Reverse(tour, i, j-i+1);\n                        improved = true;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Or-opt: move single node to a better position\n    static bool OrOpt1(int[] tour) {\n        bool improved = false;\n        for (int i=0; i<N; i++) {\n            int node = tour[i];\n            // Remove node from position i\n            // Cost of removing: fix the gap\n            int prev = (i>0) ? tour[i-1] : -1;\n            int next = (i<N-1) ? tour[i+1] : -1;\n            \n            double removedCost = 0;\n            if (prev==-1) removedCost += cost[0,node+1];\n            else removedCost += cost[prev+1,node+1];\n            if (next!=-1) removedCost += cost[node+1,next+1];\n            // After removal, the connection changes\n            double newConnection = 0;\n            if (prev==-1 && next!=-1) newConnection = cost[0,next+1];\n            else if (prev!=-1 && next!=-1) newConnection = cost[prev+1,next+1];\n            \n            double removalGain = removedCost - newConnection;\n            \n            // Try inserting at each position\n            for (int j=0; j<N; j++) {\n                if (j==i || j==i-1) continue;\n                // Insert between j and j+1 (or at position 0, before tour[0])\n                int insAfter = (j < i) ? j : j; // this is tricky with removal\n                // ... complex, let me simplify\n            }\n        }\n        return improved;\n    }\n    \n    static int[] LargeScale() {\n        // Try multiple greedy starts, apply 2-opt\n        var bestTour = GreedyStartFromDepot();\n        TwoOpt(bestTour);\n        double bestCost = TourCost(bestTour);\n        \n        var lockObj = new object();\n        \n        Parallel.For(0, N, i => {\n            var tour = GreedyStart(i);\n            TwoOpt(tour);\n            double c = TourCost(tour);\n            lock(lockObj) {\n                if (c < bestCost) {\n                    bestCost = c;\n                    Array.Copy(tour, bestTour, N);\n                }\n            }\n        });\n        \n        // Additional SA/3-opt...\n        SimulatedAnnealing(bestTour, ref bestCost);\n        \n        return bestTour;\n    }\n    \n    static Random rng = new Random(42);\n    \n    static void SimulatedAnnealing(int[] tour, ref double bestCost) {\n        var current = (int[])tour.Clone();\n        double currentCost = bestCost;\n        double T = currentCost * 0.1; // Initial temperature\n        double Tmin = currentCost * 0.0001;\n        double alpha = 0.9995;\n        \n        var sw = System.Diagnostics.Stopwatch.StartNew();\n        long maxMs = 200000; // 200 seconds\n        \n        while (T > Tmin && sw.ElapsedMilliseconds < maxMs) {\n            // Random swap\n            int i = rng.Next(N);\n            int j = rng.Next(N);\n            if (i == j) continue;\n            \n            // Swap tour[i] and tour[j]\n            // Compute delta cost\n            double delta = SwapDelta(current, i, j);\n            \n            if (delta < 0 || rng.NextDouble() < Math.Exp(-delta/T)) {\n                int tmp = current[i]; current[i] = current[j]; current[j] = tmp;\n                currentCost += delta;\n                if (currentCost < bestCost) {\n                    bestCost = currentCost;\n                    Array.Copy(current, tour, N);\n                }\n            }\n            \n            T *= alpha;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Compute delta cost of swapping positions i and j in tour\n    static double SwapDelta(int[] tour, int i, int j) {\n        if (i > j) { int t=i; i=j; j=t; }\n        if (i == j) return 0;\n        \n        // Nodes at positions i and j\n        int ni = tour[i], nj = tour[j];\n        int prevI = (i>0) ? tour[i-1] : -1;\n        int nextI = (i<N-1) ? tour[i+1] : -1;\n        int prevJ = (j>0) ? tour[j-1] : -1;\n        int nextJ = (j<N-1) ? tour[j+1] : -1;\n        \n        // If adjacent\n        if (j == i+1) {\n            // Before: ... prevI -> ni -> nj -> nextJ\n            // After:  ... prevI -> nj -> ni -> nextJ\n            double before = CostEdge(prevI, ni) + CostEdge(ni, nj) + CostEdge(nj, nextJ);\n            double after = CostEdge(prevI, nj) + CostEdge(nj, ni) + CostEdge(ni, nextJ);\n            return after - before;\n        }\n        \n        // Non-adjacent\n        double b = CostEdge(prevI, ni) + CostEdge(ni, nextI) +\n                   CostEdge(prevJ, nj) + CostEdge(nj, nextJ);\n        double a = CostEdge(prevI, nj) + CostEdge(nj, nextI) +\n                   CostEdge(prevJ, ni) + CostEdge(ni, nextJ);\n        return a - b;\n    }\n    \n    // Edge cost: -1 = depot (node 0 in cost matrix), -2 = nothing (no edge)\n    static double CostEdge(int a, int b) {\n        if (b == -1 || b == -2) return 0; // no outgoing edge from last node\n        if (a == -1) return cost[0, b+1]; // from depot\n        if (a == -2) return 0; // shouldn\'t happen\n        return cost[a+1, b+1];\n    }\n}\n```\n\nWait, there are several issues:\n1. // cost matrix, C[i,j]: 0=depot, 1..N=stations\n    static Random rng = new Random(42);\n    \n    static void Main() {\n        // Parse input\n        var line1 = Console.ReadLine().Trim().Split(new[]{\' \',\'\t\'}, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);\n        N = int.Parse(line1[0]);\n        MU = double.Parse(line1[1], CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);\n        \n        var allRV = new double[N+1][];\n        allRV[0] = ParseVec(Console.ReadLine());\n        for (int i = 1; i <= N; i++)\n            allRV[i] = ParseVec(Console.ReadLine());\n        \n        // Build cost matrix\n        C = new double[N+1, N+1];\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N; i++)\n            for (int j = 0; j <= N; j++)\n                C[i,j] = (i==j) ? 0.0 : DV(allRV[i], allRV[j]);\n        \n        int[] result;\n        if (N == 1) {\n            result = new[]{0};\n        } else if (N <= 20) {\n            result = HeldKarp();\n        } else {\n            result = LargeScale();\n        }\n        \n        Console.WriteLine(string.Join(" ", result));\n    }\n    \n    static double[] ParseVec(string s) {\n        return s.Trim().Split(new[]{\' \',\'\t\'}, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries)\n                .Select(x => double.Parse(x, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)).ToArray();\n    }\n    \n    static double SMA(double[] rv) {\n        double r = Math.Sqrt(rv[0]*rv[0]+rv[1]*rv[1]+rv[2]*rv[2]);\n        double v2 = rv[3]*rv[3]+rv[4]*rv[4]+rv[5]*rv[5];\n        double E = v2*0.5 - MU/r;\n        if (E >= 0) return double.PositiveInfinity; // hyperbolic\n        return -MU/(2*E);\n    }\n    \n    static double Inc(double[] rv) {\n        double hx = rv[1]*rv[5]-rv[2]*rv[4];\n        double hy = rv[2]*rv[3]-rv[0]*rv[5];\n        double hz = rv[0]*rv[4]-rv[1]*rv[3];\n        double h = Math.Sqrt(hx*hx+hy*hy+hz*hz);\n        if (h < 1e-10) return 0;\n        return Math.Acos(Math.Max(-1.0, Math.Min(1.0, hz/h)));\n    }\n    \n    static double DV(double[] rv1, double[] rv2) {\n        double a1 = SMA(rv1), a2 = SMA(rv2);\n        \n        // Fallback if orbits are hyperbolic or degenerate\n        if (double.IsInfinity(a1) || double.IsInfinity(a2) || a1 <= 0 || a2 <= 0) {\n            double dvx = rv2[3]-rv1[3], dvy = rv2[4]-rv1[4], dvz = rv2[5]-rv1[5];\n            return Math.Sqrt(dvx*dvx+dvy*dvy+dvz*dvz);\n        }\n        \n        // For elliptical orbits, compute Hohmann transfer + plane change\n        double i1 = Inc(rv1), i2 = Inc(rv2);\n        double di = Math.Abs(i2-i1);\n        \n        // Ensure a1 <= a2 for Hohmann formulas\n        double lo = Math.Min(a1,a2), hi = Math.Max(a1,a2);\n        double aT = (lo+hi)/2;\n        \n        // Circular velocities at each orbit\n        double vc_lo = Math.Sqrt(MU/lo);\n        double vc_hi = Math.Sqrt(MU/hi);\n        \n        // Velocities at periapsis and apoapsis of transfer ellipse\n        double vT_peri = Math.Sqrt(MU*(2/lo - 1/aT)); // velocity at lo (periapsis)\n        double vT_apo = Math.Sqrt(MU*(2/hi - 1/aT));  // velocity at hi (apoapsis)\n        \n        double dv1 = Math.Abs(vT_peri - vc_lo); // burn at periapsis\n        double dv2 = Math.Abs(vc_hi - vT_apo);  // burn at apoapsis\n        \n        // Plane change cost: optimal to combine with lower-velocity burn\n        // Do plane change at apoapsis (lower velocity) combined with circularization\n        // Combined delta-V at apoapsis:\n        // dv_combined = sqrt(vc_hi^2 + vT_apo^2 - 2*vc_hi*vT_apo*cos(di)) - but this is for full plane change\n        // Simplified: plane change at apoapsis\n        double dv2_combined = Math.Sqrt(vc_hi*vc_hi + vT_apo*vT_apo - 2*vc_hi*vT_apo*Math.Cos(di));\n        \n        return dv1 + dv2_combined;\n    }\n    \n    static double TourCost(int[] tour) {\n        if (tour.Length == 0) return 0;\n        double c = C[0, tour[0]+1];\n        for (int i = 1; i < tour.Length; i++)\n            c += C[tour[i-1]+1, tour[i]+1];\n        return c;\n    }\n    \n    // Edge cost where a=-1 means depot, b=-1 means "end" (no cost)\n    static double Edge(int a, int b) {\n        if (b == -1) return 0; // no edge\n        int ai = (a==-1) ? 0 : a+1;\n        return C[ai, b+1];\n    }\n    \n    #region Held-Karp\n    static int[] HeldKarp() {\n        int full = 1<<N;\n        var dp = new float[full * N]; // use float to save memory for N=20\n        var par = new short[full * N];\n        \n        // Initialize\n        for (int i = 0; i < dp.Length; i++) dp[i] = float.MaxValue/2;\n        for (int i = 0; i < par.Length; i++) par[i] = -1;\n        \n        for (int i = 0; i < N; i++)\n            dp[(1<<i)*N + i] = (float)C[0, i+1];\n        \n        for (int mask = 1; mask < full; mask++) {\n            int mN = mask*N;\n            for (int last = 0; last < N; last++) {\n                if ((mask & (1<<last)) == 0) continue;\n                float d = dp[mN + last];\n                if (d >= float.MaxValue/2) continue;\n                for (int next = 0; next < N; next++) {\n                    if ((mask & (1<<next)) != 0) continue;\n                    int nm = mask|(1<<next);\n                    float nd = d + (float)C[last+1, next+1];\n                    int idx = nm*N + next;\n                    if (nd < dp[idx]) {\n                        dp[idx] = nd;\n                        par[idx] = (short)last;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        \n        int fMask = full-1;\n        int fBase = fMask*N;\n        int best = 0;\n        for (int i = 1; i < N; i++)\n            if (dp[fBase+i] < dp[fBase+best]) best = i;\n        \n        var path = new int[N];\n        int cur = best, msk = fMask;\n        for (int s = N-1; s >= 0; s--) {\n            path[s] = cur;\n            int p = par[msk*N + cur];\n            msk ^= (1<<cur);\n            cur = p;\n        }\n        return path;\n    }\n    #endregion\n    \n    #region Greedy\n    static int[] GreedyNN(int startNode) {\n        // startNode: -1 = from depot, 0..N-1 = from that station\n        var visited = new bool[N];\n        var tour = new int[N];\n        int prev = startNode;\n        \n        if (startNode >= 0) {\n            tour[0] = startNode;\n            visited[startNode] = true;\n            prev = startNode;\n            for (int s = 1; s < N; s++) {\n                double best = double.MaxValue;\n                int bj = -1;\n                for (int j = 0; j < N; j++) {\n                    if (!visited[j] && C[prev+1,j+1] < best) {\n                        best = C[prev+1,j+1];\n                        bj = j;\n                    }\n                }\n                tour[s] = bj;\n                visited[bj] = true;\n                prev = bj;\n            }\n        } else {\n            // Start from depot\n            for (int s = 0; s < N; s++) {\n                double best = double.MaxValue;\n                int bj = -1;\n                int fromNode = (s==0) ? -1 : prev;\n                for (int j = 0; j < N; j++) {\n                    if (!visited[j]) {\n                        double c = Edge(fromNode, j);\n                        if (c < best) { best = c; bj = j; }\n                    }\n                }\n                tour[s] = bj;\n                visited[bj] = true;\n                prev = bj;\n            }\n        }\n        return tour;\n    }\n    #endregion\n    \n    #region 2-opt\n    static bool TwoOpt(int[] tour) {\n        bool anyImproved = false;\n        bool improved = true;\n        while (improved) {\n            improved = false;\n            for (int i = 0; i < N-1; i++) {\n                for (int j = i+2; j < N; j++) {\n                    int a = (i>0) ? tour[i-1] : -1;\n                    int b = tour[i];\n                    int c = tour[j];\n                    int d = (j<N-1) ? tour[j+1] : -1;\n                    \n                    double before = Edge(a,b) + Edge(c,d);\n                    double after = Edge(a,c) + Edge(b,d);\n                    \n                    if (after < before - 1e-9) {\n                        Array.Reverse(tour, i, j-i+1);\n                        improved = true;\n                        anyImproved = true;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        return anyImproved;\n    }\n    #endregion\n    \n    #region Or-opt\n    // Move a single station from position i to between positions j and j+1\n    static bool OrOpt1(int[] tour) {\n        bool anyImproved = false;\n        bool improved = true;\n        while (improved) {\n            improved = false;\n            for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) {\n                int node = tour[i];\n                int prev = (i>0) ? tour[i-1] : -1;\n                int next = (i<N-1) ? tour[i+1] : -1;\n                \n                // Cost of current position of node\n                double costRemove = Edge(prev, node) + Edge(node, next);\n                // New link after removal\n                double costBridge = Edge(prev, next);\n                double gain = costRemove - costBridge;\n                \n                // Try inserting at each position\n                double bestGain = 1e-9;\n                int bestPos = -1;\n                \n                for (int j = 0; j < N; j++) {\n                    if (j == i || j == i-1) continue; // inserting in same spot\n                    \n                    int jNode = tour[j];\n                    int jNext = (j<N-1) ? tour[j+1] : -1;\n                    if (jNext == node) continue; // same as current\n                    \n                    // Insert node between j and j+1\n                    double insertCost = Edge(jNode, node) + Edge(node, jNext) - Edge(jNode, jNext);\n                    double totalGain = gain - insertCost;\n                    \n                    if (totalGain > bestGain) {\n                        bestGain = totalGain;\n                        bestPos = j;\n                    }\n                }\n                \n                // Also try inserting at position 0 (before first element)\n                if (i != 0 && tour[0] != node) {\n                    int firstNode = tour[0];\n                    double insertCost = Edge(-1, node) + Edge(node, firstNode) - Edge(-1, firstNode);\n                    double totalGain = gain - insertCost;\n                    if (totalGain > bestGain) {\n                        bestGain = totalGain;\n                        bestPos = -1; // special: insert at beginning\n                    }\n                }\n                \n                if (bestPos != -2) {\n                    // Actually if bestPos is valid, apply the move\n                    if (bestGain > 1e-9 && (bestPos >= 0 || bestPos == -1)) {\n                        // Remove node from position i\n                        // Insert at position bestPos (after bestPos, or at start if -1)\n                        \n                        // Build new tour\n                        var newTour = new List<int>(N);\n                        \n                        if (bestPos == -1) {\n                            // Insert at beginning\n                            newTour.Add(node);\n                            for (int k = 0; k < N; k++)\n                                if (k != i) newTour.Add(tour[k]);\n                        } else {\n                            for (int k = 0; k < N; k++) {\n                                if (k == i) continue;\n                                newTour.Add(tour[k]);\n                                int kAdj = k;\n                                if (k > i) kAdj = k; // already adjusted because we skipped i\n                                // Wait, this is getting complicated because bestPos refers to original indices\n                                // Let me use a different approach\n                            }\n                        }\n                        // This is getting complicated, let me simplify\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        return anyImproved;\n    }\n    #endregion\n```\n\nThe Or-opt is getting complicated. Let me simplify it by working on a list and converting back to array.\n\nActually, let me just do a simpler implementation:\n\n```csharp\nstatic bool OrOpt1(int[] tour) {\n    bool improved = false;\n    for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) {\n        for (int j = 0; j < N; j++) {\n            if (i == j) continue;\n            // Try to move tour[i] to just after position j (after removal of i)\n            double delta = RelocateDelta(tour, i, j);\n            if (delta < -1e-9) {\n                ApplyRelocate(tour, i, j);\n                // After relocation, indices change...\n                improved = true;\n                i = -1; // restart\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n        if (i == -1) { i = 0; continue; } // restart outer loop\n    }\n    return improved;\n}\n```\n\nHmm, this restart approach is inefficient. I\'ll keep it reasonably concise but complete.\n\nFor the SA, I\'ll implement:\n- Swap two random elements\n- Reverse a random segment (2-opt move)\n- Relocate a random element (or-opt move)\n\nThese are efficient to compute and provide diverse search.\n\nFor the temperature schedule:\n- Initial T: based on average cost of random moves\n- Final T: very small (0.01% of initial)\n- Cooling rate: depends on N (more steps for larger N)\n\nLet me finalize the code now.\n\n```csharp\nusing System;\nusing System.Collections.Generic;\nusing System.Linq;\nusing System.Threading;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\nusing System.Diagnostics;\nusing System.Globalization;\n\nclass Program {\n    static double MU;\n    static int N;\n    static double[,] C; // C[i,j]: 0=depot, 1..N=stations\n    \n    static void Main() {\n        // Parse input\n        var firstLine = Console.ReadLine().Trim()\n            .Split(new[]{\' \',\'\t\'}, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);\n        N = int.Parse(firstLine[0]);\n        MU = double.Parse(firstLine[1], CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);\n        \n        var allRV = new double[N+1][];\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N; i++)\n            allRV[i] = ParseVec(Console.ReadLine());\n        \n        // Build cost matrix\n        C = new double[N+1, N+1];\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N; i++)\n            for (int j = 0; j <= N; j++)\n                if (i != j) C[i,j] = DV(allRV[i], allRV[j]);\n        \n        int[] result;\n        if (N == 1) {\n            result = new[]{0};\n        } else if (N <= 20) {\n            result = HeldKarp();\n        } else {\n            result = LargeScale();\n        }\n        \n        Console.WriteLine(string.Join(" ", result));\n    }\n    \n    // ... Let me write the complete, final code now.\n\nOne important thing: I need to make sure the Held-Karp implementation is correct for the open TSP (no return to depot).\n\nThe standard Held-Karp for TSP assumes we start at a fixed depot and visit all cities, returning to depot. For the open TSP (no return):\n- dp[S][v] = minimum cost to visit all cities in S, starting from depot, ending at city v\n- Initialize: dp[{i}][i] = cost(depot, i)\n- Recurrence: dp[S∪{u}][u] = min_{v∈S} (dp[S][v] + cost(v, u))\n- Answer: min_{v} dp[full][v]\n\nThis is exactly what I had. Good.\n\nNow for the reconstruction:\n- Start from the optimal final city v* = argmin dp[full][v]\n- par[full][v*] = the city visited before v* (let\'s call it p)\n- Then par[full ^ (1<<v*)][p] = city before p\n- Continue until mask has only one city set\n- The remaining city is the first visited from depot\n\nThis looks correct. Let me double-check by tracing through a small example:\n\nN=3, cities 0,1,2\n- Suppose best tour is depot -> 1 -> 0 -> 2\n- dp[{1}][1] = C[0,2] (cost from depot to city 1)\n  Wait, C[0, i+1] where i is station index (0-based)\n  So C[0, 2] = cost from depot to city 1 (station index 1, cost matrix index 2)\n  \nActually let me reclarify: in my code, stations are 0-indexed (0 to N-1), but in the cost matrix, index 0 is the depot and indices 1 to N are the stations. So:\n- C[0, i+1] = cost from depot to station i\n- C[i+1, j+1] = cost from station i to station j\n\nFor Held-Karp:\n- dp[mask, i] where i ∈ {0..N-1} (0-indexed stations)\n- dp[mask with bit i set, i] = min cost to start from depot and visit all stations in mask, ending at station i\n- Initialize: dp[1<<i, i] = C[0, i+1] for all i\n- Recurrence: for each mask, for each last i in mask, for each next j not in mask:\n  dp[mask|(1<<j), j] = min(dp[mask|(1<<j), j], dp[mask, i] + C[i+1, j+1])\n- Answer: min_i dp[full, i]\n\nThis is correct. The path reconstruction:\n- Start at bestLast with fullMask\n- par[fullMask, bestLast] = station visited before bestLast in the optimal tour\n- Unmask bestLast from fullMask, move to par[...][bestLast]\n- Continue...\n\nLooks good.\n\nOne more concern: for large N (e.g., 20), the dp and par arrays might be large. Let me check:\n- N=20: full=2^20=1048576, dp = 1048576*20 = ~20M entries * 4 bytes (float) = 80 MB, par = 20M * 2 bytes = 40 MB\n- Total ~120 MB, fine.\n- N=22: full=4M, dp = 4M*22*4=352 MB, par = 4M*22*2=176 MB. Total ~4.8 GB. Feasible!\n- N=26: similar to N=25 but doubled. ~9.6 GB. Way too slow.\n  \nSo N=20 is about the max for Held-Karp with the 5-minute time limit:\n- N=20: 2^20 * 20 * 20 = 419 million ops ≈ a few seconds. Fine.\n- N=22: 2^22 * 22 * 22 ≈ 2 billion. Let me write the final code now.\n\nActually, for a cleaner implementation, let me use the following structure for LargeScale:\n\n1. Run N+1 greedy tours (from depot + from each station) in parallel\n2. Apply 2-opt to each (in parallel)\n3. Apply Or-opt1 to each (in parallel)\n4. Keep the best\n5. Apply SA to the best\n6. Return result\n\nFor Or-opt, the cleanest implementation:\n\n```csharp\nstatic bool OrOpt1Pass(int[] t) {\n    // Try to relocate each single node to a better position\n    bool improved = false;\n    for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) {\n        int node = t[i];\n        int prev = (i>0) ? t[i-1] : -1; // -1 = depot\n        int next = (i<N-1) ? t[i+1] : -1; // -1 = nothing\n        \n        // Gain from removing node from current position\n        double currentCost = Edge(prev, node) + Edge(node, next);\n        double afterBridge = Edge(prev, next);\n        double removalGain = currentCost - afterBridge;\n        \n        // Find best position to insert\n        int bestJ = -2; // -2 = no improvement\n        double bestGain = 1e-9;\n        \n        for (int j = -1; j < N; j++) { // j = -1: insert before t[0]\n            // Insert node between position j and j+1\n            // When j=i or j=i-1, it\'s the same as current (skip)\n            if (j == i-1 || j == i) continue;\n            \n            int jNode = (j == -1) ? -1 : t[j]; // -1 = depot\n            int jNext = (j+1 < N) ? t[j+1] : -1;\n            \n            // But if j >= i, the actual indices shift by -1 after removal\n            // For simplicity, let\'s compute cost in original array context\n            // and just check if it\'s the same position\n            \n            // Cost of insertion: edge(j, node) + edge(node, j+1) - edge(j, j+1)\n            double insertCost = Edge(jNode, node) + Edge(node, jNext) - Edge(jNode, jNext);\n            \n            double totalGain = removalGain - insertCost;\n            if (totalGain > bestGain) {\n                bestGain = totalGain;\n                bestJ = j;\n            }\n        }\n        \n        if (bestJ > -2) {\n            // Apply the move: remove from i, insert after j\n            // We need to be careful about index shifts\n            int insertAfter = bestJ;\n            if (bestJ > i) insertAfter = bestJ; // position in original; after removal, it shifts\n            \n            // Remove node at position i\n            // If bestJ > i, insert at position bestJ (shift by -1 after removal = bestJ-1)\n            // But in the new array, the position after bestJ is bestJ (since i was removed)\n            // Wait, if we insert "after position j" in the original array:\n            // If j < i: remove t[i], then insert after t[j] -> position j+1 in new array\n            // If j > i: remove t[i], then insert after t[j] -> position j in new array (shifted left)\n            \n            // Let\'s just build the new array:\n            var newT = new List<int>(N);\n            if (bestJ < i) {\n                // Insert before position i\n                for (int k = 0; k < N; k++) {\n                    if (k == bestJ+1) newT.Add(node); // insert after j\n                    if (k != i) newT.Add(t[k]);\n                }\n            } else { // bestJ > i\n                for (int k = 0; k < N; k++) {\n                    if (k == i) continue; // skip\n                    newT.Add(t[k]);\n                    if (k == bestJ) newT.Add(node); // insert after j\n                }\n            }\n            \n            for (int k = 0; However, if I\'m computing gain_remove using original positions, and the gain_insert is using original positions too, the combined gain might not be exactly correct when j > i.\n\nLet me think more carefully:\n\nOriginal tour: ... prev -> node -> next ... But let me simplify by just building a new list and copying back, to avoid the complex index management:\n\n```csharp\nstatic bool OrOpt1(int[] t) {\n    bool anyImproved = false;\n    bool improved = true;\n    while (improved) {\n        improved = false;\n        for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) {\n            int node = t[i];\n            int prev = (i > 0) ? t[i-1] : -1;\n            int next = (i < N-1) ? t[i+1] : -1;\n            \n            double gainRemove = Edge(prev, node) + Edge(node, next) - Edge(prev, next);\n            \n            int bestJ = int.MinValue;\n            double bestGain = 1e-9;\n            \n            // Try all insertion positions\n            // Positions: -1 (before t[0]), 0 (after t[0]), ..., N-2 (after t[N-2]), N-1 (after t[N-1])\n            for (int j = -1; j < N; j++) {\n                // Insert after position j (j=-1 means before first element)\n                // Position j in original array\n                // Skip if inserting back at same place\n                if (j == i-1 || j == i) continue; // same as current position\n                \n                int A = (j == -1) ? -1 : t[j];\n                int B = (j+1 < N) ? t[j+1] : -1;\n                \n                // But if j >= i, then in the original array t[j+1] might be the node itself\n                // (j+1 == i), but we already skip j == i-1\n                // If j < i: A=t[j], B=t[j+1] (both different from node)\n                // If j == i: same position, skip\n                // If j > i: A=t[j], B=t[j+1] (both different from node since j > i and j+1 > i)\n                // If j == N-1: B = -1 (end of tour)\n                \n                double gainInsert = Edge(A, B) - Edge(A, node) - Edge(node, B);\n                double totalGain = gainRemove + gainInsert;\n                \n                if (totalGain > bestGain) {\n                    bestGain = totalGain;\n                    bestJ = j;\n                }\n            }\n            \n            if (bestJ > int.MinValue) {\n                // Build new tour\n                var newT = new List<int>(N);\n                bool inserted = false;\n                \n                if (bestJ == -1) {\n                    newT.Add(node);\n                    for (int k = 0; k < N; k++)\n                        if (k != i) newT.Add(t[k]);\n                } else {\n                    // Go through original array, skip position i, insert after bestJ\n                    for (int k = 0; k < N; k++) {\n                        if (k == i) continue;\n                        newT.Add(t[k]);\n                        // Insert after bestJ in original array\n                        // In the new list, we insert after the element that was at t[bestJ]\n                        // So after adding t[k] where t[k] == t[bestJ], insert node\n                        if (k == bestJ && !inserted) {\n                            newT.Add(node);\n                            inserted = true;\n                        }\n                    }\n                    if (!inserted) newT.Add(node); // shouldn\'t happen\n                }\n                \n                for (int k = 0; k < N; k++) t[k] = newT[k];\n                improved = true;\n                anyImproved = true;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    return anyImproved;\n}\n```\n\nWait, there\'s still an issue: if bestJ > i, then when I iterate k through the original array and skip i, k==bestJ is fine. But if bestJ < i, then I insert after t[bestJ] in the original array, which happens before I reach k==i (which I skip). That\'s still correct.\n\nLet me trace: original [A, B, C, D, E] (indices 0-4), i=3 (D), bestJ=1 (B):\n- k=0: add A (k!=3, k!=1)\n- k=1: add B, then add D (inserted)\n- k=2: add C\n- k=3: skip (i)\n- k=4: add E\n- Result: [A, B, D, C, E] ✓\n\nAnother trace: i=1 (B), bestJ=3 (D):\n- k=0: add A\n- k=1: skip (i)\n- k=2: add C\n- k=3: add D, then add B (inserted)\n- k=4: add E\n- Result: [A, C, D, B, E] ✓\n\nGood, this approach works correctly!\n\nBut there\'s a performance issue: creating a List<int> every time is slow for large N. Let me use the ApplyRelocate approach for performance.\n\nActually, for simplicity and correctness, let me just use the list approach but avoid the inner loop. Instead:\n\n```csharp\nstatic void ApplyRelocate(int[] t, int i, int j) {\n    // Remove t[i] and insert after position j (in original indexing)\n    // j can be -1 (insert at start) or 0..N-1 (insert after t[j])\n    int node = t[i];\n    if (j == -1) {\n        // Insert at start\n        for (int k = i; k > 0; k--) t[k] = t[k-1];\n        t[0] = node;\n    } else if (j < i) {\n        // Shift right from j+1 to i\n        for (int k = i; k > j+1; k--) t[k] = t[k-1];\n        t[j+1] = node;\n    } else { // j > i (j cannot equal i)\n        // Shift left from i+1 to j\n        for (int k = i; k < j; k++) t[k] = t[k+1];\n        t[j] = node;\n    }\n}\n```\n\nThis is O(N) per operation but avoids List allocation.\n\nOkay, let me now put together the complete code. I\'ll keep it clean and handle all edge cases.\n\nAlso, I realize I should handle the special case in the gain formula more carefully. When computing gainInsert for j = N-1 (inserting after last element):\n- A = t[N-1], B = -1 (no next element)\n- Edge(A, B) = 0 (no edge from last)\n- Edge(A, node) = C[A+1, node+1] if A != -1, else C[0, node+1]\n- Edge(node, B) = 0\n- gainInsert = 0 - Edge(A, node) - 0 = -Edge(A, node)\n\nThis means inserting at the end always has a cost of Edge(A, node). This is always non-negative (delta-V ≥ 0), so gainInsert ≤ 0 for appending. Combined with gainRemove > 0, it could still be beneficial.\n\nOkay I think the formulation is correct. Let me now write the final clean code.\n\nFor the simulated annealing, I\'ll implement:\n1. Random swap (O(1) delta computation)\n2. Random 2-opt (O(1) delta computation)\n3. Random relocate (O(1) delta computation)\n\nWith proper temperature scheduling.\n\nHere\'s my final implementation plan:\n\n```csharp\nusing System;\nusing System.Collections.Generic;\nusing System.Linq;\nusing System.Threading;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\nusing System.Diagnostics;\nusing System.Globalization;\n\nclass Program {\n    static double MU;\n    static int N;\n    static double[,] C; // cost[i,j]: 0=depot, 1..N=stations\n    static Stopwatch sw = Stopwatch.StartNew();\n    static long timeLimitMs = 270000; // 4.5 minutes\n    \n    static void Main() {\n        // Parse\n        var tok = Console.ReadLine().Trim()\n            .Split(new[]{\' \',\'\t\'}, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);\n        N = int.Parse(tok[0]);\n        MU = double.Parse(tok[1], CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);\n        \n        var allRV = new double[N+1][];\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N; i++)\n            allRV[i] = ParseVec(Console.ReadLine());\n        \n        C = new double[N+1, N+1];\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N; i++)\n            for (int j = 0; j <= N; j++)\n                if (i != j) C[i,j] = DeltaV(allRV[i], allRV[j]);\n        \n        int[] result;\n        if (N == 1) result = new[]{0};\n        else if (N <= 20) result = SolveHeldKarp();\n        else result = SolveLarge();\n        \n        Console.WriteLine(string.Join(" ", result));\n    }\n    \n    // ... rest of implementation\n}\n```\n\nOkay let me write the full thing now. I\'ll be careful and complete.\n\nI realize I need to think about the SA parameters more carefully for large N:\n- N=100: initial tour cost might be ~1-10 km/s total\n- Initial temperature T0: maybe 0.01 * avg_cost (1% of initial cost)\n- Final temperature Tf: 0.0001 * avg_cost\n- Number of iterations: maybe 10^7 for N=100 within 4 minutes\n- alpha: (Tf/T0)^(1/iterations)\n\nFor a typical orbital problem with delta-V in km/s:\n- Typical DV per hop: 0.1 - 5 km/s\n- Initial tour cost: 10-500 km/s for 100 stations\n- T0: 0.5-5 km/s\n- T_final: 0.001 km/s\n\nActually, let me calibrate T based on actual tour cost after greedy:\n- T0 = 0.1 * initial_cost / N (10% of average step cost)\n- T_final = T0 * 1e-4\n\nNumber of iterations in 4 minutes with ~10M ops/sec: 600M iterations total. For N=100, each iteration is ~O(1), so maybe 100M iterations.\n\nOkay let me just code it up with reasonable parameters and let the timer control when to stop.\n\nLet me also think about parallelism for large N:\n- Run SA from multiple starting points in parallel (use 64 cores)\n- Each thread gets its own copy of the tour and runs SA independently\n- Periodically share the best found solution between threads\n\nThis is called "parallel simulated annealing with occasional synchronization".\n\nFor simplicity, I\'ll use:\n- 64 parallel SA runs\n- Each starts from a different greedy seed\n- No communication between threads (embarrassingly parallel)\n- At the end, pick the best from all threads\n\nThis is simple to implement and effective.\n\nOkay, here\'s my final code:\n\n```csharp\nusing System;\nusing System.Collections.Generic;\nusing System.Linq;\nusing System.Threading;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\nusing System.Diagnostics;\nusing System.Globalization;\n\nclass Program {\n    static double MU;\n    static int N;\n    static double[,] C;\n    static Stopwatch sw;\n    \n    static void Main() {\n        sw = Stopwatch.StartNew();\n        \n        var line1 = Console.ReadLine().Trim().Split(new[]{\' \',\'\\t\'}, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);\n        N = int.Parse(line1[0]);\n        MU = double.Parse(line1[1], CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);\n        \n        var allRV = new double[N+1][];\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N; i++)\n            allRV[i] = ParseVec(Console.ReadLine());\n        \n        C = new double[N+1, N+1];\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N; i++)\n            for (int j = 0; j <= N; j++)\n                if (i != j) C[i,j] = DeltaV(allRV[i], allRV[j]);\n        \n        string result;\n        if (N == 1) {\n            result = "0";\n        } else if (N <= 20) {\n            result = string.Join(" ", SolveHeldKarp());\n        } else {\n            result = string.Join(" ", SolveLarge());\n        }\n        \n        Console.WriteLine(result);\n    }\n    \n    static double[] ParseVec(string s) {\n        return s.Trim().Split(new[]{\' \',\'\\t\'}, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries)\n                .Select(t => double.Parse(t, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)).ToArray();\n    }\n    \n    static double SMA(double[] rv) {\n        double r = Math.Sqrt(rv[0]*rv[0]+rv[1]*rv[1]+rv[2]*rv[2]);\n        double v2 = rv[3]*rv[3]+rv[4]*rv[4]+rv[5]*rv[5];\n        double E = v2*0.5 - MU/r;\n        return (E < 0) ? -MU/(2*E) : double.MaxValue;\n    }\n    \n    static double Inc(double[] rv) {\n        double hx = rv[1]*rv[5]-rv[2]*rv[4];\n        double hy = rv[2]*rv[3]-rv[0]*rv[5];\n        double hz = rv[0]*rv[4]-rv[1]*rv[3];\n        double h = Math.Sqrt(hx*hx+hy*hy+hz*hz);\n        return (h > 1e-10) ? Math.Acos(Math.Max(-1.0, Math.Min(1.0, hz/h))) : 0.0;\n    }\n    \n    static double DeltaV(double[] rv1, double[] rv2) {\n        double a1 = SMA(rv1), a2 = SMA(rv2);\n        \n        if (a1 >= double.MaxValue/2 || a2 >= double.MaxValue/2 || a1 <= 0 || a2 <= 0) {\n            // Fallback: velocity difference\n            double dvx=rv2[3]-rv1[3], dvy=rv2[4]-rv1[4], dvz=rv2[5]-rv1[5];\n            return Math.Sqrt(dvx*dvx+dvy*dvy+dvz*dvz);\n        }\n        \n        double i1 = Inc(rv1), i2 = Inc(rv2);\n        double di = Math.Abs(i2 - i1);\n        \n        double lo = Math.Min(a1,a2), hi = Math.Max(a1,a2);\n        double aT = (lo + hi) / 2.0;\n        \n        double vc_lo = Math.Sqrt(MU/lo);\n        double vc_hi = Math.Sqrt(MU/hi);\n        double vT_peri = Math.Sqrt(MU*(2.0/lo - 1.0/aT));\n        double vT_apo  = Math.Sqrt(MU*(2.0/hi - 1.0/aT));\n        \n        double dv1 = Math.Abs(vT_peri - vc_lo);\n        // Combined plane change and circularization at apoapsis\n        double dv2 = Math.Sqrt(vc_hi*vc_hi + vT_apo*vT_apo - 2*vc_hi*vT_apo*Math.Cos(di));\n        \n        return dv1 + dv2;\n    }\n    \n    static double TourCost(int[] t) {\n        double c = C[0, t[0]+1];\n        for (int i = 1; i < N; i++) c += C[t[i-1]+1, t[i]+1];\n        return c;\n    }\n    \n    // Edge cost: a=-1 means depot, b=-1 means end (no cost)\n    static double E(int a, int b) {\n        if (a == -1 && b == -1) return 0;\n        if (b == -1) return 0; // no outgoing edge to nothing\n        if (a == -1) return C[0, b+1];\n        return C[a+1, b+1];\n    }\n    \n    #region Held-Karp\n    static int[] SolveHeldKarp() {\n        int full = 1 << N;\n        var dp = new float[full * N];\n        var par = new short[full * N];\n        \n        const float INF = float.MaxValue / 2;\n        for (int i = 0; i < dp.Length; i++) { dp[i] = INF; par[i] = -1; }\n        \n        for (int i = 0; i < N; i++)\n            dp[(1<<i)*N + i] = (float)C[0, i+1];\n        \n        for (int mask = 1; mask < full; mask++) {\n            int mN = mask * N;\n            for (int last = 0; last < N; last++) {\n                if ((mask & (1<<last)) == 0) continue;\n                float d = dp[mN + last];\n                if (d >= INF) continue;\n                for (int next = 0; next < N; next++) {\n                    if ((mask & (1<<next)) != 0) continue;\n                    int nm = mask | (1<<next);\n                    float nd = d + (float)C[last+1, next+1];\n                    int idx = nm*N + next;\n                    if (nd < dp[idx]) {\n                        dp[idx] = nd;\n                        par[idx] = (short)last;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        \n        int fMask = full - 1;\n        int fBase = fMask * N;\n        int best = 0;\n        for (int i = 1; i < N; i++)\n            if (dp[fBase+i] < dp[fBase+best]) best = i;\n        \n        var path = new int[N];\n        int cur = best, msk = fMask;\n        for (int s = N-1; s >= 0; s--) {\n            path[s] = cur;\n            int p = par[msk*N + cur];\n            msk ^= (1<<cur);\n            cur = p;\n        }\n        return path;\n    }\n    #endregion\n    \n    #region Large Scale Heuristics\n    static int[] GreedyNN(int seed) {\n        // seed: -1 = from depot, 0..N-1 = from that station first\n        var visited = new bool[N];\n        var tour = new int[N];\n        int cur = seed;\n        int start = 0;\n        \n        if (seed >= 0) {\n            tour[0] = seed;\n            visited[seed] = true;\n            start = 1;\n        }\n        \n        for (int s = start; s < N; s++) {\n            double best = double.MaxValue;\n            int bj = -1;\n            for (int j = 0; j < N; j++) {\n                if (!visited[j]) {\n                    double cost = (cur < 0) ? C[0, j+1] : C[cur+1, j+1];\n                    if (cost < best) { best = cost; bj = j; }\n                }\n            }\n            tour[s] = bj;\n            visited[bj] = true;\n            cur = bj;\n        }\n        return tour;\n    }\n    \n    static void TwoOpt(int[] t) {\n        bool improved = true;\n        while (improved) {\n            improved = false;\n            for (int i = 0; i < N-1; i++) {\n                for (int j = i+2; j < N; j++) {\n                    int a = (i>0) ? t[i-1] : -1;\n                    int b = t[i], c = t[j];\n                    int d = (j<N-1) ? t[j+1] : -1;\n                    double before = E(a,b) + E(c,d);\n                    double after = E(a,c) + E(b,d);\n                    if (after < before - 1e-9) {\n                        Array.Reverse(t, i, j-i+1);\n                        improved = true;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    static void OrOpt1(int[] t) {\n        // Repeatedly try to relocate single nodes to better positions\n        bool improved = true;\n        while (improved) {\n            improved = false;\n            for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) {\n                int node = t[i];\n                int prev = (i>0) ? t[i-1] : -1;\n                int next = (i<N-1) ? t[i+1] : -1;\n                double gainRemove = E(prev,node) + E(node,next) - E(prev,next);\n                \n                int bestJ = int.MinValue;\n                double bestGain = 1e-9;\n                \n                for (int j = -1; j < N; j++) {\n                    if (j == i-1 || j == i) continue;\n                    int A = (j==-1) ? -1 : t[j];\n                    int B = (j+1<N) ? t[j+1] : -1;\n                    // Skip if B is the node itself (only possible if j+1 == i, i.e., j == i-1, already excluded)\n                    double gi = E(A,B) - E(A,node) - E(node,B);\n                    double tg = gainRemove + gi;\n                    if (tg > bestGain) { bestGain = tg; bestJ = j; }\n                }\n                \n                if (bestJ > int.MinValue) {\n                    ApplyRelocate(t, i, bestJ);\n                    improved = true;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    static void ApplyRelocate(int[] t, int from, int insertAfter) {\n        int node = t[from];\n        if (insertAfter == -1) {\n            for (int k = from; k > 0; k--) t[k] = t[k-1];\n            t[0] = node;\n        } else if (insertAfter < from) {\n            for (int k = from; k > insertAfter+1; k--) t[k] = t[k-1];\n            t[insertAfter+1] = node;\n        } else {\n            for (int k = from; k < insertAfter; k++) t[k] = t[k+1];\n            t[insertAfter] = node;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    static int[] SolveLarge() {\n        int numThreads = Math.Min(Environment.ProcessorCount, N+1);\n        var results = new (int[] tour, double cost)[numThreads];\n        \n        Parallel.For(0, numThreads, new ParallelOptions { MaxDegreeOfParallelism = numThreads }, idx => {\n            int seed = (idx == 0) ? -1 : (idx-1) % N;\n            var tour = GreedyNN(seed);\n            TwoOpt(tour);\n            OrOpt1(tour);\n            TwoOpt(tour);\n            results[idx] = (tour, TourCost(tour));\n        });\n        \n        // Find best\n        int bestIdx = 0;\n        for (int i = 1; i < numThreads; i++)\n            if (results[i].cost < results[bestIdx].cost) bestIdx = i;\n        \n        var best = (int[])results[bestIdx].tour.Clone();\n        double bestCost = results[bestIdx].cost;\n        \n        // Run SA from best for remaining time\n        SA(best, ref bestCost, 270000 - (int)sw.ElapsedMilliseconds);\n        \n        return best;\n    }\n    \n    static void SA(int[] tour, ref double bestCost, int timeBudgetMs) {\n        var current = (int[])tour.Clone();\n        double currentCost = bestCost;\n        \n        var rng = new Random(42);\n        double T = currentCost * 0.05; // 5% of tour cost\n        long endMs = sw.ElapsedMilliseconds + timeBudgetMs;\n        \n        long iterations = 0;\n        long accepted = 0;\n        \n        // Pre-compute ending temperature\n        double Tfinal = T * 1e-5;\n        long totalIterations = (long)(timeBudgetMs * 1000); // rough estimate: 1M per second per thread\n        double alpha = Math.Pow(Tfinal/T, 1.0/totalIterations);\n        \n        while (sw.ElapsedMilliseconds < endMs) {\n            iterations++;\n            \n            int moveType = rng.Next(3);\n            double delta;\n            int a, b;\n            \n            if (moveType == 0) {\n                // Swap\n                a = rng.Next(N); b = rng.Next(N);\n                if (a == b) { T *= alpha; continue; }\n                delta = SwapDelta(current, a, b);\n            } else if (moveType == 1) {\n                // Reverse segment (2-opt)\n                a = rng.Next(N); b = rng.Next(N);\n                if (a > b) { int t = a; a = b; b = t; }\n                if (a == b) { T *= alpha; continue; }\n                delta = TwoOptDelta(current, a, b);\n            } else {\n                // Relocate\n                a = rng.Next(N); b = rng.Next(N+1) - 1; // -1 to N-1\n                if (b == a-1 || b == a) { T *= alpha; continue; }\n                delta = RelocateDelta(current, a, b);\n            }\n            \n            if (delta < 0 || rng.NextDouble() < Math.Exp(-delta/T)) {\n                ApplyMove(current, moveType, a, b);\n                currentCost += delta;\n                if (currentCost < bestCost - 1e-9) {\n                    bestCost = currentCost;\n                    Array.Copy(current, tour, N);\n                }\n                accepted++;\n            }\n            \n            T *= alpha;\n            if (T < Tfinal) T = Tfinal; // don\'t let T go below minimum\n        }\n    }\n    \n    static double SwapDelta(int[] t, int i, int j) {\n        if (i > j) { int tmp = i; i = j; j = tmp; }\n        if (j == i+1) {\n            // Adjacent\n            int a = (i>0) ? t[i-1] : -1;\n            int ni = t[i], nj = t[j];\n            int d = (j<N-1) ? t[j+1] : -1;\n            return E(a,nj)+E(nj,ni)+E(ni,d) - E(a,ni)-E(ni,nj)-E(nj,d);\n        }\n        int prev_i=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1, next_i=(i<N-1)?t[i+1]:-1;\n        int prev_j=(j>0)?t[j-1]:-1, next_j=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n        double before = E(prev_i,t[i])+E(t[i],next_i)+E(prev_j,t[j])+E(t[j],next_j);\n        double after = E(prev_i,t[j])+E(t[j],next_i)+E(prev_j,t[i])+E(t[i],next_j);\n        return after - before;\n    }\n    \n    static double TwoOptDelta(int[] t, int i, int j) {\n        // Reverse segment t[i..j]\n        int a=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1, b=t[i], c=t[j], d=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n        return E(a,c)+E(b,d) - E(a,b)-E(c,d);\n    }\n    \n    static double RelocateDelta(int[] t, int from, int insertAfter) {\n        // Remove t[from], insert after position insertAfter\n        // insertAfter = -1: insert at beginning\n        int node = t[from];\n        int prev = (from>0)?t[from-1]:-1;\n        int next = (from<N-1)?t[from+1]:-1;\n        double gainRemove = E(prev,node)+E(node,next)-E(prev,next);\n        \n        int A = (insertAfter==-1)?-1:t[insertAfter];\n        int B;\n        if (insertAfter == -1) B = t[0];\n        else if (insertAfter+1 < N) B = t[insertAfter+1];\n        else B = -1;\n        \n        // But we need to handle the case where insertAfter+1 == from\n        // In that case B would be node itself, but we already excluded that with the check in SA\n        \n        double gainInsert = E(A,B)-E(A,node)-E(node,B);\n        return -(gainRemove + gainInsert); // delta = new_cost - old_cost = -(gain)\n    }\n    \n    static void ApplyMove(int[] t, int moveType, int a, int b) {\n        if (moveType == 0) {\n            int tmp = t[a]; t[a] = t[b]; t[b] = tmp;\n        } else if (moveType == 1) {\n            if (a > b) { int tmp = a; a = b; b = tmp; }\n            Array.Reverse(t, a, b-a+1);\n        } else {\n            ApplyRelocate(t, a, b);\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\nHmm wait, there are several issues:\n1. In SwapDelta for non-adjacent nodes, I need to be careful: the edges from/to t[i] and t[j] include edges like (prev_i, t[i]), (t[i], next_i), (prev_j, t[j]), (t[j], next_j). After swap, they become (prev_i, t[j]), (t[j], next_i), (prev_j, t[i]), (t[i], next_j). This is correct ONLY if i+1 != j (non-adjacent). If i and j are adjacent (j == i+1), then prev_j == t[i] and the formula breaks down because we\'re double-counting the middle edge.\n\nI handle the adjacent case separately, so that\'s fine.\n\n2. In RelocateDelta, if insertAfter > from, then B = t[insertAfter+1] might reference the wrong element because after removing t[from], indices shift. But for delta computation, I\'m working in the ORIGINAL array, and the gain formula I derived earlier shows this is correct (the nodes A and B are identified by value, not index).\n\nBut wait: if insertAfter > from, then after removal:\n- Elements shift left by 1 from from+1 onwards\n- The element that WAS at insertAfter is now at insertAfter-1\n- The element that WAS at insertAfter+1 is now at insertAfter\n\nIn my original derivation, A = t[insertAfter] and B = t[insertAfter+1] in the ORIGINAL array. The delta is:\ndelta = E(prev,next) + E(A,node) + E(node,B) - E(prev,node) - E(node,next) - E(A,B)\n\nThis formula is in terms of the nodes (by identity), not their positions. But to avoid hardcoding estimates, I\'ll check the stopwatch periodically and adjust alpha dynamically.\n\nAlternatively, I can use a simpler approach: just run SA until time is up, with a fixed alpha that gives good results in practice:\n\n```csharp\nstatic void SA(int[] tour, ref double bestCost, int timeBudgetMs) {\n    var current = (int[])tour.Clone();\n    double currentCost = bestCost;\n    var rng = new Random(123);\n    \n    // Estimate initial temperature: accept 50% of random swaps\n    double avgEdge = currentCost / N;\n    double T = avgEdge * 0.2; // 20% of average edge cost\n    double Tmin = avgEdge * 1e-6;\n    \n    // Use a reheat schedule for stuck solutions\n    long endMs = sw.ElapsedMilliseconds + timeBudgetMs;\n    long checkInterval = 100000;\n    long iters = 0;\n    int noImproveCount = 0;\n    \n    while (sw.ElapsedMilliseconds < endMs) {\n        // Batch of iterations\n        for (long k = 0; k < checkInterval; k++) {\n            // Random move\n            int moveType = rng.Next(3);\n            int a = rng.Next(N), b;\n            double delta;\n            \n            if (moveType == 0) {\n                b = rng.Next(N);\n                if (b == a) continue;\n                delta = SwapDelta(current, a, b);\n            } else if (moveType == 1) {\n                b = rng.Next(N);\n                if (a == b) continue;\n                if (a > b) { int tmp = a; a = b; b = tmp; }\n                delta = TwoOptDelta(current, a, b);\n            } else {\n                b = rng.Next(N+1) - 1;\n                if (b == a-1 || b == a) continue;\n                delta = RelocateDelta(current, a, b);\n            }\n            \n            if (delta < 0 || (T > Tmin && rng.NextDouble() < Math.Exp(-delta/T))) {\n                ApplyMove(current, moveType, a, b);\n                currentCost += delta;\n                if (currentCost < bestCost - 1e-9) {\n                    bestCost = currentCost;\n                    Array.Copy(current, tour, N);\n                    noImproveCount = 0;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        \n        iters += checkInterval;\n        T *= 0.999; // gradual cooling\n        \n        if (T < Tmin) T = Tmin;\n    }\n}\n```\n\nWith alpha=0.999 per checkInterval of 100000, T will decrease by factor e^(-1) ≈ 0.37 every 1000 check intervals. With 240 seconds and checks at 100k iterations each:\n- At 10M iters/sec: 2.4B total iters / 100k per check = 24000 checks\n- T after 24000 checks: T0 * 0.999^24000 ≈ T0 * e^(-24) ≈ T0 * 3.7e-11\n\nThat\'s way too cold! k < 10000; k++) {\n            int moveType = rng.Next(3);\n            int a = rng.Next(N), b;\n            double delta;\n            \n            if (moveType == 0) { // swap\n                b = rng.Next(N);\n                if (b == a) continue;\n                delta = SwapDelta(current, a, b);\n            } else if (moveType == 1) { // 2-opt\n                b = rng.Next(N);\n                if (a == b) continue;\n                if (a > b) { int tmp = a; Let me proceed.\n\nAlternatively, I can precompute the acceptance probability: if delta < 0, always accept; else compute exp(-delta/T).\n\nHere\'s my concern about RelocateDelta when insertAfter = N-1 and from = N-2:\n- node = t[N-2]\n- prev = t[N-3] (or -1 if N=2)\n- next = t[N-1]\n- gainRemove = E(prev, node) + E(node, t[N-1]) - E(prev, t[N-1])\n- A = t[N-1], B = -1\n- gainInsert = E(t[N-1], -1) - E(t[N-1], node) - E(node, -1)\n            = 0 - E(t[N-1], node) - 0\n            = -E(t[N-1], node)\n\nBut wait: this computes the gain of moving t[N-2] to after t[N-1].
