Fine.\n\nOkay let me now write the complete code. I\'ll try to be concise but comprehensive.\n\nActually, I realize I need to double-check my delta-V formula. For Hohmann transfer between two circular orbits of radii r1 and r2 (r1 < r2):\n\n- Circular velocity at r1: v_c1 = sqrt(mu/r1)\n- Circular velocity at r2: v_c2 = sqrt(mu/r2)\n- Transfer ellipse semi-major axis: a_t = (r1 + r2) / 2\n- Velocity at periapsis of transfer: v_t1 = sqrt(mu * (2/r1 - 1/a_t)) = sqrt(2*mu*r2 / (r1*(r1+r2)))\n- Velocity at apoapsis of transfer: v_t2 = sqrt(mu * (2/r2 - 1/a_t)) = sqrt(2*mu*r1 / (r2*(r1+r2)))\n\n- DV1 = v_t1 - v_c1 (burn to raise apoapsis to r2)\n- DV2 = v_c2 - v_t2 (burn to circularize at r2)\n\nFor the plane change combined with DV2 at apoapsis:\n- DV2_combined = sqrt(v_c2^2 + v_t2^2 - 2*v_c2*v_t2*cos(delta_i))\n\nThis is the combined delta-V for the plane change and circularization at apoapsis. This is correct!\n\nWhen a1 = a2 (same semi-major axis but different inclination):\n- a_t = a1\n- v_t1 = sqrt(mu*(2/a1 - 1/a1)) = sqrt(mu/a1) = v_c1\n- v_t2 = sqrt(mu*(2/a1 - 1/a1)) = v_c1\n- DV1 = v_t1 - v_c1 = 0 (no Hohmann burn needed)\n- DV2_combined = sqrt(v_c1^2 + v_c1^2 - 2*v_c1^2*cos(di)) = 2*v_c1*sin(di/2)\n\nThis is the plane change delta-V for orbits at the same altitude. ✓\n\nFor a1 < a2 (Hohmann to higher orbit):\n- DV1 = v_t1 - v_c1 > 0 (prograde burn to raise orbit)\n- Combined: DV2_combined = sqrt(v_c2^2 + v_t2^2 - 2*v_c2*v_t2*cos(di))\n  - When di=0: DV2_combined = |v_c2 - v_t2| = DV2 ✓\n  - When di>0: DV2_combined > DV2 ✓\n\nGreat, the formula looks correct.\n\nBut what if a1 > a2? In my code, I use lo=min(a1,a2) and hi=max(a1,a2), which always sets lo < hi. Then:\n- Transfer goes from lo (periapsis) to hi (apoapsis)\n- DV1 is burn at lo (periapsis) to enter transfer\n- DV2_combined is burn at hi (apoapsis) to circularize + plane change\n\nBut if the actual orbit 1 is at hi (larger SMA) and orbit 2 is at lo (smaller SMA), then:\n- Transfer goes from hi (periapsis of Hohmann... wait, for a transfer from hi to lo, the periapsis is lo and apoapsis is hi)\n- Actually for a transfer from hi to lo:\n  - Burn at hi: slow down to enter transfer ellipse (periapsis at lo)\n  - Burn at lo: slow down more to circularize\n  - The transfer ellipse has periapsis at lo and apoapsis at hi\n\nSo whether we go from lo→hi or hi→lo, the transfer ellipse is the same (with periapsis at lo and apoapsis at hi). The delta-Vs are:\n- DV1 at hi: v_t_at_hi - v_c_hi = (v_t2 in my notation, which is the velocity at apoapsis of the transfer, when I set hi as apoapsis)\n  Wait, I\'m confusing myself.\n\nLet me redo:\n- For transfer from orbit 1 (at a1) to orbit 2 (at a2), assuming circular:\n  - Case a1 < a2 (going to higher orbit):\n    - Burn at a1 (prograde): dv1 = v_t_peri - v_c1 > 0 (where v_t_peri is periapsis velocity of transfer)\n    - Burn at a2 (prograde): dv2 = v_c2 - v_t_apo > 0 (circularize at a2)\n  - Case a1 > a2 (going to lower orbit):\n    - Burn at a1 (retrograde): dv1 = v_c1 - v_t_apo > 0 (slow down to enter transfer, now at apoapsis)\n    - Burn at a2 (retrograde): dv2 = v_t_peri - v_c2 > 0 (circularize at a2)\n  \n  In both cases:\n  - Transfer ellipse has periapsis at min(a1,a2) and apoapsis at max(a1,a2)\n  - v_t_peri = sqrt(mu*(2/lo - 1/aT)) where lo=min(a1,a2), aT=(a1+a2)/2\n  - v_t_apo = sqrt(mu*(2/hi - 1/aT)) where hi=max(a1,a2)\n  - dv1 = |v_c_source - v_t_at_source| where v_t_at_source is the transfer velocity at the source orbit\n  - dv2 = |v_c_dest - v_t_at_dest| where v_t_at_dest is the transfer velocity at the dest orbit\n\nFor asymmetric cost (a1→a2 vs a2→a1):\n- Transfer from a1 to a2 (a1<a2): dv1=|v_t_peri-v_c_lo|, dv2=|v_c_hi-v_t_apo|\n- Transfer from a2 to a1 (a2>a1): dv1=|v_c_hi-v_t_apo|, dv2=|v_t_peri-v_c_lo|\n- Total is the same in both cases! Hohmann transfer is symmetric in terms of total DV.\n\nSo for Hohmann transfers (no plane change), cost(a1→a2) = cost(a2→a1). The cost matrix is symmetric for pure Hohmann.\n\nWith plane changes, if I do the plane change at the apoapsis regardless of direction, it\'s still the same in both directions. So the cost matrix should be symmetric.\n\nBut wait, the source orbit might be at the apoapsis or periapsis of the transfer. If a1 > a2, the source is at a1 (apoapsis of transfer), and I should do the plane change at a1 (the transfer apoapsis), giving:\n- DV1_combined = sqrt(v_c1^2 + v_t_apo^2 - 2*v_c1*v_t_apo*cos(di)) [combined plane change and deorbit]\n- DV2 = v_t_peri - v_c2 [circularize at destination]\n\nAlternatively, if a1 < a2, the source is at a1 (periapsis), and I do the plane change at a2 (apoapsis):\n- DV1 = v_t_peri - v_c1 [prograde burn at periapsis]\n- DV2_combined = sqrt(v_c2^2 + v_t_apo^2 - 2*v_c2*v_t_apo*cos(di)) [combined at apoapsis]\n\nFor a1 > a2:\n- DV1_combined = sqrt(v_c1^2 + v_t_apo^2 - 2*v_c1*v_t_apo*cos(di))\n  (where v_t_apo here is velocity at apoapsis of transfer = velocity at source orbit)\n  Wait, for a1 > a2: source at a1 = apoapsis of transfer, v_t_at_a1 = v_t_apo\n  DV1_combined = sqrt(v_c1^2 + v_t_apo^2 - 2*v_c1*v_t_apo*cos(di))\n- DV2 = |v_t_peri - v_c2|\n\nHmm, this makes the cost asymmetric (DV for a1→a2 ≠ DV for a2→a1).\n\nActually, this is more correct physically: the optimal strategy depends on direction:\n- Going up (a1<a2): do plane change at apoapsis\n- Going down (a1>a2): do plane change at periapsis (= departure point)\n\nWait, actually the optimal is always to do the plane change at the point of lowest velocity (apoapsis), regardless of direction. For going down:\n- Start at a1 (= apoapsis of transfer since a1>a2)\n- The apoapsis IS the starting point\n- So you do the plane change + deorbit burn at the start\n- DV1 = sqrt(v_c1^2 + v_t_apo^2 - 2*v_c1*v_t_apo*cos(di)) [at source = apoapsis]\n- DV2 = |v_t_peri - v_c2| [circularize at dest = periapsis, no plane change]\n\nFor going up:\n- Start at a1 (= periapsis of transfer since a1<a2)\n- DV1 = |v_t_peri - v_c1| [prograde at source = periapsis, no plane change here]\n- DV2 = sqrt(v_c2^2 + v_t_apo^2 - 2*v_c2*v_t_apo*cos(di)) [at dest = apoapsis]\n\nSo the cost is:\n- a1<a2: dv1 + dv2_combined = |v_t_peri - v_c1| + sqrt(v_c2^2 + v_t_apo^2 - 2*v_c2*v_t_apo*cos(di))\n- a1>a2: dv1_combined + dv2 = sqrt(v_c1^2 + v_t_apo^2 - 2*v_c1*v_t_apo*cos(di)) + |v_t_peri - v_c2|\n\nFor symmetric case (a1=a2=a): both give 2*v_c*sin(di/2). ✓\n\nFor di=0:\n- a1<a2: |v_t_peri - v_c1| + |v_c2 - v_t_apo| = DV_Hohmann ✓\n- a1>a2: |v_c1 - v_t_apo| + |v_t_peri - v_c2| = DV_Hohmann ✓ (same Hohmann DV by symmetry)\n\nSo the costs for a1→a2 and a2→a1 (with the same di) might differ when di≠0. This makes the cost matrix asymmetric, which is fine for TSP (though TSP with asymmetric costs requires slightly different handling).\n\nFor simplicity, I\'ll make the cost symmetric by taking the average or using the minimum of the two directions. Or I\'ll just use the formula I have and let it be slightly asymmetric (which is physically more accurate).\n\nIn my code:\n```csharp\nstatic double DeltaV(double[] rv1, double[] rv2) {\n    // ...\n    double lo = Math.Min(a1,a2), hi = Math.Max(a1,a2);\n    // Transfer ellipse\n    double aT = (lo+hi)/2;\n    double vT_peri = Math.Sqrt(MU*(2/lo - 1/aT));\n    double vT_apo = Math.Sqrt(MU*(2/hi - 1/aT));\n    \n    double vc_lo = Math.Sqrt(MU/lo);\n    double vc_hi = Math.Sqrt(MU/hi);\n    \n    double dv1 = Math.Abs(vT_peri - vc_lo);\n    double dv2 = Math.Sqrt(vc_hi*vc_hi + vT_apo*vT_apo - 2*vc_hi*vT_apo*Math.Cos(di));\n    \n    return dv1 + dv2;\n}\n```\n\nThis assumes:\n- If a1 < a2: dv1 is the burn at a1 (periapsis), dv2 is the combined burn at a2 (apoapsis)\n- If a1 > a2: treating the orbit as going from lo to hi is WRONG\n  - We actually start at hi (a1 if a1>a2) and transfer to lo\n  - My formula always treats the lower orbit as periapsis and higher as apoapsis, giving dv1 at lo and dv2 at hi\n  - But for a1>a2 direction, we start at hi (a1), so dv1 should be at hi and dv2 at lo\n\nSo my current formula has an error for the asymmetric direction.\n\nTo fix this, I should compute DV based on the actual direction (a1→a2 vs a2→a1):\n\n```csharp\nstatic double DeltaV(double[] rv1, double[] rv2) {\n    double a1 = SMA(rv1), a2 = SMA(rv2);\n    // ... (hyperbolic check)\n    \n    double i1 = Inc(rv1), i2 = Inc(rv2);\n    double di = Math.Abs(i2-i1);\n    \n    double aT = (a1+a2)/2;\n    double vc1 = Math.Sqrt(MU/a1);\n    double vc2 = Math.Sqrt(MU/a2);\n    double vT_at_a1 = Math.Sqrt(MU*(2/a1 - 1/aT));\n    double vT_at_a2 = Math.Sqrt(MU*(2/a2 - 1/aT));\n    \n    // For going from a1 to a2:\n    // - If a1 < a2: a1 is periapsis, do plane change at a2 (apoapsis)\n    //   dv1 = |vT_at_a1 - vc1|, dv2 = sqrt(vc2^2 + vT_at_a2^2 - 2*vc2*vT_at_a2*cos(di))\n    // - If a1 > a2: a1 is apoapsis, do plane change at a1 (combined burn)\n    //   dv1 = sqrt(vc1^2 + vT_at_a1^2 - 2*vc1*vT_at_a1*cos(di)), dv2 = |vT_at_a2 - vc2|\n    \n    double dv;\n    if (a1 <= a2) {\n        double dv1 = Math.Abs(vT_at_a1 - vc1);\n        double dv2 = Math.Sqrt(vc2*vc2 + vT_at_a2*vT_at_a2 - 2*vc2*vT_at_a2*Math.Cos(di));\n        dv = dv1 + dv2;\n    } else {\n        double dv1 = Math.Sqrt(vc1*vc1 + vT_at_a1*vT_at_a1 - 2*vc1*vT_at_a1*Math.Cos(di));\n        double dv2 = Math.Abs(vT_at_a2 - vc2);\n        dv = dv1 + dv2;\n    }\n    \n    return dv;\n}\n```\n\nLet me verify for a1 = a2:\n- aT = a1 = a2\n- vT_at_a1 = sqrt(mu*(2/a1 - 1/a1)) = sqrt(mu/a1) = vc1\n- Similarly for vT_at_a2\n- Case a1<=a2: dv1 = |vc1-vc1| = 0, dv2 = sqrt(vc2^2+vc2^2-2*vc2^2*cos(di)) = vc2*sqrt(2*(1-cos(di))) = 2*vc2*sin(di/2) ✓\n- Case a1>a2: never (since a1==a2, we take a1<=a2 case) ✓\n\nFor a1 < a2, di = 0:\n- dv1 = |vT_at_a1 - vc1| = vT_at_a1 - vc1 (since transfer periapsis velocity > circular) ✓\n- dv2 = sqrt(vc2^2+vT_at_a2^2-2*vc2*vT_at_a2) = |vc2-vT_at_a2| ✓\n\nThis looks correct!\n\nNow let me verify for a1 > a2, di = 0:\n- vT_at_a1 = sqrt(mu*(2/a1-1/aT)): since a1 > aT, 2/a1-1/aT = (2*aT-a1)/(a1*aT) = (2*(a1+a2)/2-a1)/(a1*aT) = a2/(a1*aT) > 0\n  Wait: aT=(a1+a2)/2, so 1/aT=2/(a1+a2). 2/a1 - 1/aT = 2/a1 - 2/(a1+a2) = 2(a1+a2-a1)/(a1(a1+a2)) = 2a2/(a1(a1+a2))\n  vT_at_a1 = sqrt(MU * 2*a2/(a1*(a1+a2)))\n  vc1 = sqrt(MU/a1)\n  Since a1 is at apoapsis of transfer: vT_at_a1 < vc1 (slower at apoapsis) ✓\n  dv1 = |sqrt(vc1^2+vT_at_a1^2-0)-...| = ... wait, for di=0:\n  dv1 = sqrt(vc1^2+vT_at_a1^2-2*vc1*vT_at_a1) = |vc1-vT_at_a1| = vc1-vT_at_a1 ✓\n  \n  Similarly dv2 = |vT_at_a2 - vc2|\n  vT_at_a2 = sqrt(mu*(2/a2-1/aT)): a2 is periapsis, so vT_at_a2 > vc2 ✓\n  dv2 = vT_at_a2 - vc2 ✓\n  \n  Total: vc1-vT_at_a1 + vT_at_a2 - vc2 = DV_Hohmann (for a1>a2 case) ✓\n\nGreat, the formula is correct.\n\nLet me also verify symmetry for di=0:\n- a1→a2 (a1<a2): (vT_peri-vc1) + (vc2-vT_apo) where vT_peri is at a1, vT_apo is at a2\n  Wait, I need to be careful about notation. Let me use subscripts:\n  - For a1<a2: source=a1 (periapsis), dest=a2 (apoapsis)\n    - vT_peri = sqrt(MU*(2/a1-1/aT)), vT_apo = sqrt(MU*(2/a2-1/aT))\n    - DV = (vT_peri-vc1) + (vc2-vT_apo)\n  - For a2→a1 (a2>a1): source=a2 (apoapsis), dest=a1 (periapsis)\n    - vT_apo_at_a2 = sqrt(MU*(2/a2-1/aT)) = same vT_apo\n    - vT_peri_at_a1 = sqrt(MU*(2/a1-1/aT)) = same vT_peri\n    - DV = (vc2-vT_apo) + (vT_peri-vc1)\n  \n  These are equal! Hohmann transfer is symmetric. ✓\n\nFor the asymmetric cost matrix (different di for each direction), it depends on whether we do the plane change at the departure or arrival.\n\nAnyway, let me just go with my formula above which is physically sound. The cost matrix may be slightly asymmetric, which is fine.\n\nNow, let me think about one more edge case: when aT is very small (if a1 or a2 is near zero). This shouldn\'t happen for real orbital states (the problem says altitude ~3807 km, so radius ~10178 km). Real orbits have SMA > Earth\'s radius = 6371 km. So SMA > 6371 km. The delta-V values will be in the range 0-10 km/s typically.\n\nAlright, I\'m going to write the final code now. Let me consolidate everything.\n\nA few final design decisions:\n1. Use double for DP (not float)\n2. Use short for parent pointers (N <= 20, so values 0-19 fit in short)\n3. SA with time-based cooling\n4. Parallel greedy starts for large N\n5. Two-opt + Or-opt after greedy\n\nHere\'s the complete final code:\n\n(Let me check array allocation for N=20:\n- dp: 2^20 * 20 * 8 bytes = 167,772,160 bytes ≈ 160 MB\n- par: 2^20 * 20 * 2 bytes = 41,943,040 bytes ≈ 40 MB\n- Total: ~200 MB. Fine.)\n\nHere\'s the full code:\n\n```csharp\nusing System;\nusing System.Collections.Generic;\nusing System.Linq;\nusing System.Threading;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\nusing System.Diagnostics;\nusing System.Globalization;\n\nclass Program {\n    static double MU;\n    static int N;\n    static double[,] C; // C[i,j]: 0=depot, 1..N=stations (station k has cost index k+1)\n    static Stopwatch Sw = Stopwatch.StartNew();\n\n    static void Main() {\n        var tok = Console.ReadLine().Trim()\n            .Split(new char[]{\' \',\'\\t\'}, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);\n        N = int.Parse(tok[0]);\n        MU = double.Parse(tok[1], CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);\n\n        var allRV = new double[N + 1][];\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N; i++)\n            allRV[i] = ParseVec(Console.ReadLine());\n\n        C = new double[N + 1, N + 1];\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N; i++)\n            for (int j = 0; j <= N; j++)\n                if (i != j) C[i, j] = DeltaV(allRV[i], allRV[j]);\n\n        int[] result;\n        if (N == 1)\n            result = new[] { 0 };\n        else if (N <= 20)\n            result = HeldKarp();\n        else\n            result = SolveLarge();\n\n        Console.WriteLine(string.Join(" ", result));\n    }\n\n    static double[] ParseVec(string s) {\n        return s.Trim().Split(new char[]{\' \',\'\\t\'}, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries)\n                .Select(x => double.Parse(x, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)).ToArray();\n    }\n\n    static double SMA(double[] rv) {\n        double r = Math.Sqrt(rv[0]*rv[0] + rv[1]*rv[1] + rv[2]*rv[2]);\n        double v2 = rv[3]*rv[3] + rv[4]*rv[4] + rv[5]*rv[5];\n        double E = 0.5*v2 - MU/r;\n        return (E < 0) ? -MU/(2.0*E) : -1.0; // -1 for hyperbolic\n    }\n\n    static double Inc(double[] rv) {\n        double hx = rv[1]*rv[5] - rv[2]*rv[4];\n        double hy = rv[2]*rv[3] - rv[0]*rv[5];\n        double hz = rv[0]*rv[4] - rv[1]*rv[3];\n        double h = Math.Sqrt(hx*hx + hy*hy + hz*hz);\n        return (h > 1e-10) ? Math.Acos(Math.Max(-1.0, Math.Min(1.0, hz/h))) : 0.0;\n    }\n\n    static double DeltaV(double[] rv1, double[] rv2) {\n        double a1 = SMA(rv1), a2 = SMA(rv2);\n        if (a1 <= 0 || a2 <= 0) {\n            // Fallback: Δv = |Δv|\n            double dvx = rv2[3]-rv1[3], dvy = rv2[4]-rv1[4], dvz = rv2[5]-rv1[5];\n            return Math.Sqrt(dvx*dvx + dvy*dvy + dvz*dvz);\n        }\n        double i1 = Inc(rv1), i2 = Inc(rv2);\n        double di = Math.Abs(i2 - i1);\n        double aT = (a1 + a2) / 2.0;\n        double vc1 = Math.Sqrt(MU/a1);\n        double vc2 = Math.Sqrt(MU/a2);\n        double vT1 = Math.Sqrt(MU*(2.0/a1 - 1.0/aT));\n        double vT2 = Math.Sqrt(MU*(2.0/a2 - 1.0/aT));\n        double dv;\n        if (a1 <= a2) {\n            // Source at periapsis, dest at apoapsis: do plane change at apoapsis\n            double burn1 = Math.Abs(vT1 - vc1);\n            double burn2 = Math.Sqrt(vc2*vc2 + vT2*vT2 - 2*vc2*vT2*Math.Cos(di));\n            dv = burn1 + burn2;\n        } else {\n            // Source at apoapsis, dest at periapsis: do plane change at apoapsis (source)\n            double burn1 = Math.Sqrt(vc1*vc1 + vT1*vT1 - 2*vc1*vT1*Math.Cos(di));\n            double burn2 = Math.Abs(vT2 - vc2);\n            dv = burn1 + burn2;\n        }\n        return dv;\n    }\n\n    // Edge cost: a=-1 means depot, b=-1 means no edge (0 cost)\n    static double Ecost(int a, int b) {\n        if (b == -1) return 0.0;\n        int ai = (a == -1) ? 0 : a + 1;\n        return C[ai, b + 1];\n    }\n\n    static double TourCost(int[] t) {\n        double cost = Ecost(-1, t[0]);\n        for (int i = 1; i < t.Length; i++) cost += Ecost(t[i-1], t[i]);\n        return cost;\n    }\n\n    #region Held-Karp DP\n    static int[] HeldKarp() {\n        int full = 1 << N;\n        var dp = new double[full * N];\n        var par = new short[full * N];\n        const double INF = double.MaxValue / 2;\n        for (int i = 0; i < dp.Length; i++) { dp[i] = INF; par[i] = -1; }\n\n        for (int i = 0; i < N; i++)\n            dp[(1 << i) * N + i] = C[0, i + 1];\n\n        for (int mask = 1; mask < full; mask++) {\n            int mN = mask * N;\n            for (int last = 0; last < N; last++) {\n                if ((mask & (1 << last)) == 0) continue;\n                double d = dp[mN + last];\n                if (d >= INF) continue;\n                for (int next = 0; next < N; next++) {\n                    if ((mask & (1 << next)) != 0) continue;\n                    int nm = mask | (1 << next);\n                    double nd = d + C[last + 1, next + 1];\n                    int idx = nm * N + next;\n                    if (nd < dp[idx]) {\n                        dp[idx] = nd;\n                        par[idx] = (short)last;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        int fMask = full - 1, fBase = fMask * N;\n        int best = 0;\n        for (int i = 1; i < N; i++)\n            if (dp[fBase + i] < dp[fBase + best]) best = i;\n\n        var path = new int[N];\n        int cur = best, msk = fMask;\n        for (int s = N - 1; s >= 0; s--) {\n            path[s] = cur;\n            int p = par[msk * N + cur];\n            msk ^= (1 << cur);\n            cur = p;\n        }\n        return path;\n    }\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Greedy & 2-opt & Or-opt\n    static int[] GreedyNN(int firstStation) {\n        // firstStation: -1 = start from depot (pick cheapest first)\n        var visited = new bool[N];\n        var tour = new int[N];\n        int cur = firstStation;\n        int startStep = 0;\n        if (firstStation >= 0) {\n            tour[0] = firstStation;\n            visited[firstStation] = true;\n            startStep = 1;\n        }\n        for (int s = startStep; s < N; s++) {\n            double best = double.MaxValue;\n            int bj = -1;\n            for (int j = 0; j < N; j++) {\n                if (!visited[j]) {\n                    double c = Ecost(cur, j);\n                    if (c < best) { best = c; bj = j; }\n                }\n            }\n            tour[s] = bj;\n            visited[bj] = true;\n            cur = bj;\n        }\n        return tour;\n    }\n\n    static void TwoOpt(int[] t) {\n        bool improved = true;\n        while (improved) {\n            improved = false;\n            for (int i = 0; i < N - 1; i++) {\n                for (int j = i + 2; j < N; j++) {\n                    int a = (i > 0) ? t[i-1] : -1;\n                    int b = t[i], c = t[j];\n                    int d = (j < N - 1) ? t[j+1] : -1;\n                    double before = Ecost(a, b) + Ecost(c, d);\n                    double after = Ecost(a, c) + Ecost(b, d);\n                    if (after < before - 1e-10) {\n                        Array.Reverse(t, i, j - i + 1);\n                        improved = true;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    static void OrOpt1(int[] t) {\n        bool improved = true;\n        while (improved) {\n            improved = false;\n            for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) {\n                int node = t[i];\n                int prev = (i > 0) ? t[i-1] : -1;\n                int next = (i < N-1) ? t[i+1] : -1;\n                double gainRemove = Ecost(prev, node) + Ecost(node, next) - Ecost(prev, next);\n                int bestJ = int.MinValue;\n                double bestGain = 1e-10;\n                for (int j = -1; j < N; j++) {\n                    if (j == i-1 || j == i) continue;\n                    int A = (j == -1) ? -1 : t[j];\n                    int B = (j + 1 < N) ? t[j+1] : -1;\n                    // Check if B == node (when j+1 == i)\n                    // j+1==i implies j==i-1, already excluded\n                    double gi = Ecost(A, B) - Ecost(A, node) - Ecost(node, B);\n                    if (gainRemove + gi > bestGain) {\n                        bestGain = gainRemove + gi;\n                        bestJ = j;\n                    }\n                }\n                if (bestJ > int.MinValue) {\n                    ApplyRelocate(t, i, bestJ);\n                    improved = true;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    static void ApplyRelocate(int[] t, int from, int insertAfter) {\n        int node = t[from];\n        if (insertAfter < from) {\n            // Shift right: t[insertAfter+1..from] shift right by 1\n            for (int k = from; k > insertAfter + 1; k--) t[k] = t[k-1];\n            t[insertAfter + 1] = node;\n        } else {\n            // insertAfter > from\n            // Shift left: t[from..insertAfter-1] shift left by 1\n            for (int k = from; k < insertAfter; k++) t[k] = t[k+1];\n            t[insertAfter] = node;\n        }\n    }\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Simulated Annealing\n    static double SwapDelta(int[] t, int i, int j) {\n        if (i > j) { int tmp = i; i = j; j = tmp; }\n        if (j == i + 1) {\n            int a = (i > 0) ? t[i-1] : -1;\n            int ni = t[i], nj = t[j];\n            int d = (j < N-1) ? t[j+1] : -1;\n            return (Ecost(a, nj) + Ecost(nj, ni) + Ecost(ni, d))\n                 - (Ecost(a, ni) + Ecost(ni, nj) + Ecost(nj, d));\n        }\n        int pi = (i>0)?t[i-1]:-1, ni2 = (i<N-1)?t[i+1]:-1;\n        int pj = (j>0)?t[j-1]:-1, nj2 = (j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n        double before = Ecost(pi,t[i]) + Ecost(t[i],ni2) + Ecost(pj,t[j]) + Ecost(t[j],nj2);\n        double after = Ecost(pi,t[j]) + Ecost(t[j],ni2) + Ecost(pj,t[i]) + Ecost(t[i],nj2);\n        return after - before;\n    }\n\n    static double TwoOptDelta(int[] t, int i, int j) {\n        // Reverse segment [i..j]\n        int a = (i>0)?t[i-1]:-1, b = t[i], c = t[j], d = (j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n        return (Ecost(a, c) + Ecost(b, d)) - (Ecost(a, b) + Ecost(c, d));\n    }\n\n    static double RelocateDelta(int[] t, int from, int insertAfter) {\n        // Remove t[from] and insert after position insertAfter\n        // insertAfter == -1: insert at beginning\n        int node = t[from];\n        int prev = (from > 0) ? t[from-1] : -1;\n        int next = (from < N-1) ? t[from+1] : -1;\n        double gainRemove = Ecost(prev, node) + Ecost(node, next) - Ecost(prev, next);\n        int A = (insertAfter == -1) ? -1 : t[insertAfter];\n        int B;\n        if (insertAfter == -1) B = (N > 0) ? t[0] : -1;\n        else if (insertAfter + 1 < N) B = t[insertAfter + 1];\n        else B = -1;\n        double gainInsert = Ecost(A, B) - Ecost(A, node) - Ecost(node, B);\n        return -(gainRemove + gainInsert);\n    }\n\n    static void SA(int[] tour, ref double bestCost, long timeBudgetMs) {\n        if (timeBudgetMs <= 0) return;\n        var current = (int[])tour.Clone();\n        double currentCost = bestCost;\n        var rng = new Random(42);\n        double avgEdge = currentCost / N;\n        double T0 = avgEdge * 0.5;\n        double Tmin = avgEdge * 1e-6;\n        if (T0 <= 0) T0 = 1.0;\n        long startMs = Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds;\n        long endMs = startMs + timeBudgetMs;\n        while (Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds < endMs) {\n            long nowMs = Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds;\n            if (nowMs >= endMs) break;\n            double progress = (double)(nowMs - startMs) / timeBudgetMs;\n            double T = T0 * Math.Pow(Tmin / T0, progress);\n            if (T < Tmin) T = Tmin;\n            for (int k = 0; k < 10000; k++) {\n                int moveType = rng.Next(3);\n                int a = rng.Next(N), b;\n                double delta;\n                if (moveType == 0) {\n                    b = rng.Next(N);\n                    if (b == a) continue;\n                    delta = SwapDelta(current, a, b);\n                } else if (moveType == 1) {\n                    b = rng.Next(N);\n                    if (a == b) continue;\n                    if (a > b) { int tmp = a; a = b; b = tmp; }\n                    if (a == b) continue;\n                    delta = TwoOptDelta(current, a, b);\n                } else {\n                    b = rng.Next(N + 1) - 1; // -1 to N-1\n                    if (b == a - 1 || b == a) continue;\n                    delta = RelocateDelta(current, a, b);\n                }\n                if (delta <= 0 || rng.NextDouble() < Math.Exp(-delta / T)) {\n                    if (moveType == 0) {\n                        int tmp = current[a]; current[a] = current[b]; current[b] = tmp;\n                    } else if (moveType == 1) {\n                        Array.Reverse(current, a, b - a + 1);\n                    } else {\n                        ApplyRelocate(current, a, b);\n                    }\n                    currentCost += delta;\n                    if (currentCost < bestCost - 1e-10) {\n                        bestCost = currentCost;\n                        Array.Copy(current, tour, N);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Large Scale\n    static int[] SolveLarge() {\n        int numSeeds = Math.Min(Environment.ProcessorCount * 2, N + 1);\n        var results = new (int[] tour, double cost)[numSeeds];\n        Parallel.For(0, numSeeds, new ParallelOptions { MaxDegreeOfParallelism = 64 }, idx => {\n            int seed = (idx == 0) ? -1 : (idx - 1) % N;\n            var t = GreedyNN(seed);\n            TwoOpt(t);\n            OrOpt1(t);\n            TwoOpt(t);\n            results[idx] = (t, TourCost(t));\n        });\n        \n        int bestIdx = 0;\n        for (int i = 1; i < numSeeds; i++)\n            if (results[i].cost < results[bestIdx].cost) bestIdx = i;\n        \n        var bestTour = results[bestIdx].tour;\n        double bestCost = results[bestIdx].cost;\n        \n        long remaining = 270000 - Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds;\n        if (remaining > 1000) SA(bestTour, ref bestCost, remaining);\n        \n        return bestTour;\n    }\n    #endregion\n}\n```\n\nHmm, I think there might be an issue with the ApplyRelocate when insertAfter == -1 (insert at the beginning):\n- from = some position > 0 (since if i=0 and j=-1, it\'s excluded by j==i-1)\n- Actually, when i=0 and j=-1: j == i-1 = -1 ✓ so it IS excluded. The gain formula I derived was:\ngain = gainRemove + (E(A,B) - E(A,node) - E(node,B))\n\nThis is correct as I showed in my derivation. The key insight is that the gain only involves the original positions of the affected edges, regardless of index shifts.\n\nLet me double-check with a small example:\n- Tour: [0, 1, 2, 3, 4] (depot -> 0 -> 1 -> 2 -> 3 -> 4)\n- from=1 (node=1), insertAfter=3 (insert after element 3)\n- Original cost contributions: E(0,1)+E(1,2)+E(3,4)\n- After move: [0, 2, 3, 1, 4]\n- New cost contributions: E(0,2)+E(3,1)+E(1,4)\n- Delta = E(0,2)+E(3,1)+E(1,4) - E(0,1)-E(1,2)-E(3,4)\n\nMy formula:\n- gainRemove = E(0,1)+E(1,2)-E(0,2) (removing node 1 from between 0 and 2)\n- A = t[3] = 3, B = t[4] = 4\n- gainInsert = E(3,4)-E(3,1)-E(1,4)\n- Total gain = gainRemove + gainInsert = E(0,1)+E(1,2)-E(0,2) + E(3,4)-E(3,1)-E(1,4)\n- Delta = -(total gain) = E(0,2)+E(3,1)+E(1,4) - E(0,1)-E(1,2)-E(3,4) ✓\n\nPerfect, the formula is correct!\n\nNow there\'s one more subtle issue: in the RelocateDelta function, when I access t[insertAfter+1], and insertAfter+1 could equal from. I\'ll also add some minor optimizations:\n1. In 2-opt, use a cache or just the standard O(N^2) implementation.\n2. In OrOpt1, don\'t restart from the beginning after each improvement; do a full pass and restart only if any improvement was found.\n\nWait, in my current OrOpt1, I restart from i=0 after each improvement (because I set `improved = true` and the while loop restarts). But within a single pass, when I find an improvement for some i, I apply it and then set `improved = true` but continue the for loop. This might cause issues because subsequent i values reference the modified array.\n\nActually, looking at the code:\n```csharp\nstatic void OrOpt1(int[] t) {\n    bool improved = true;\n    while (improved) {\n        improved = false;\n        for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) {\n            // ... find bestJ ...\n            if (bestJ > int.MinValue) {\n                ApplyRelocate(t, i, bestJ);\n                improved = true;\n                // CONTINUE the for loop (don\'t break)\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\nThe inner for loop continues after applying a relocation. The remaining iterations of the for loop will see the modified array, which might give incorrect delta computations for the already-visited i values. But since we\'re going forward (i increases), the values at positions < current i have already been processed. The values at positions > current i haven\'t been processed yet and might be affected by the relocation.\n\nThis could lead to incorrect results. For correctness, after each improvement, I should restart the inner loop (set i = -1 and increment to 0). But this might be slow for cases with many improvements.\n\nFor simplicity, let me just not restart within the loop and do multiple passes until no improvement:\n\nActually, the current code does multiple passes (the while loop). Within each pass (the for loop), applying a relocation and continuing might give suboptimal moves for subsequent iterations. But the next pass will catch any remaining improvements. So the code is correct in terms of final result, just might take a few more passes.\n\nTo be safe and correct, let me break out of the inner loop after each improvement:\n\n```csharp\nstatic void OrOpt1(int[] t) {\n    bool improved = true;\n    while (improved) {\n        improved = false;\n        for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) {\n            // ... find bestJ ...\n            if (bestJ > int.MinValue) {\n                ApplyRelocate(t, i, bestJ);\n                improved = true;\n                break; // restart the pass\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\nThis restarts the inner loop after each improvement, which is O(N) per improvement. Total: O(N^2) per improvement found, and with at most O(N^2) total improvements, O(N^4) in worst case. For N=100: 10^8 operations. Might be 1-10 seconds. Acceptable.\n\nBut alternatively, not breaking and doing full passes might be faster in practice (fewer passes needed, even if each pass has some suboptimality). Let me just leave it without the break for performance.\n\nActually, thinking about it more: after applying ApplyRelocate(t, i, bestJ), the positions of elements in the array change. If bestJ < i, elements at positions bestJ+1 to i shift right. The current i is now pointing to a different element. If bestJ > i, elements at positions i+1 to bestJ shift left. The current i now has the element that was at i+1.\n\nSo continuing the loop after a relocation might process elements incorrectly. To avoid this, I\'ll break after each improvement:\n\nActually for the OrOpt1 in local search (not SA), it\'s fine to use break. The SA will handle further improvements.\n\nLet me use break for correctness.\n\nOkay, I think I\'ve spent too long analyzing. Let me just write the clean final code.\n\nHere\'s my final version - writing it now:\n\n```csharp\nusing System;\nusing System.Linq;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\nusing System.Diagnostics;\nusing System.Globalization;\n\nclass Program {\n    static double MU;\n    static int N;\n    static double[,] C;\n    static readonly Stopwatch Sw = Stopwatch.StartNew();\n\n    static void Main() {\n        var tok = Console.ReadLine().Trim()\n            .Split(new char[]{\' \',\'\\t\'}, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);\n        N = int.Parse(tok[0]);\n        MU = double.Parse(tok[1], CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);\n\n        var allRV = new double[N + 1][];\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N; i++)\n            allRV[i] = Console.ReadLine().Trim()\n                .Split(new char[]{\' \',\'\\t\'}, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries)\n                .Select(s => double.Parse(s, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)).ToArray();\n\n        C = new double[N + 1, N + 1];\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N; i++)\n            for (int j = 0; j <= N; j++)\n                if (i != j) C[i, j] = DeltaV(allRV[i], allRV[j]);\n\n        int[] result;\n        if (N == 1)\n            result = new[] { 0 };\n        else if (N <= 20)\n            result = HeldKarp();\n        else\n            result = SolveLarge();\n\n        Console.WriteLine(string.Join(" ", result));\n    }\n\n    static double SMA(double[] rv) {\n        double r = Math.Sqrt(rv[0]*rv[0] + rv[1]*rv[1] + rv[2]*rv[2]);\n        double v2 = rv[3]*rv[3] + rv[4]*rv[4] + rv[5]*rv[5];\n        double E = 0.5*v2 - MU/r;\n        return E < 0 ? -MU/(2.0*E) : -1.0;\n    }\n\n    static double Inc(double[] rv) {\n        double hx = rv[1]*rv[5] - rv[2]*rv[4];\n        double hy = rv[2]*rv[3] - rv[0]*rv[5];\n        double hz = rv[0]*rv[4] - rv[1]*rv[3];\n        double h = Math.Sqrt(hx*hx + hy*hy + hz*hz);\n        return h > 1e-10 ? Math.Acos(Math.Max(-1.0, Math.Min(1.0, hz/h))) : 0.0;\n    }\n\n    static double DeltaV(double[] rv1, double[] rv2) {\n        double a1 = SMA(rv1), a2 = SMA(rv2);\n        if (a1 <= 0 || a2 <= 0) {\n            double dx = rv2[3]-rv1[3], dy = rv2[4]-rv1[4], dz = rv2[5]-rv1[5];\n            return Math.Sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy + dz*dz);\n        }\n        double di = Math.Abs(Inc(rv1) - Inc(rv2));\n        double aT = (a1+a2)/2.0;\n        double vc1 = Math.Sqrt(MU/a1), vc2 = Math.Sqrt(MU/a2);\n        double vT1 = Math.Sqrt(MU*(2.0/a1 - 1.0/aT));\n        double vT2 = Math.Sqrt(MU*(2.0/a2 - 1.0/aT));\n        double dv1, dv2;\n        if (a1 <= a2) {\n            dv1 = Math.Abs(vT1 - vc1);\n            dv2 = Math.Sqrt(vc2*vc2 + vT2*vT2 - 2*vc2*vT2*Math.Cos(di));\n        } else {\n            dv1 = Math.Sqrt(vc1*vc1 + vT1*vT1 - 2*vc1*vT1*Math.Cos(di));\n            dv2 = Math.Abs(vT2 - vc2);\n        }\n        return dv1 + dv2;\n    }\n\n    static double Ecost(int a, int b) {\n        if (b < 0) return 0.0;\n        return C[(a < 0) ? 0 : a+1, b+1];\n    }\n\n    static double TourCost(int[] t) {\n        double c = Ecost(-1, t[0]);\n        for (int i = 1; i < t.Length; i++) c += Ecost(t[i-1], t[i]);\n        return c;\n    }\n\n    static int[] HeldKarp() {\n        int full = 1 << N;\n        var dp = new double[full * N];\n        var par = new short[full * N];\n        for (int i = 0; i < dp.Length; i++) { dp[i] = double.MaxValue/2; par[i] = -1; }\n        for (int i = 0; i < N; i++)\n            dp[(1<<i)*N + i] = C[0, i+1];\n        for (int mask = 1; mask < full; mask++) {\n            int mN = mask*N;\n            for (int last = 0; last < N; last++) {\n                if ((mask & (1<<last)) == 0) continue;\n                double d = dp[mN+last];\n                if (d >= double.MaxValue/2) continue;\n                for (int next = 0; next < N; next++) {\n                    if ((mask & (1<<next)) != 0) continue;\n                    int nm = mask|(1<<next);\n                    double nd = d + C[last+1, next+1];\n                    int idx = nm*N+next;\n                    if (nd < dp[idx]) { dp[idx] = nd; par[idx] = (short)last; }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        int fM = full-1, fB = fM*N, best = 0;\n        for (int i = 1; i < N; i++) if (dp[fB+i] < dp[fB+best]) best = i;\n        var path = new int[N];\n        int cur = best, msk = fM;\n        for (int s = N-1; s >= 0; s--) {\n            path[s] = cur;\n            int p = par[msk*N+cur];\n            msk ^= (1<<cur);\n            cur = p;\n        }\n        return path;\n    }\n\n    static int[] GreedyNN(int first) {\n        var vis = new bool[N];\n        var t = new int[N];\n        int cur = first, start = 0;\n        if (first >= 0) { t[0] = first; vis[first] = true; start = 1; }\n        for (int s = start; s < N; s++) {\n            double best = double.MaxValue; int bj = 0;\n            for (int j = 0; j < N; j++) {\n                if (!vis[j]) { double c = Ecost(cur, j); if (c < best) { best = c; bj = j; } }\n            }\n            t[s] = bj; vis[bj] = true; cur = bj;\n        }\n        return t;\n    }\n\n    static void TwoOpt(int[] t) {\n        bool imp = true;\n        while (imp) {\n            imp = false;\n            for (int i = 0; i < N-1; i++) for (int j = i+2; j < N; j++) {\n                int a=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1, b=t[i], c=t[j], d=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n                if (Ecost(a,c)+Ecost(b,d) < Ecost(a,b)+Ecost(c,d) - 1e-10) {\n                    Array.Reverse(t, i, j-i+1); imp = true;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    static void OrOpt(int[] t, int segLen) {\n        bool imp = true;\n        while (imp) {\n            imp = false;\n            for (int i = 0; i <= N-segLen; i++) {\n                int prev = (i>0)?t[i-1]:-1;\n                int firstSeg = t[i], lastSeg = t[i+segLen-1];\n                int after = (i+segLen<N)?t[i+segLen]:-1;\n                double gainRem = Ecost(prev,firstSeg)+Ecost(lastSeg,after)-Ecost(prev,after);\n                double bestGain = 1e-10; int bestJ = int.MinValue;\n                // Try inserting segment after position j\n                for (int j = -1; j < N; j++) {\n                    if (j >= i-1 && j < i+segLen) continue; // overlaps current position\n                    int A = (j==-1)?-1:t[j];\n                    int B = (j+1<N)?t[j+1]:-1;\n                    double gi = Ecost(A,B)-Ecost(A,firstSeg)-Ecost(lastSeg,B);\n                    if (gainRem+gi > bestGain) { bestGain = gainRem+gi; bestJ = j; }\n                }\n                if (bestJ > int.MinValue) {\n                    // Extract segment\n                    var seg = new int[segLen];\n                    for (int k = 0; k < segLen; k++) seg[k] = t[i+k];\n                    // Apply: remove segment from i, insert after bestJ\n                    ApplySegmentRelocate(t, i, segLen, bestJ);\n                    imp = true; break; // restart\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    static void ApplySegmentRelocate(int[] t, int from, int segLen, int insertAfter) {\n        var seg = new int[segLen];\n        for (int k = 0; k < segLen; k++) seg[k] = t[from+k];\n        // Remove segment\n        var list = new System.Collections.Generic.List<int>(t);\n        list.RemoveRange(from, segLen);\n        // Find insertion point\n        int insertPos;\n        if (insertAfter < from)\n            insertPos = insertAfter + 1;\n        else\n            insertPos = insertAfter - segLen + 1;\n        if (insertPos < 0) insertPos = 0;\n        list.InsertRange(insertPos, seg);\n        for (int k = 0; k < N; k++) t[k] = list[k];\n    }\n\n    static double SwapDelta(int[] t, int i, int j) {\n        if (i > j) { int tmp = i; i = j; j = tmp; }\n        if (j == i+1) {\n            int a=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1, ni=t[i], nj=t[j], d=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n            return Ecost(a,nj)+Ecost(nj,ni)+Ecost(ni,d) - Ecost(a,ni)-Ecost(ni,nj)-Ecost(nj,d);\n        }\n        int pi=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1, ni2=(i<N-1)?t[i+1]:-1, pj=(j>0)?t[j-1]:-1, nj2=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n        return Ecost(pi,t[j])+Ecost(t[j],ni2)+Ecost(pj,t[i])+Ecost(t[i],nj2)\n             - Ecost(pi,t[i])-Ecost(t[i],ni2)-Ecost(pj,t[j])-Ecost(t[j],nj2);\n    }\n\n    static double TwoOptDelta(int[] t, int i, int j) {\n        int a=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1, b=t[i], c=t[j], d=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n        return Ecost(a,c)+Ecost(b,d) - Ecost(a,b)-Ecost(c,d);\n    }\n\n    static double RelocateDelta(int[] t, int from, int insertAfter) {\n        int node = t[from];\n        int prev = (from>0)?t[from-1]:-1, next = (from<N-1)?t[from+1]:-1;\n        double gainRem = Ecost(prev,node)+Ecost(node,next)-Ecost(prev,next);\n        int A = (insertAfter<0)?-1:t[insertAfter];\n        int B = (insertAfter+1<N)?t[insertAfter+1]:-1;\n        double gainIns = Ecost(A,B)-Ecost(A,node)-Ecost(node,B);\n        return -(gainRem+gainIns);\n    }\n\n    static void ApplyRelocate(int[] t, int from, int insertAfter) {\n        int node = t[from];\n        if (insertAfter < from) {\n            for (int k = from; k > insertAfter+1; k--) t[k] = t[k-1];\n            t[insertAfter+1] = node;\n        } else {\n            for (int k = from; k < insertAfter; k++) t[k] = t[k+1];\n            t[insertAfter] = node;\n        }\n    }\n\n    static void SA(int[] tour, ref double bestCost, long budgetMs) {\n        if (budgetMs <= 0) return;\n        var cur = (int[])tour.Clone();\n        double curCost = bestCost;\n        var rng = new Random(42);\n        double avgE = curCost / N;\n        double T0 = avgE*0.5, Tmin = avgE*1e-6;\n        if (T0 <= 0) T0 = 0.1;\n        long startMs = Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds, endMs = startMs+budgetMs;\n        while (true) {\n            long nowMs = Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds;\n            if (nowMs >= endMs) break;\n            double prog = Math.Min(1.0, (double)(nowMs-startMs)/budgetMs);\n            double T = T0 * Math.Pow(Tmin/T0, prog);\n            if (T < Tmin) T = Tmin;\n            for (int k = 0; k < 10000; k++) {\n                int mt = rng.Next(3), a = rng.Next(N), b;\n                double delta;\n                if (mt == 0) {\n                    b = rng.Next(N); if (b==a) continue;\n                    delta = SwapDelta(cur, a, b);\n                } else if (mt == 1) {\n                    b = rng.Next(N); if (b==a) continue;\n                    if (a>b) { int tmp=a; a=b; b=tmp; }\n                    delta = TwoOptDelta(cur, a, b);\n                } else {\n                    b = rng.Next(N+1)-1; if (b==a-1||b==a) continue;\n                    delta = RelocateDelta(cur, a, b);\n                }\n                if (delta <= 0 || rng.NextDouble() < Math.Exp(-delta/T)) {\n                    if (mt==0) { int tmp=cur[a]; cur[a]=cur[b]; cur[b]=tmp; }\n                    else if (mt==1) Array.Reverse(cur, a, b-a+1);\n                    else ApplyRelocate(cur, a, b);\n                    curCost += delta;\n                    if (curCost < bestCost-1e-10) {\n                        bestCost = curCost;\n                        Array.Copy(cur, tour, N);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    static int[] SolveLarge() {\n        int cores = Math.Min(64, Environment.ProcessorCount);\n        int numSeeds = Math.Min(cores*2, N+1);\n        var results = new (int[] t, double c)[numSeeds];\n        Parallel.For(0, numSeeds, new ParallelOptions{MaxDegreeOfParallelism=cores}, idx => {\n            int s = (idx==0)?-1:(idx-1)%N;\n            var t = GreedyNN(s);\n            TwoOpt(t);\n            OrOpt(t, 1);\n            OrOpt(t, 2);\n            OrOpt(t, 3);\n            TwoOpt(t);\n            results[idx] = (t, TourCost(t));\n        });\n        int bi = 0;\n        for (int i = 1; i < numSeeds; i++) if (results[i].c < results[bi].c) bi = i;\n        var best = results[bi].t;\n        double bc = results[bi].c;\n        long rem = 270000 - Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds;\n        if (rem > 2000) SA(best, ref bc, rem);\n        return best;\n    }\n}\n```\n\nWait, I have an issue with `ApplySegmentRelocate`: when `insertAfter < from` and `insertAfter >= 0`, the insertion position after removal is `insertAfter + 1`. Let me write it out completely:\n\n```csharp\nusing System;\nusing System.Linq;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\nusing System.Diagnostics;\nusing System.Globalization;\n\nclass Program {\n    static double MU;\n    static int N;\n    static double[,] C; // C[i,j]: 0=depot, 1..N stations\n    static readonly Stopwatch Sw = Stopwatch.StartNew();\n\n    static void Main() {\n        // Parse\n        var t1 = (Console.ReadLine() ?? "").Trim()\n            .Split(new[]{\' \',\'\\t\'}, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);\n        N = int.Parse(t1[0]);\n        MU = double.Parse(t1[1], CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);\n        var allRV = new double[N+1][];\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N; i++)\n            allRV[i] = (Console.ReadLine() ?? "").Trim()\n                .Split(new[]{\' \',\'\\t\'}, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries)\n                .Select(x => double.Parse(x, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)).ToArray();\n        \n        // Build cost matrix\n        C = new double[N+1, N+1];\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N; i++)\n            for (int j = 0; j <= N; j++)\n                if (i != j) C[i,j] = DV(allRV[i], allRV[j]);\n        \n        // Solve\n        int[] result;\n        if (N == 1) result = new[]{0};\n        else if (N <= 20) result = HeldKarp();\n        else result = LargeScale();\n        \n        Console.WriteLine(string.Join(" ", result));\n    }\n\n    // Orbital mechanics helpers\n    static double SMA(double[] rv) {\n        double r = Math.Sqrt(rv[0]*rv[0]+rv[1]*rv[1]+rv[2]*rv[2]);\n        double v2 = rv[3]*rv[3]+rv[4]*rv[4]+rv[5]*rv[5];\n        double E = 0.5*v2 - MU/r;\n        return E < 0 ? -MU/(2*E) : -1.0;\n    }\n    static double Inc(double[] rv) {\n        double hx=rv[1]*rv[5]-rv[2]*rv[4], hy=rv[2]*rv[3]-rv[0]*rv[5], hz=rv[0]*rv[4]-rv[1]*rv[3];\n        double h=Math.Sqrt(hx*hx+hy*hy+hz*hz);\n        return h>1e-10 ? Math.Acos(Math.Max(-1.0,Math.Min(1.0,hz/h))) : 0.0;\n    }\n    static double DV(double[] rv1, double[] rv2) {\n        double a1=SMA(rv1), a2=SMA(rv2);\n        if (a1<=0||a2<=0) {\n            double dx=rv2[3]-rv1[3],dy=rv2[4]-rv1[4],dz=rv2[5]-rv1[5];\n            return Math.Sqrt(dx*dx+dy*dy+dz*dz);\n        }\n        double di=Math.Abs(Inc(rv1)-Inc(rv2));\n        double aT=(a1+a2)/2;\n        double vc1=Math.Sqrt(MU/a1),vc2=Math.Sqrt(MU/a2);\n        double vT1=Math.Sqrt(MU*(2.0/a1-1.0/aT)),vT2=Math.Sqrt(MU*(2.0/a2-1.0/aT));\n        if (a1<=a2) return Math.Abs(vT1-vc1)+Math.Sqrt(vc2*vc2+vT2*vT2-2*vc2*vT2*Math.Cos(di));\n        else return Math.Sqrt(vc1*vc1+vT1*vT1-2*vc1*vT1*Math.Cos(di))+Math.Abs(vT2-vc2);\n    }\n    \n    // Edge cost helper: indices are station indices (0..N-1), -1=depot, -2=nothing\n    static double E(int a, int b) {\n        if (b==-1||b==-2) return 0;\n        return C[(a==-1||a==-2)?0:a+1, b+1];\n    }\n    static double TourCost(int[] t) {\n        double c=E(-1,t[0]);\n        for (int i=1;i<t.Length;i++) c+=E(t[i-1],t[i]);\n        return c;\n    }\n    \n    // Held-Karp exact solver for N<=20\n    static int[] HeldKarp() {\n        int full=1<<N;\n        var dp=new double[full*N];\n        var par=new short[full*N];\n        for (int i=0;i<dp.Length;i++){dp[i]=double.MaxValue/2;par[i]=-1;}\n        for (int i=0;i<N;i++) dp[(1<<i)*N+i]=C[0,i+1];\n        for (int mask=1;mask<full;mask++) {\n            int mN=mask*N;\n            for (int last=0;last<N;last++) {\n                if ((mask&(1<<last))==0) continue;\n                double d=dp[mN+last];\n                if (d>=double.MaxValue/2) continue;\n                for (int next=0;next<N;next++) {\n                    if ((mask&(1<<next))!=0) continue;\n                    int nm=mask|(1<<next);\n                    double nd=d+C[last+1,next+1];\n                    int idx=nm*N+next;\n                    if (nd<dp[idx]){dp[idx]=nd;par[idx]=(short)last;}\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        int fM=full-1,fB=fM*N,best=0;\n        for (int i=1;i<N;i++) if (dp[fB+i]<dp[fB+best]) best=i;\n        var path=new int[N];\n        int cur=best,msk=fM;\n        for (int s=N-1;s>=0;s--) {\n            path[s]=cur;\n            int p=par[msk*N+cur];\n            msk^=(1<<cur);\n            cur=p;\n        }\n        return path;\n    }\n    \n    // Greedy nearest neighbor\n    static int[] Greedy(int first) { // first=-1: from depot\n        var vis=new bool[N];\n        var t=new int[N];\n        int cur=first,s0=0;\n        if (first>=0){t[0]=first;vis[first]=true;s0=1;}\n        for (int s=s0;s<N;s++) {\n            double best=double.MaxValue;int bj=0;\n            for (int j=0;j<N;j++) if (!vis[j]&&E(cur,j)<best){best=E(cur,j);bj=j;}\n            t[s]=bj;vis[bj]=true;cur=bj;\n        }\n        return t;\n    }\n    \n    // 2-opt local search\n    static bool TwoOpt(int[] t) {\n        bool anyImp=false,imp=true;\n        while (imp) {\n            imp=false;\n            for (int i=0;i<N-1;i++) for (int j=i+2;j<N;j++) {\n                int a=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,b=t[i],c=t[j],d=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n                if (E(a,c)+E(b,d)<E(a,b)+E(c,d)-1e-10){\n                    Array.Reverse(t,i,j-i+1);imp=anyImp=true;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        return anyImp;\n    }\n    \n    // Or-opt: relocate segments of size segLen\n    static bool OrOpt(int[] t, int segLen) {\n        bool anyImp=false,imp=true;\n        while (imp) {\n            imp=false;\n            for (int i=0;i<=N-segLen;i++) {\n                int prev=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1;\n                int fs=t[i],ls=t[i+segLen-1];\n                int aft=(i+segLen<N)?t[i+segLen]:-1;\n                double gRem=E(prev,fs)+E(ls,aft)-E(prev,aft);\n                if (gRem<=1e-10) continue; // can\'t gain from removing\n                int bestJ=int.MinValue;double bestG=1e-10;\n                for (int j=-1;j<N;j++) {\n                    if (j>=i-1&&j<i+segLen) continue;\n                    int A=(j<0)?-1:t[j],B=(j+1<N)?t[j+1]:-1;\n                    // Edge case: if j+1 is within segment (j+1 in [i..i+segLen-1]), but that\'s excluded by j<i+segLen\n                    double gI=E(A,B)-E(A,fs)-E(ls,B);\n                    double tg=gRem+gI;\n                    if (tg>bestG){bestG=tg;bestJ=j;}\n                }\n                if (bestJ>int.MinValue){\n                    ApplySegMove(t,i,segLen,bestJ);\n                    imp=anyImp=true;break;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        return anyImp;\n    }\n    \n    static void ApplySegMove(int[] t, int from, int segLen, int insertAfter) {\n        var seg=new int[segLen];\n        Array.Copy(t,from,seg,0,segLen);\n        if (insertAfter<from) {\n            // Shift t[insertAfter+1..from-1] right by segLen\n            for (int k=from-1;k>=insertAfter+1;k--) t[k+segLen]=t[k];\n            for (int k=0;k<segLen;k++) t[insertAfter+1+k]=seg[k];\n        } else {\n            // insertAfter >= from+segLen\n            // Shift t[from+segLen..insertAfter] left by segLen\n            for (int k=from;k<=insertAfter-segLen;k++) t[k]=t[k+segLen];\n            for (int k=0;k<segLen;k++) t[insertAfter-segLen+1+k]=seg[k];\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // SA delta computations\n    static double DeltaSwap(int[] t, int i, int j) {\n        if (i>j){int tmp=i;i=j;j=tmp;}\n        if (j==i+1) {\n            int a=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,ni=t[i],nj=t[j],d=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n            return E(a,nj)+E(nj,ni)+E(ni,d)-E(a,ni)-E(ni,nj)-E(nj,d);\n        }\n        int pi=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,ni2=t[i+1],pj=t[j-1],nj2=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n        return E(pi,t[j])+E(t[j],ni2)+E(pj,t[i])+E(t[i],nj2)\n             - E(pi,t[i])-E(t[i],ni2)-E(pj,t[j])-E(t[j],nj2);\n    }\n    static double Delta2Opt(int[] t, int i, int j) {\n        int a=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,b=t[i],c=t[j],d=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n        return E(a,c)+E(b,d)-E(a,b)-E(c,d);\n    }\n    static double DeltaReloc(int[] t, int from, int iA) {\n        int node=t[from],prev=(from>0)?t[from-1]:-1,next=(from<N-1)?t[from+1]:-1;\n        double gR=E(prev,node)+E(node,next)-E(prev,next);\n        int A=(iA<0)?-1:t[iA],B=(iA+1<N)?t[iA+1]:-1;\n        return -(gR+E(A,B)-E(A,node)-E(node,B));\n    }\n    \n    static void SA(int[] tour, ref double bestCost, long budgetMs) {\n        if (budgetMs<=100) return;\n        var cur=(int[])tour.Clone();\n        double curCost=bestCost;\n        var rng=new Random(42);\n        double avgE=curCost/N;\n        double T0=avgE*0.5,Tmin=avgE*1e-6;\n        if (T0<=0) T0=0.1;\n        long startMs=Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds,endMs=startMs+budgetMs;\n        while (true) {\n            long nowMs=Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds;\n            if (nowMs>=endMs) break;\n            double prog=Math.Min(1.0,(double)(nowMs-startMs)/budgetMs);\n            double T=T0*Math.Pow(Tmin/T0,prog);\n            if (T<Tmin) T=Tmin;\n                   delta=DeltaSwap(cur,a,b);\n                } else if (mt==1) {\n                    b=rng.Next(N);if (b==a) continue;\n                    if (a>b){int tmp=a;a=b;b=tmp;}\n                    delta=Delta2Opt(cur,a,b);\n                } else {\n                    b=rng.Next(N+1)-1;if (b==a-1||b==a) continue;\n                    delta=DeltaReloc(cur,a,b);\n                }\n                if (delta<=0||rng.NextDouble()<Math.Exp(-delta/T)) {\n                    if (mt==0){int tmp=cur[a];cur[a]=cur[b];cur[b]=tmp;}\n                    else if (mt==1) Array.Reverse(cur,a,b-a+1);\n                    else ApplySegMove(cur,a,1,b); // use ApplySegMove for relocation\n                    curCost+=delta;\n                    if (curCost<bestCost-1e-10){\n                        bestCost=curCost;\n                        Array.Copy(cur,tour,N);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    static int[] LargeScale() {\n        int cores=Math.Min(64,Environment.ProcessorCount);\n        int numS=Math.Min(cores+1,N+1);\n        var results=new (int[] t, double c)[numS];\n        Parallel.For(0,numS,new ParallelOptions{MaxDegreeOfParallelism=cores},idx=>{\n            int s=(idx==0)?-1:(idx-1)%N;\n            var t=Greedy(s);\n            TwoOpt(t);\n Here it is:\n\nActually wait, there\'s one more issue I want to address: for large N (e.g., 100), the OrOpt with restart (`break` after finding improvement) can be slow because:\n- O(N) to scan for improvement\n- O(N) to apply the move\n- Repeat until no improvement: at most O(N^2) improvements\n- Total: O(N^3) for segLen=1 alone\n\nFor N=100: O(100^3) = O(10^6). Fine.\nFor N=100 with segLen=1,2,3 and TwoOpt: all fast.\n\nThe main time sink will be TwoOpt:\n- O(N^2) per pass\n- Multiple passes until convergence\n- For N=100: each pass is 10^4 operations, maybe 100 passes: 10^6 operations total\n- Very fast\n\nSo the parallel phase should complete in well under 10 seconds for N=100, leaving plenty of time for SA.\n\nOkay let me just write the code. I\'ll double check everything during writing.\n\nHere\'s the final code:\n\n```csharp\nusing System;\nusing System.Linq;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\nusing System.Diagnostics;\nusing System.Globalization;\n\nclass Program {\n    static double MU;\n    static int N;\n    static double[,] C;\n    static readonly Stopwatch Sw = Stopwatch.StartNew();\n\n    static void Main() {\n        var toks = (Console.ReadLine() ?? "").Trim()\n            .Split(new[]{\' \',\'\\t\'}, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);\n        N = int.Parse(toks[0]);\n        MU = double.Parse(toks[1], CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);\n\n        var rv = new double[N+1][];\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N; i++)\n            rv[i] = (Console.ReadLine() ?? "").Trim()\n                .Split(new[]{\' \',\'\\t\'}, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries)\n                .Select(s => double.Parse(s, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)).ToArray();\n\n        C = new double[N+1, N+1];\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N; i++)\n            for (int j = 0; j <= N; j++)\n                if (i != j) C[i,j] = DV(rv[i], rv[j]);\n\n        int[] ans;\n        if (N == 1) ans = new[]{0};\n        else if (N <= 20) ans = HK();\n        else ans = Large();\n\n        Console.WriteLine(string.Join(" ", ans));\n    }\n\n    static double SMA(double[] r) {\n        double d = Math.Sqrt(r[0]*r[0]+r[1]*r[1]+r[2]*r[2]);\n        double v2 = r[3]*r[3]+r[4]*r[4]+r[5]*r[5];\n        double e = 0.5*v2 - MU/d;\n        return e < 0 ? -MU/(2*e) : -1;\n    }\n    static double Inc(double[] r) {\n        double hx=r[1]*r[5]-r[2]*r[4],hy=r[2]*r[3]-r[0]*r[5],hz=r[0]*r[4]-r[1]*r[3];\n        double h=Math.Sqrt(hx*hx+hy*hy+hz*hz);\n        return h>1e-10 ? Math.Acos(Math.Max(-1.0,Math.Min(1.0,hz/h))) : 0;\n    }\n    static double DV(double[] r1, double[] r2) {\n        double a1=SMA(r1), a2=SMA(r2);\n        if (a1<=0||a2<=0) {\n            double dx=r2[3]-r1[3],dy=r2[4]-r1[4],dz=r2[5]-r1[5];\n            return Math.Sqrt(dx*dx+dy*dy+dz*dz);\n        }\n        double di=Math.Abs(Inc(r1)-Inc(r2));\n        double aT=(a1+a2)/2, vc1=Math.Sqrt(MU/a1), vc2=Math.Sqrt(MU/a2);\n        double vT1=Math.Sqrt(MU*(2/a1-1/aT)), vT2=Math.Sqrt(MU*(2/a2-1/aT));\n        if (a1<=a2)\n            return Math.Abs(vT1-vc1)+Math.Sqrt(vc2*vc2+vT2*vT2-2*vc2*vT2*Math.Cos(di));\n        return Math.Sqrt(vc1*vc1+vT1*vT1-2*vc1*vT1*Math.Cos(di))+Math.Abs(vT2-vc2);\n    }\n\n    // Edge cost: indices are station-0-indexed; -1=depot, "after last"=-2 is handled by return 0\n    static double Ec(int a, int b) {\n        if (b < 0) return 0;\n        return C[a < 0 ? 0 : a+1, b+1];\n    }\n    static double TC(int[] t) {\n        double c = Ec(-1, t[0]);\n        for (int i = 1; i < t.Length; i++) c += Ec(t[i-1], t[i]);\n        return c;\n    }\n\n    static int[] HK() {\n        int full = 1<<N;\n        double[] dp = new double[full*N];\n        short[] par = new short[full*N];\n        for (int i = 0; i < dp.Length; i++) { dp[i] = double.MaxValue/2; par[i] = -1; }\n        for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) dp[(1<<i)*N+i] = C[0,i+1];\n        for (int mask = 1; mask < full; mask++) {\n            int mN = mask*N;\n            for (int last = 0; last < N; last++) {\n                if ((mask&(1<<last))==0) continue;\n                double d = dp[mN+last];\n                if (d >= double.MaxValue/2) continue;\n                for (int nxt = 0; nxt < N; nxt++) {\n                    if ((mask&(1<<nxt))!=0) continue;\n                    int nm = mask|(1<<nxt);\n                    double nd = d+C[last+1,nxt+1];\n                    int idx = nm*N+nxt;\n                    if (nd<dp[idx]){dp[idx]=nd;par[idx]=(short)last;}\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        int fM=full-1, fB=fM*N, best=0;\n        for (int i=1;i<N;i++) if (dp[fB+i]<dp[fB+best]) best=i;\n        var path = new int[N];\n        int cur=best, msk=fM;\n        for (int s=N-1;s>=0;s--) {\n            path[s]=cur;\n            short p=par[msk*N+cur];\n            msk^=(1<<cur);\n            cur=p;\n        }\n        return path;\n    }\n\n    static int[] Greedy(int first) {\n        var vis = new bool[N];\n        var t = new int[N];\n        int cur=first, s0=0;\n        if (first>=0){t[0]=first;vis[first]=true;s0=1;}\n        for (int s=s0;s<N;s++) {\n            double best=double.MaxValue;int bj=0;\n            for (int j=0;j<N;j++)\n                if (!vis[j]){double c=Ec(cur,j);if(c<best){best=c;bj=j;}}\n            t[s]=bj;vis[bj]=true;cur=bj;\n        }\n        return t;\n    }\n\n    static void TwoOpt(int[] t) {\n        bool imp=true;\n        while(imp){\n            imp=false;\n            for (int i=0;i<N-1;i++)\n            for (int j=i+2;j<N;j++) {\n                int a=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,b=t[i],c=t[j],d=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n                if (Ec(a,c)+Ec(b,d)<Ec(a,b)+Ec(c,d)-1e-10)\n                    {Array.Reverse(t,i,j-i+1);imp=true;}\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    static void OrOpt(int[] t, int sl) { // sl = segment length\n        bool imp=true;\n        while(imp){\n            imp=false;\n            for (int i=0;i<=N-sl;i++) {\n                int prev=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,fs=t[i],ls=t[i+sl-1],aft=(i+sl<N)?t[i+sl]:-1;\n                double gR=Ec(prev,fs)+Ec(ls,aft)-Ec(prev,aft);\n                if (gR<=1e-10) continue;\n                int bj=int.MinValue;double bg=1e-10;\n                for (int j=-1;j<N;j++) {\n                    if (j>=i-1&&j<i+sl) continue;\n                    int A=j<0?-1:t[j],B=j+1<N?t[j+1]:-1;\n                    double gI=Ec(A,B)-Ec(A,fs)-Ec(ls,B);\n                    if (gR+gI>bg){bg=gR+gI;bj=j;}\n                }\n                if (bj>int.MinValue){ApplySeg(t,i,sl,bj);imp=true;break;}\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    static void ApplySeg(int[] t, int from, int sl, int ia) { // ia=insertAfter\n        var seg=new int[sl];\n        Array.Copy(t,from,seg,0,sl);\n        if (ia<from) {\n            for (int k=from-1;k>=ia+1;k--) t[k+sl]=t[k];\n            for (int k=0;k<sl;k++) t[ia+1+k]=seg[k];\n        } else { // ia>=from+sl\n            for (int k=from;k<=ia-sl;k++) t[k]=t[k+sl];\n            for (int k=0;k<sl;k++) t[ia-sl+1+k]=seg[k];\n        }\n    }\n\n    // SA helpers\n    static double DDeltaSwap(int[] t, int i, int j) {\n        if (i>j){int tmp=i;i=j;j=tmp;}\n        if (j==i+1){\n            int a=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,b=t[i],c=t[j],d=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n            return Ec(a,c)+Ec(c,b)+Ec(b,d)-Ec(a,b)-Ec(b,c)-Ec(c,d);\n        }\n        int pi=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,ni=t[i+1],pj=t[j-1],nj=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n        return Ec(pi,t[j])+Ec(t[j],ni)+Ec(pj,t[i])+Ec(t[i],nj)\n             - Ec(pi,t[i])-Ec(t[i],ni)-Ec(pj,t[j])-Ec(t[j],nj);\n    }\n    static double DDelta2Opt(int[] t, int i, int j) {\n        int a=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,b=t[i],c=t[j],d=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n        return Ec(a,c)+Ec(b,d)-Ec(a,b)-Ec(c,d);\n    }\n    static double DDeltaReloc(int[] t, int from, int ia) {\n        int nd=t[from],pv=(from>0)?t[from-1]:-1,nx=(from<N-1)?t[from+1]:-1;\n        double gR=Ec(pv,nd)+Ec(nd,nx)-Ec(pv,nx);\n        int A=ia<0?-1:t[ia],B=ia+1<N?t[ia+1]:-1;\n        return -(gR+Ec(A,B)-Ec(A,nd)-Ec(nd,B));\n    }\n\n    static void SA(int[] tour, ref double best, long ms) {\n        if (ms<=0) return;\n        var cur=(int[])tour.Clone();\n        double cc=best;\n        var rng=new Random(42);\n        double T0=best/N*0.5,Tf=T0*1e-6;\n        if (T0<=0)T0=0.01;\n        long t0=Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds,t1=t0+ms;\n        while(true){\n            long tnow=Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds;\n            if (tnow>=t1) break;\n            double prog=Math.Min(1,(double)(tnow-t0)/ms);\n            double T=T0*Math.Pow(Tf/T0,prog);\n            for (int k=0;k<10000;k++) {\n                int mt=rng.Next(3),a=rng.Next(N),b;\n                double dlt;\n                if (mt==0){\n                    b=rng.Next(N);if(b==a)continue;\n                    dlt=DDeltaSwap(cur,a,b);\n                }else if(mt==1){\n                    b=rng.Next(N);if(b==a)continue;\n                    if(a>b){int tmp=a;a=b;b=tmp;}\n                    dlt=DDelta2Opt(cur,a,b);\n                }else{\n                    b=rng.Next(N+1)-1;if(b==a-1||b==a)continue;\n                    dlt=DDeltaReloc(cur,a,b);\n                }\n                if (dlt<=0||rng.NextDouble()<Math.Exp(-dlt/T)){\n                    if(mt==0){int tmp=cur[a];cur[a]=cur[b];cur[b]=tmp;}\n                    else if(mt==1)Array.Reverse(cur,a,b-a+1);\n                    else ApplySeg(cur,a,1,b);\n                    cc+=dlt;\n                    if(cc<best-1e-10){best=cc;Array.Copy(cur,tour,N);}\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    static int[] Large() {\n        int np=Math.Min(64,Environment.ProcessorCount);\n        int ns=Math.Min(np+1,N+1);\n        var res=new (int[] t, double c)[ns];\n        Parallel.For(0,ns,new ParallelOptions{MaxDegreeOfParallelism=np},idx=>{\n            int s=idx==0?-1:(idx-1)%N;\n            var t=Greedy(s);\n            TwoOpt(t);\n            OrOpt(t,1);OrOpt(t,2);OrOpt(t,3);\n            TwoOpt(t);\n            res[idx]=(t,TC(t));\n        });\n        int bi=0;\n        for(int i=1;i<ns;i++)if(res[i].c<res[bi].c)bi=i;\n        var bst=res[bi].t;\n        double bc=res[bi].c;\n        long rem=270000-Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds;\n        if(rem>2000)SA(bst,ref bc,rem);\n        return bst;\n    }\n}\n```\n\nLet me trace through the
