If a1 <= a2 (which is true when equal): burn1 = 0, burn2 = 2*vc2*sin(di/2). ✓\n\nOkay, I\'m satisfied. Let me write the final code. This time I\'ll write it all out carefully.\n\nActually, I want to add one more optimization to the large-scale solver: after the parallel phase (multiple greedy+2opt+oropt starts), run multiple SA instances in parallel for the remaining time, and pick the best result at the end.\n\nThis would utilize the 64 cores more effectively. Let me adjust:\n\n```csharp\nstatic int[] Large() {\n    int cores = Math.Min(64, Environment.ProcessorCount);\n    int ns = Math.Min(cores+1, N+1);\n    var greedyRes = new (int[] t, double c)[ns];\n    Parallel.For(0, ns, ..., idx => {\n        // Greedy + local search\n        greedyRes[idx] = ...;\n    });\n    \n    // Find global best from greedy phase\n    int bi = best from greedyRes;\n    var bestTour = ...\n    double bestCost = ...\n    \n    long rem = 270000 - Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds;\n    if (rem > 5000) {\n        // Run parallel SA from each of the top k solutions\n        int k = Math.Min(cores, ns);\n        var saResults = new (int[] t, double c)[k];\n        // Initialize saResults with top k greedy results\n        ...\n        \n        Parallel.For(0, k, ..., idx => {\n            var t = (int[])saResults[idx].t.Clone();\n            double c = saResults[idx].c;\n            SA(t, ref c, rem - 2000);\n            saResults[idx] = (t, c);\n        });\n        \n        // Pick best SA result\n        int bi2 = best from saResults;\n        if (saResults[bi2].c < bestCost) {\n            bestTour = saResults[bi2].t;\n            bestCost = saResults[bi2].c;\n        }\n    } else if (rem > 2000) {\n        SA(bestTour, ref bestCost, rem - 1000);\n    }\n    \n    return bestTour;\n}\n```\n\nThis is more complex. Let me decide whether to implement it.\n\nFor the problem at hand:\n- Greedy + 2opt + oropt: very fast (< 30 seconds for N=100 with 64 cores)\n- SA: can run for the remaining time\n\nIf SA runs on a single thread for 4 minutes for N=100: 10M iterations/sec * 240 seconds = 2.4B iterations. That\'s a LOT of SA iterations. Should give excellent results.\n\nBut with 64 cores, we could do 64x more SA iterations. However, parallel SA from different starting points with no communication is called "embarrassingly parallel SA". The best result from all 64 threads is then the final answer.\n\nLet me implement this:\n\n```csharp\nstatic int[] Large() {\n    int cores = Math.Min(64, Environment.ProcessorCount);\n    int ns = Math.Min(cores, N+1);\n    var res = new (int[] t, double c)[ns];\n    \n    // Phase 1: Greedy + local search (parallel)\n    Parallel.For(0, ns, new ParallelOptions{MaxDegreeOfParallelism=cores}, idx => {\n        int s = idx == 0 ? -1 : (idx-1) % N;\n        var t = Greedy(s);\n        TwoOpt(t);\n        OrOpt(t,1); OrOpt(t,2); OrOpt(t,3);\n        TwoOpt(t);\n        res[idx] = (t, TC(t));\n    });\n    \n    // Phase 2: Parallel SA from each starting point\n    long rem = 270000 - Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds;\n    if (rem > 5000) {\n        var saRes = new (int[] t, double c)[ns];\n        for (int i = 0; i < ns; i++) saRes[i] = res[i];\n        \n        Parallel.For(0, ns, new ParallelOptions{MaxDegreeOfParallelism=cores}, idx => {\n            var t = (int[])saRes[idx].t.Clone();\n            double c = saRes[idx].c;\n            SA_Seeded(t, ref c, rem - 1000, 42 + idx);\n            saRes[idx] = (t, c);\n        });\n        \n        // Find overall best\n        int bi = 0;\n        for (int i = 1; i < ns; i++) if (saRes[i].c < saRes[bi].c) bi = i;\n        return saRes[bi].t;\n    }\n    \n    // Find best greedy result\n    int bi2 = 0;\n    for (int i = 1; i < ns; i++) if (res[i].c < res[bi2].c) bi2 = i;\n    var bst = res[bi2].t;\n    double bc = res[bi2].c;\n    if (rem > 2000) SA_Seeded(bst, ref bc, rem - 1000, 42);\n    return bst;\n}\n```\n\nThis utilizes all 64 cores for both the greedy phase and the SA phase, which should give much better results for large N.\n\nI\'ll need to modify SA to take a seed:\n```csharp\nstatic void SA_Seeded(int[] tour, ref double best, long ms, int seed) {\n    // Same as SA but with given random seed\n    if (ms <= 0) return;\n    var cur = (int[])tour.Clone();\n    double cc = best;\n    var rng = new Random(seed);\n    // ...\n}\n```\n\nOkay let me finalize with this parallel SA approach. This should give the best results.\n\nNow let me write the actual complete code:\n\nSome things to keep in mind:\n1. The `ApplySeg` function with segLen=1 and insertAfter=-1 through N-1: works correctly as I analyzed.\n2. The SA applies random moves: swap, 2-opt, relocate. All have O(1) delta computation and O(N) worst-case application.\n3. For the parallel SA, each thread uses its own Random with different seed, so they explore different parts of the solution space.\n\nLet me check if there are any issues with the parallel SA approach:\n- Each thread has its own copy of the tour array and its own Random\n- No shared state between SA threads (except reading from C, which is read-only)\n- At the end, we collect all results and pick the best\n\nThis is embarrassingly parallel and correct. ✓\n\nOne potential issue: for N=21 to N=100, we use LargeScale(). For N=21, the greedy + 2opt + oropt should give good results, and SA will refine it.\n\nOkay, here\'s my truly final code. Let me write it cleanly:\n\nActually, I also want to handle the edge case where HeldKarp might run into memory issues for N=20. The dp array is 2^20 * 20 * 8 = 167MB and par is 42MB. Total 209MB. With 127GB RAM, no issue.\n\nFor N>20, the LargeScale function handles it.\n\nLet me now write the final code. I\'ll be concise but include all the necessary functionality.\n\nFinal considerations:\n1. Error handling: What if N=0? Not in spec, skip.\n2. What if a station has the same orbital state as the starting position? DV=0, handled correctly.\n3. What if N=1 with LargeScale? Won\'t happen (N<=20 uses HK, N=1 returns {0}).\n\nOkay, writing the code now:\n\nHere it is:\n\n```csharp\nusing System;\nusing System.Linq;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\nusing System.Diagnostics;\nusing System.Globalization;\n\nclass Program {\n    static double MU;\n    static int N;\n    static double[,] C;\n    static readonly Stopwatch Sw = Stopwatch.StartNew();\n    const long TimeLimitMs = 270000;\n\n    static void Main() {\n        // --- Input Parsing ---\n        string line1 = Console.ReadLine() ?? "";\n        var p1 = line1.Trim().Split(new[]{\' \',\'\\t\'}, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);\n        N = int.Parse(p1[0]);\n        MU = double.Parse(p1[1], CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);\n\n        double[][] rv = new double[N+1][];\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N; i++) {\n            string ln = Console.ReadLine() ?? "";\n            rv[i] = ln.Trim().Split(new[]{\' \',\'\\t\'}, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries)\n                      .Select(s => double.Parse(s, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)).ToArray();\n        }\n\n        // --- Cost Matrix ---\n        C = new double[N+1, N+1];\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N; i++)\n            for (int j = 0; j <= N; j++)\n                if (i != j) C[i, j] = DV(rv[i], rv[j]);\n\n        // --- Solve ---\n        int[] ans;\n        if (N == 1) ans = new[]{0};\n        else if (N <= 20) ans = HK();\n        else ans = Large();\n\n        Console.WriteLine(string.Join(" ", ans));\n    }\n\n    // ============================================================\n    // PHYSICS\n    // ============================================================\n    static double SMA(double[] r) {\n        double mag = Math.Sqrt(r[0]*r[0]+r[1]*r[1]+r[2]*r[2]);\n        double v2 = r[3]*r[3]+r[4]*r[4]+r[5]*r[5];\n        double E = 0.5*v2 - MU/mag;\n        return E < 0 ? -MU/(2*E) : -1;\n    }\n    static double Inc(double[] r) {\n        double hx=r[1]*r[5]-r[2]*r[4], hy=r[2]*r[3]-r[0]*r[5], hz=r[0]*r[4]-r[1]*r[3];\n        double h = Math.Sqrt(hx*hx+hy*hy+hz*hz);\n        return h > 1e-10 ? Math.Acos(Math.Max(-1.0, Math.Min(1.0, hz/h))) : 0.0;\n    }\n    static double DV(double[] r1, double[] r2) {\n        double a1 = SMA(r1), a2 = SMA(r2);\n        if (a1 <= 0 || a2 <= 0) {\n            // Fallback: delta-v magnitude\n            double dx=r2[3]-r1[3], dy=r2[4]-r1[4], dz=r2[5]-r1[5];\n            return Math.Sqrt(dx*dx+dy*dy+dz*dz);\n        }\n        double di = Math.Abs(Inc(r1) - Inc(r2));\n        double aT = (a1+a2)*0.5;\n        double vc1 = Math.Sqrt(MU/a1), vc2 = Math.Sqrt(MU/a2);\n        double vT1 = Math.Sqrt(MU*(2.0/a1-1.0/aT));\n        double vT2 = Math.Sqrt(MU*(2.0/a2-1.0/aT));\n        // Transfer from a1 to a2:\n        // If a1 < a2: source is at periapsis, do plane change at apoapsis (a2)\n        // If a1 > a2: source is at apoapsis (higher SMA), do plane change there\n        if (a1 <= a2) {\n            double dv1 = Math.Abs(vT1 - vc1);\n            double dv2 = Math.Sqrt(vc2*vc2 + vT2*vT2 - 2*vc2*vT2*Math.Cos(di));\n            return dv1 + dv2;\n        } else {\n            double dv1 = Math.Sqrt(vc1*vc1 + vT1*vT1 - 2*vc1*vT1*Math.Cos(di));\n            double dv2 = Math.Abs(vT2 - vc2);\n            return dv1 + dv2;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ============================================================\n    // COST HELPERS\n    // ============================================================\n    static double Ec(int a, int b) { // station indices, -1=depot\n        if (b < 0) return 0;\n        return C[a < 0 ? 0 : a+1, b+1];\n    }\n    static double TC(int[] t) {\n        double c = Ec(-1, t[0]);\n        for (int i = 1; i < t.Length; i++) c += Ec(t[i-1], t[i]);\n        return c;\n    }\n\n    // ============================================================\n    // HELD-KARP (Exact, N <= 20)\n    // ============================================================\n    static int[] HK() {\n        int full = 1 << N;\n        double[] dp = new double[full*N];\n        short[] par = new short[full*N];\n        for (int i = 0; i < dp.Length; i++) { dp[i] = double.MaxValue/2; par[i] = -1; }\n        for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) dp[(1<<i)*N+i] = C[0, i+1];\n        for (int mask = 1; mask < full; mask++) {\n            int mN = mask*N;\n            for (int last = 0; last < N; last++) {\n                if ((mask & (1<<last)) == 0) continue;\n                double d = dp[mN+last];\n                if (d >= double.MaxValue/2) continue;\n                for (int nxt = 0; nxt < N; nxt++) {\n                    if ((mask & (1<<nxt)) != 0) continue;\n                    double nd = d + C[last+1, nxt+1];\n                    int idx = (mask|(1<<nxt))*N+nxt;\n                    if (nd < dp[idx]) { dp[idx]=nd; par[idx]=(short)last; }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        int fM = full-1, fB = fM*N, best = 0;\n        for (int i = 1; i < N; i++) if (dp[fB+i] < dp[fB+best]) best = i;\n        int[] path = new int[N];\n        int cur = best, msk = fM;\n        for (int s = N-1; s >= 0; s--) {\n            path[s] = cur;\n            int p = par[msk*N+cur];\n            msk ^= (1<<cur);\n            cur = p;\n        }\n        return path;\n    }\n\n    // ============================================================\n    // HEURISTICS\n    // ============================================================\n    static int[] Greedy(int first) { // first=-1: from depot\n        bool[] vis = new bool[N];\n        int[] t = new int[N];\n        int cur = first, s0 = 0;\n        if (first >= 0) { t[0]=first; vis[first]=true; s0=1; }\n        for (int s = s0; s < N; s++) {\n            double best = double.MaxValue; int bj = 0;\n            for (int j = 0; j < N; j++)\n                if (!vis[j]) { double c=Ec(cur,j); if(c<best){best=c;bj=j;} }\n            t[s]=bj; vis[bj]=true; cur=bj;\n        }\n        return t;\n    }\n\n    static void TwoOpt(int[] t) {\n        bool imp = true;\n        while (imp) {\n            imp = false;\n            for (int i = 0; i < N-1; i++)\n                for (int j = i+2; j < N; j++) {\n                    int a=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1, b=t[i], c=t[j], d=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n                    if (Ec(a,c)+Ec(b,d) < Ec(a,b)+Ec(c,d)-1e-10)\n                        { Array.Reverse(t,i,j-i+1); imp=true; }\n                }\n        }\n    }\n\n    static void OrOpt(int[] t, int sl) {\n        bool imp = true;\n        while (imp) {\n            imp = false;\n            for (int i = 0; i <= N-sl; i++) {\n                int prev=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1, fs=t[i], ls=t[i+sl-1], aft=(i+sl<N)?t[i+sl]:-1;\n                double gR = Ec(prev,fs)+Ec(ls,aft)-Ec(prev,aft);\n                if (gR <= 1e-10) continue;\n                int bj = int.MinValue; double bg = 1e-10;\n                for (int j = -1; j < N; j++) {\n                    if (j >= i-1 && j < i+sl) continue;\n                    int A=j<0?-1:t[j], B=j+1<N?t[j+1]:-1;\n                    double g = gR + Ec(A,B) - Ec(A,fs) - Ec(ls,B);\n                    if (g > bg) { bg=g; bj=j; }\n                }\n                if (bj > int.MinValue) { ApplySeg(t,i,sl,bj); imp=true; break; }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    static void ApplySeg(int[] t, int from, int sl, int ia) {\n        int[] seg = new int[sl];\n        Array.Copy(t, from, seg, 0, sl);\n        if (ia < from) {\n            for (int k = from-1; k >= ia+1; k--) t[k+sl]=t[k];\n            for (int k = 0; k < sl; k++) t[ia+1+k]=seg[k];\n        } else {\n            for (int k = from; k <= ia-sl; k++) t[k]=t[k+sl];\n            for (int k = 0; k < sl; k++) t[ia-sl+1+k]=seg[k];\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ============================================================\n    // SIMULATED ANNEALING\n    // ============================================================\n    static double DS(int[] t, int i, int j) { // delta for swap\n        if (i>j){int tmp=i;i=j;j=tmp;}\n        if (j==i+1){\n            int a=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,b=t[i],c=t[j],d=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n            return Ec(a,c)+Ec(c,b)+Ec(b,d)-Ec(a,b)-Ec(b,c)-Ec(c,d);\n        }\n        int pi=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,ni=t[i+1],pj=t[j-1],nj=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n        return Ec(pi,t[j])+Ec(t[j],ni)+Ec(pj,t[i])+Ec(t[i],nj)\n             - Ec(pi,t[i])-Ec(t[i],ni)-Ec(pj,t[j])-Ec(t[j],nj);\n    }\n    static double D2(int[] t, int i, int j) { // delta for 2-opt\n        int a=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,b=t[i],c=t[j],d=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n        return Ec(a,c)+Ec(b,d)-Ec(a,b)-Ec(c,d);\n    }\n    static double DR(int[] t, int from, int ia) { // delta for relocate\n        int nd=t[from],pv=(from>0)?t[from-1]:-1,nx=(from<N-1)?t[from+1]:-1;\n        double gR=Ec(pv,nd)+Ec(nd,nx)-Ec(pv,nx);\n        int A=ia<0?-1:t[ia],B=ia+1<N?t[ia+1]:-1;\n        return -(gR+Ec(A,B)-Ec(A,nd)-Ec(nd,B));\n    }\n\n    static void SA(int[] tour, ref double best, long ms, int seed=42) {\n        if (ms <= 0) return;\n        int[] cur = (int[])tour.Clone();\n        double cc = best;\n        Random rng = new Random(seed);\n        double T0 = best/N*0.5, Tf = T0*1e-5;\n        if (T0 <= 1e-9) T0 = 0.01;\n        long t0 = Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds, t1 = t0+ms;\n        while (true) {\n            long tn = Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds;\n            if (tn >= t1) break;\n            double prog = Math.Min(1.0,(double)(tn-t0)/ms);\n            double T = T0*Math.Pow(Tf/T0,prog);\n            if (T < Tf) T = Tf;\n            for (int k = 0; k < 10000; k++) {\n                int mt = rng.Next(3), a = rng.Next(N), b;\n                double d;\n                if (mt==0) {\n                    b=rng.Next(N); if(b==a) continue;\n                    d=DS(cur,a,b);\n                } else if (mt==1) {\n                    b=rng.Next(N); if(b==a) continue;\n                    if(a>b){int tmp=a;a=b;b=tmp;}\n                    d=D2(cur,a,b);\n                } else {\n                    b=rng.Next(N+1)-1;\n                    if(b==a-1||b==a) continue;\n                    d=DR(cur,a,b);\n                }\n                if (d<=0||rng.NextDouble()<Math.Exp(-d/T)) {\n                    if (mt==0){int tmp=cur[a];cur[a]=cur[b];cur[b]=tmp;}\n                    else if (mt==1) Array.Reverse(cur,a,b-a+1);\n                    else ApplySeg(cur,a,1,b);\n                    cc+=d;\n                    if (cc<best-1e-10){best=cc;Array.Copy(cur,tour,N);}\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ============================================================\n    // LARGE SCALE SOLVER\n    // ============================================================\n    static int[] Large() {\n        int cores = Math.Min(64, Environment.ProcessorCount);\n        int ns = Math.Min(cores, N+1);\n        (int[] t, double c)[] res = new (int[], double)[ns];\n        Parallel.For(0, ns, new ParallelOptions{MaxDegreeOfParallelism=cores}, idx => {\n            int s = idx == 0 ? -1 : (idx-1)%N;\n            int[] t = Greedy(s);\n            TwoOpt(t);\n            OrOpt(t,1); OrOpt(t,2); OrOpt(t,3);\n            TwoOpt(t);\n            res[idx] = (t, TC(t));\n        });\n        \n        long rem = TimeLimitMs - Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds;\n        if (rem > 5000) {\n            // Parallel SA\n            (int[] t, double c)[] saRes = new (int[], double)[ns];\n            for (int i = 0; i < ns; i++) saRes[i] = ((int[])res[i].t.Clone(), res[i].c);\n            Parallel.For(0, ns, new ParallelOptions{MaxDegreeOfParallelism=cores}, idx => {\n                var tt = saRes[idx].t;\n                var cc = saRes[idx].c;\n                SA(tt, ref cc, rem - 2000, 42+idx*7);\n                saRes[idx] = (tt, cc);\n            });\n            int bi = 0;\n            for (int i = 1; i < ns; i++) if (saRes[i].c < saRes[bi].c) bi = i;\n            return saRes[bi].t;\n        }\n        \n        int bi2 = 0;\n        for (int i = 1; i < ns; i++) if (res[i].c < res[bi2].c) bi2 = i;\n        var bst = res[bi2].t;\n        double bc = res[bi2].c;\n        if (rem > 2000) SA(bst, ref bc, rem-1000);\n        return bst;\n    }\n}\n```\n\nWait, I think there might be an issue with the Parallel.For for SA: each thread reads and writes to `saRes[idx]`, and the struct `(int[], double)` is being assigned. Since each thread accesses a different index, there\'s no contention. ✓\n\nBut the `SA` function modifies `tour` in place (via `Array.Copy`). Since `tour = saRes[idx].t` (a reference to the array), this should work correctly.\n\nActually, let me trace this:\n- `var tt = saRes[idx].t;` - tt is a reference to the array in saRes[idx].t\n- `var cc = saRes[idx].c;` - cc is a copy of the double\n- `SA(tt, ref cc, ...)` - SA modifies tt in place and updates cc via ref\n- `saRes[idx] = (tt, cc)` - updates the tuple (but tt is already the same array reference)\n\nSince saRes[idx].t = tt (same array reference), the assignment `saRes[idx] = (tt, cc)` mainly updates the cost. The array is modified in place by SA. ✓\n\nBut wait: when I do `for (int i = 0; i < ns; i++) saRes[i] = ((int[])res[i].t.Clone(), res[i].c)`, I create clones of the greedy tours. Each SA thread then gets its own clone to work with. ✓\n\nOkay, the parallel SA approach is correct.\n\nOne more thing: in the DS function for swap, when j == i+1 (adjacent), I need to check that j < N to access t[j]. Since j = i+1 and we\'re called with a,b from the SA (random indices), i+1 could be <= N-1. Let me check:\n\n- In SA: `if(b==a)continue;` ensures a ≠ b.\n- After sorting i <= j, if j == i+1: both i and j are valid indices (0 <= i < j <= N-1).\n- Accessing t[j] = t[i+1]: valid since j <= N-1. ✓\n- Accessing t[j+1] = t[j+1] only when j < N-1: guarded by `(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1`. ✓\n\nFor the non-adjacent case (j > i+1):\n- `ni=t[i+1]`: i+1 <= j-1 < j <= N-1, so i+1 < N. ✓\n- `pj=t[j-1]`: j-1 >= i+1 >= 1, so j-1 >= 0. ✓\n\nGreat, all accesses are valid.\n\nLet me also verify D2 (2-opt delta):\n- `a=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1, b=t[i], c=t[j], d=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1`\n- a: valid (either t[i-1] with i>0 or -1)\n- b=t[i]: i >= 0, i < j < N, so valid\n- c=t[j]: j <= N-1, valid\n- d: valid\n✓\n\nAnd DR (relocate delta):\n- `nd=t[from]`: from in [0,N-1]. ✓\n- `pv=(from>0)?t[from-1]:-1`: valid. ✓\n- `nx=(from<N-1)?t[from+1]:-1`: valid. ✓\n- `A=ia<0?-1:t[ia]`: ia in [-1, N-1]. If ia >= 0, t[ia] is valid. ✓\n- `B=ia+1<N?t[ia+1]:-1`: if ia < N-1, t[ia+1] is valid. ✓\n\nBut wait: if ia > from, then t[ia] might actually point to an element that\'s AFTER the from position in the original array. After we remove t[from], t[ia] shifts. But as I analyzed before, the gain formula is still correct because we\'re computing gains in terms of nodes (not positions). ✓\n\nBut there\'s one more edge case: when from=0 and ia=-1, which would mean removing the first element and inserting before the first element (same position). This is excluded by `if(b==a-1||b==a)` in SA: b=-1, a=0, b==a-1=-1 ✓. Excluded.\n\nWhen from=N-1 and ia=N-2 (=from-1), also excluded by `b==a-1`. ✓\n\nWhen from=N-1 and ia=N-1 (same position), excluded by `b==a`. ✓\n\nOkay, I\'m satisfied. Let me finalize the code and make sure it compiles.\n\nActually, one thing I realized: in the DR function, I access `t[ia]` with ia=N-1 (the last element). And then B=ia+1<N? No, ia+1=N, so B=-1. Then I access Ec(A,B)=Ec(t[N-1],-1)=0 and Ec(nd,B)=Ec(t[from],-1)=0. So the gain for relocating to after the last element correctly computes. ✓\n\nAlso in DR, I access `t[ia+1]` only when `ia+1 < N`. So if ia=N-1, I don\'t access t[N] (which would be out of bounds). ✓\n\nOne potential issue: `t[ia]` when `ia > from` gives the element at position ia in the ORIGINAL array. But after removing t[from], the element that was at ia is now at ia-1. However, for the purpose of computing the gain delta, we work with node identities (values), not positions, and the formula is correct. ✓\n\nBut when actually applying the move with ApplySeg(cur, a, 1, b) where b = ia = insertAfter:\n- `from=a, ia=b`\n- If ia < from: shift t[ia+1..from-1] right, place t[from] at t[ia+1]\n- If ia > from: shift t[from+1..ia] left, place t[from] at t[ia]\n\nLet me verify with example: t=[0,1,2,3,4], from=1 (t[1]=1), ia=3 (t[3]=3):\n- Segment [1] at position 1, insert after position 3 (t[3]=3)\n- ia=3 > from=1: shift left from 2 to 3-1=2 (k from 1 to 2: t[1]=t[2]=2, t[2]=t[3]=3)\n  Wait, loop: `for k=from to ia-sl=2: t[k]=t[k+sl]` where sl=1:\n  k=1: t[1]=t[2]=2; k=2: t[2]=t[3]=3\n  Then t[ia-sl+1]=t[3]=seg[0]=1\n  Result: [0,2,3,1,4] ✓\n\nGain computation for this move (node=1, from=1, ia=3):\n- prev=t[0]=0, next=t[2]=2\n- gainR = Ec(0,1)+Ec(1,2)-Ec(0,2)\n- A=t[3]=3, B=t[4]=4\n- gainI = Ec(3,4)-Ec(3,1)-Ec(1,4)\n- delta = -(gainR+gainI) = Ec(0,2)+Ec(3,1)+Ec(1,4)-Ec(0,1)-Ec(1,2)-Ec(3,4)\n\nVerify directly:\n- Original: depot->0->1->2->3->4: cost includes Ec(0,1)+Ec(1,2)+Ec(3,4) among others\n- After move: depot->0->2->3->1->4: cost includes Ec(0,2)+Ec(3,1)+Ec(1,4)\n- Delta = (Ec(0,2)+Ec(3,1)+Ec(1,4)) - (Ec(0,1)+Ec(1,2)+Ec(3,4)) ✓\n\nGreat, the formula matches.\n\nOkay let me now write the truly final code. I\'ll just write it out:\n\nI need to handle one edge case in ApplySeg: when `ia >= from + sl`, the loop `for k=from to ia-sl: t[k]=t[k+sl]`. If ia=from+sl (insert immediately after segment), then:\n- loop: k from from to ia-sl=from: t[from]=t[from+sl]\n- Then t[ia-sl+1]=t[from+1]=seg[0]\n\nWait, that gives t[from]=t[from+sl] (shift one element left by sl), then t[from+1]=seg[0]. For sl=1: t[from]=t[from+1], then t[from+1]=node. This effectively swaps t[from] and t[from+1], which is a swap of adjacent elements. ✓\n\nBut for ia=from+sl, this is the same as inserting right after the segment. Let me make it clean and complete:\n\nNote: I need to handle the special case where N=2 and we\'re using Large() incorrectly. But since N<=20 uses HK(), N=2 is handled by HK(). ✓\n\nAlso, for N=1 (though specs say minimum 2): output "0". Handled separately.\n\nFinal note on memory: for N=20 with double dp and short par:\n- dp: 2^20 * 20 * 8 = 167,772,160 bytes ≈ 160 MB\n- par: 2^20 * 20 * 2 = 41,943,040 bytes ≈ 40 MB\n- Total: ~200 MB. I\'ll keep it under 300 lines for clarity:\n\n```csharp\nusing System;\nusing System.Linq;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\nusing System.Diagnostics;\nusing System.Globalization;\n\nclass Program {\n    static double MU;\n    static int N;\n    static double[,] C;\n    static readonly Stopwatch Sw = Stopwatch.StartNew();\n\n    static void Main() {\n        // Parse input\n        string[] f = (Console.ReadLine() ?? "").Trim()\n            .Split(new[]{\' \',\'\\t\'}, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);\n        N = int.Parse(f[0]);\n        MU = double.Parse(f[1], CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);\n        double[][] rv = new double[N+1][];\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N; i++)\n            rv[i] = (Console.ReadLine() ?? "").Trim()\n                .Split(new[]{\' \',\'\\t\'}, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries)\n                .Select(s => double.Parse(s, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)).ToArray();\n        // Build cost matrix\n        C = new double[N+1, N+1];\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N; i++)\n            for (int j = 0; j <= N; j++)\n                if (i != j) C[i,j] = DV(rv[i], rv[j]);\n        // Solve and output\n        int[] ans = N == 1 ? new[]{0} : N <= 20 ? HK() : Large();\n        Console.WriteLine(string.Join(" ", ans));\n    }\n\n    // === Physics ===\n    static double SMA(double[] r) {\n        double mag = Math.Sqrt(r[0]*r[0]+r[1]*r[1]+r[2]*r[2]);\n        double E = 0.5*(r[3]*r[3]+r[4]*r[4]+r[5]*r[5]) - MU/mag;\n        return E < 0 ? -MU/(2*E) : -1;\n    }\n    static double Inc(double[] r) {\n        double hx=r[1]*r[5]-r[2]*r[4],hy=r[2]*r[3]-r[0]*r[5],hz=r[0]*r[4]-r[1]*r[3];\n        double h = Math.Sqrt(hx*hx+hy*hy+hz*hz);\n        return h > 1e-10 ? Math.Acos(Math.Max(-1.0,Math.Min(1.0,hz/h))) : 0;\n    }\n    static double DV(double[] r1, double[] r2) {\n        double a1=SMA(r1), a2=SMA(r2);\n        if (a1<=0||a2<=0) { double dx=r2[3]-r1[3],dy=r2[4]-r1[4],dz=r2[5]-r1[5]; return Math.Sqrt(dx*dx+dy*dy+dz*dz); }\n        double di=Math.Abs(Inc(r1)-Inc(r2)), aT=(a1+a2)/2;\n        double vc1=Math.Sqrt(MU/a1),vc2=Math.Sqrt(MU/a2),vT1=Math.Sqrt(MU*(2/a1-1/aT)),vT2=Math.Sqrt(MU*(2/a2-1/aT));\n        return a1<=a2\n            ? Math.Abs(vT1-vc1)+Math.Sqrt(vc2*vc2+vT2*vT2-2*vc2*vT2*Math.Cos(di))\n            : Math.Sqrt(vc1*vc1+vT1*vT1-2*vc1*vT1*Math.Cos(di))+Math.Abs(vT2-vc2);\n    }\n\n    // === Edge cost (a,b: station 0-indexed, -1=depot) ===\n    static double Ec(int a, int b) {\n        if (b<0) return 0;\n        return C[a<0?0:a+1,b+1];\n    }\n    static double TC(int[] t) { double c=Ec(-1,t[0]); for(int i=1;i<t.Length;i++) c+=Ec(t[i-1],t[i]); return c; }\n\n    // === Held-Karp ===\n    static int[] HK() {\n        int full=1<<N;\n        double[] dp = new double[full*N];\n        short[] par = new short[full*N];\n        for(int i=0;i<dp.Length;i++){dp[i]=double.MaxValue/2;par[i]=-1;}\n        for(int i=0;i<N;i++) dp[(1<<i)*N+i]=C[0,i+1];\n        for(int mask=1;mask<full;mask++){\n            int mN=mask*N;\n            for(int last=0;last<N;last++){\n                if((mask&(1<<last))==0) continue;\n                double d=dp[mN+last]; if(d>=double.MaxValue/2) continue;\n                for(int nxt=0;nxt<N;nxt++){\n                    if((mask&(1<<nxt))!=0) continue;\n                    double nd=d+C[last+1,nxt+1];\n                    int idx=(mask|(1<<nxt))*N+nxt;\n                    if(nd<dp[idx]){dp[idx]=nd;par[idx]=(short)last;}\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        int fM=full-1,fB=fM*N,best=0;\n        for(int i=1;i<N;i++) if(dp[fB+i]<dp[fB+best]) best=i;\n        int[] path=new int[N]; int cur=best,msk=fM;\n        for(int s=N-1;s>=0;s--){path[s]=cur;int p=par[msk*N+cur];msk^=(1<<cur);cur=p;}\n        return path;\n    }\n\n    // === Greedy Nearest Neighbor ===\n    static int[] Greedy(int first) {\n        bool[] vis=new bool[N]; int[] t=new int[N]; int cur=first,s0=0;\n        if(first>=0){t[0]=first;vis[first]=true;s0=1;}\n        for(int s=s0;s<N;s++){double best=double.MaxValue;int bj=0;\n            for(int j=0;j<N;j++) if(!vis[j]){double c=Ec(cur,j);if(c<best){best=c;bj=j;}}\n            t[s]=bj;vis[bj]=true;cur=bj;}\n        return t;\n    }\n\n    // === 2-opt ===\n    static void TwoOpt(int[] t) {\n        bool imp=true; while(imp){imp=false;\n            for(int i=0;i<N-1;i++) for(int j=i+2;j<N;j++){\n                int a=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,b=t[i],c=t[j],d=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n                if(Ec(a,c)+Ec(b,d)<Ec(a,b)+Ec(c,d)-1e-10){Array.Reverse(t,i,j-i+1);imp=true;}\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // === Or-opt ===\n    static void OrOpt(int[] t, int sl) {\n        bool imp=true; while(imp){imp=false;\n            for(int i=0;i<=N-sl;i++){\n                int prev=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,fs=t[i],ls=t[i+sl-1],aft=(i+sl<N)?t[i+sl]:-1;\n                double gR=Ec(prev,fs)+Ec(ls,aft)-Ec(prev,aft);\n                if(gR<=1e-10) continue;\n                int bj=int.MinValue; double bg=1e-10;\n                for(int j=-1;j<N;j++){\n                    if(j>=i-1&&j<i+sl) continue;\n                    int A=j<0?-1:t[j],B=j+1<N?t[j+1]:-1;\n                    double g=gR+Ec(A,B)-Ec(A,fs)-Ec(ls,B);\n                    if(g>bg){bg=g;bj=j;}\n                }\n                if(bj>int.MinValue){ApplySeg(t,i,sl,bj);imp=true;break;}\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    static void ApplySeg(int[] t, int from, int sl, int ia) {\n        int[] seg=new int[sl]; Array.Copy(t,from,seg,0,sl);\n        if(ia<from){for(int k=from-1;k>=ia+1;k--) t[k+sl]=t[k]; for(int k=0;k<sl;k++) t[ia+1+k]=seg[k];}\n        else{for(int k=from;k<=ia-sl;k++) t[k]=t[k+sl]; for(int k=0;k<sl;k++) t[ia-sl+1+k]=seg[k];}\n    }\n\n    // === SA helpers ===\n    static double DS(int[] t, int i, int j) {\n        if(i>j){int tmp=i;i=j;j=tmp;}\n        if(j==i+1){int a=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,b=t[i],c=t[j],d=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n            return Ec(a,c)+Ec(c,b)+Ec(b,d)-Ec(a,b)-Ec(b,c)-Ec(c,d);}\n        int pi=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,ni=t[i+1],pj=t[j-1],nj=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n        return Ec(pi,t[j])+Ec(t[j],ni)+Ec(pj,t[i])+Ec(t[i],nj)-Ec(pi,t[i])-Ec(t[i],ni)-Ec(pj,t[j])-Ec(t[j],nj);\n    }\n    static double D2(int[] t, int i, int j) {\n        int a=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,b=t[i],c=t[j],d=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n        return Ec(a,c)+Ec(b,d)-Ec(a,b)-Ec(c,d);\n    }\n    static double DR(int[] t, int from, int ia) {\n        int nd=t[from],pv=(from>0)?t[from-1]:-1,nx=(from<N-1)?t[from+1]:-1;\n        double gR=Ec(pv,nd)+Ec(nd,nx)-Ec(pv,nx);\n        int A=ia<0?-1:t[ia],B=ia+1<N?t[ia+1]:-1;\n        return -(gR+Ec(A,B)-Ec(A,nd)-Ec(nd,B));\n    }\n    static void SA(int[] tour, ref double best, long ms, int seed=42) {\n        if(ms<=0) return;\n        int[] cur=(int[])tour.Clone(); double cc=best;\n        Random rng=new Random(seed);\n        double T0=best/N*0.5,Tf=T0*1e-5; if(T0<=1e-9) T0=0.01;\n        long t0=Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds,t1=t0+ms;\n        while(true){\n            long tn=Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds; if(tn>=t1) break;\n            double prog=Math.Min(1.0,(double)(tn-t0)/ms);\n            double T=T0*Math.Pow(Tf/T0,prog); if(T<Tf) T=Tf;\n            for(int k=0;k<10000;k++){\n                int mt=rng.Next(3),a=rng.Next(N),b; double d;\n                if(mt==0){b=rng.Next(N);if(b==a)continue;d=DS(cur,a,b);}\n                else if(mt==1){b=rng.Next(N);if(b==a)continue;if(a>b){int tmp=a;a=b;b=tmp;}d=D2(cur,a,b);}\n                else{b=rng.Next(N+1)-1;if(b==a-1||b==a)continue;d=DR(cur,a,b);}\n                if(d<=0||rng.NextDouble()<Math.Exp(-d/T)){\n                    if(mt==0){int tmp=cur[a];cur[a]=cur[b];cur[b]=tmp;}\n                    else if(mt==1) Array.Reverse(cur,a,b-a+1);\n                    else ApplySeg(cur,a,1,b);\n                    cc+=d;\n                    if(cc<best-1e-10){best=cc;Array.Copy(cur,tour,N);}\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // === Large Scale Solver ===\n    static int[] Large() {\n        int cores=Math.Min(64,Environment.ProcessorCount);\n        int ns=Math.Min(cores,N+1);\n        var res=new (int[] t,double c)[ns];\n        Parallel.For(0,ns,new ParallelOptions{MaxDegreeOfParallelism=cores},idx=>{\n            int s=idx==0?-1:(idx-1)%N;\n            var t=Greedy(s); TwoOpt(t); OrOpt(t,1);OrOpt(t,2);OrOpt(t,3); TwoOpt(t);\n            res[idx]=(t,TC(t));\n        });\n        long rem=270000-Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds;\n        if(rem>5000){\n            var saRes=new (int[] t,double c)[ns];\n            for(int i=0;i<ns;i++) saRes[i]=((int[])res[i].t.Clone(),res[i].c);\n            Parallel.For(0,ns,new ParallelOptions{MaxDegreeOfParallelism=cores},idx=>{\n                var tt=saRes[idx].t; var cc2=saRes[idx].c;\n                SA(tt,ref cc2,rem-2000,42+idx*7);\n                saRes[idx]=(tt,cc2);\n            });\n            int bi=0; for(int i=1;i<ns;i++) if(saRes[i].c<saRes[bi].c) bi=i;\n            return saRes[bi].t;\n        }\n        int bi2=0; for(int i=1;i<ns;i++) if(res[i].c<res[bi2].c) bi2=i;\n        var bst=res[bi2].t; double bc=res[bi2].c;\n        if(rem>2000) SA(bst,ref bc,rem-1000);\n        return bst;\n    }\n}\n```\n\nI think this code is correct and efficient. Let me do one final review:\n\n1. Input parsing: ✓\n2. Cost matrix: ✓\n3. HK for small N: ✓\n4. Greedy for initialization: ✓\n5. TwoOpt: ✓\n6. OrOpt: ✓\n7. SA: ✓\n8. Large scale: greedy + 2opt + oropt in parallel, then SA in parallel: ✓\n\nPotential issues:\n1. When `Tf/T0 = 0` (if Tf=0): `Math.Pow(0, prog)` = 0 for prog>0, causing T=0. Let me ensure Tf > 0:\n   - `Tf = T0*1e-5`. Since T0 > 1e-9 (guarded by `if(T0<=1e-9) T0=0.01`), Tf > 1e-14. ✓\n2. When `Math.Pow(Tf/T0, prog)` with prog=0: returns 1. T = T0. ✓\n3. When `T = 0` (if Tf = 0 somehow): `Math.Exp(-d/0)` = 0 for d > 0, so we\'d only accept improvements. That\'s fine (greedy descent). ✓\n4. When `N = 2` with TwoOpt: inner loops go from i=0 to N-2=0, j=i+2=2 which is N=2, so j<N is false. Loop doesn\'t execute. That\'s fine (no 2-opt possible for N=2, the only possibility is to reverse the single segment of length 2 which is a swap). Actually for N=2, 2-opt would check i=0, j=2 which is N=2, out of bounds. The loop `for(j=i+2;j<N;j++)` with j starting at 2 and N=2 means j<2 is false immediately, so no iterations. ✓\n   But for N=2, the greedy would still give a valid tour (either [0,1] or [1,0]).For HK (N<=20), N=2 is handled exactly. ✓\n5. For `ApplySeg` when ia=from+sl exactly (insert right after segment):\n   - Loop: k from from to ia-sl=from: just k=from: t[from]=t[from+sl]\n   - Then t[ia-sl+1]=t[from+1]=seg[0]\n   - For sl=1: t[from]=t[from+1], t[from+1]=seg[0]=t_orig[from]\n   - This swaps t[from] and t[from+1] ✓\n6. The check `b==a-1` with b=from-1=ia. So if ia=from-1, b=from-1=a-1 → excluded. ✓\n\nBut what about ia=from-2? Then B=t[ia+1]=t[from-1]. Since from-1 ≠ from, B is not the node. ✓\n\nWhat about ia=from+1 (just one after)? This is excluded for sl=1 in OrOpt: j=i+1 → j is in [i-1, i+sl) = [i-1, i+1). Since j=i+1 is NOT in [i-1, i+1) (as i+1 is NOT less than i+1), it\'s NOT excluded. Wait:\n\nOrOpt exclusion: `if(j>=i-1 && j<i+sl) continue`. With sl=1, i+sl=i+1. So exclude j in [i-1, i). That\'s just j=i-1. But j=i+1 > i, and j < i+sl = i+1 is false. So j=i+1 is NOT excluded by OrOpt.\n\nBut j=i+1 means inserting between t[i+1] and t[i+2], right after the element that comes after the node. This IS a valid move:\n- Original: ..., prev, node, t[i+1], t[i+2], ...\n- Remove node: ..., prev, t[i+1], t[i+2], ...\n- Insert after t[i+1]: ..., prev, t[i+1], node, t[i+2], ...\n- Net effect: node moved from position i to position i+1 (shifted right by 1)\n\nGain computation for j=i+1:\n- gainR = Ec(prev, node) + Ec(node, t[i+1]) - Ec(prev, t[i+1])\n- A = t[i+1], B = t[i+2] (if exists)\n- gainI = Ec(t[i+1], B) - Ec(t[i+1], node) - Ec(node, B)\n  = Ec(t[i+1], t[i+2]) - Ec(t[i+1], node) - Ec(node, t[i+2])\n\nTotal gain = gainR + gainI\n= Ec(prev,node)+Ec(node,t[i+1])-Ec(prev,t[i+1]) + Ec(t[i+1],t[i+2])-Ec(t[i+1],node)-Ec(node,t[i+2])\n\nDirect verification:\n- Original cost: Ec(prev,node) + Ec(node,t[i+1]) + Ec(t[i+1],t[i+2])\n- New cost: Ec(prev,t[i+1]) + Ec(t[i+1],node) + Ec(node,t[i+2])\n- Gain = original - new = Ec(prev,node)+Ec(node,t[i+1])+Ec(t[i+1],t[i+2]) - Ec(prev,t[i+1])-Ec(t[i+1],node)-Ec(node,t[i+2]) ✓\n\nSo j=i+1 is a valid move and correctly computed. ✓\n\nBut in the SA, for relocate: `b=rng.Next(N+1)-1` gives b in [-1, N-1]. When a=i and b=i+1: `b==a-1` means i+1==i-1 (false), `b==a` means i+1==i (false). So not excluded. ✓\n\nDR(t, from=i, ia=i+1):\n- nd=t[i], pv=t[i-1] (or -1), nx=t[i+1]\n- gainR = Ec(pv,nd)+Ec(nd,t[i+1])-Ec(pv,t[i+1])\n- A=t[i+1], B=t[i+2] (or -1)\n- gainI = Ec(t[i+1],B)-Ec(t[i+1],nd)-Ec(nd,B)\n- return -(gainR+gainI) ✓\n\nGood.\n\nAnd ApplySeg(t, i, 1, i+1):\n- ia=i+1 > from=i: shift left from i+1 to i+1-1=i: loop k=i to i: t[i]=t[i+1]\n- Then t[i+1]=seg[0]=t_orig[i]\n- This swaps t[i] and t[i+1] ✓\n\nPerfect.\n\nOkay, I\'m very confident the code is correct. Let me now add one more thing: for the OrOpt exclusion, I wrote `if(j>=i-1&&j<i+sl) continue`. But j=i is in [i-1, i+sl) for sl>=1. This correctly excludes inserting right before the segment (j=i-1) or within/at the segment (j=i to i+sl-1).\n\nFor j=i: inserting between t[i] and t[i+1], which means right after the first element of the segment. For sl=1, this means inserting node after itself (no-op). For sl>1, this would mean inserting the segment after its first element, which makes no sense. So j=i is correctly excluded.\n\nFor j=i+sl (inserting right after segment): NOT excluded. This is the "shift segment right" move, which is valid. ✓\n\nOkay I\'m done checking. Let me now write the final complete code.\n\nI realize there are also some implicit assumptions in how I handle the open TSP for 2-opt and OrOpt. Let me verify:\n\nFor 2-opt with i=0 and j=N-1 (reverse entire tour):\n- a = -1 (depot), b = t[0], c = t[N-1], d = -1 (no next)\n- delta = Ec(-1, t[N-1]) + Ec(t[0], -1) - Ec(-1, t[0]) - Ec(t[N-1], -1)\n        = Ec(-1, t[N-1]) + 0 - Ec(-1, t[0]) - 0\n        = C[0, t[N-1]+1] - C[0, t[0]+1]\n\nThis is positive if starting from depot to t[N-1] (reversed start) is cheaper than to t[0] (original start), minus the effect of reversing all edges. But wait, when we reverse the tour, ALL edges are reversed (and the cost matrix might be asymmetric). So the new tour cost after reversing would be:\n- Ec(-1, t[N-1]) + Ec(t[N-1], t[N-2]) + ... + Ec(t[1], t[0])\n\nWhile the 2-opt delta only accounts for the two boundary edges (a→b and c→d):  \n- Old: Ec(a,b) = Ec(-1,t[0]) and Ec(c,d) = Ec(t[N-1],-1) = 0\n- New: Ec(a,c) = Ec(-1,t[N-1]) and Ec(b,d) = Ec(t[0],-1) = 0\n- delta = Ec(-1,t[N-1]) - Ec(-1,t[0])\n\nBut the reversal also changes ALL the intermediate edges: Ec(t[k],t[k+1]) → Ec(t[k+1],t[k]).\n\nFor a SYMMETRIC cost matrix (Ec(a,b) = Ec(b,a)), the intermediate edges have the same cost when reversed, so only the boundary edges matter. The formula is correct for symmetric costs.\n\nFor ASYMMETRIC costs (like our DV which is slightly asymmetric depending on direction), the 2-opt formula is incorrect because it doesn\'t account for the reversal of intermediate edges.\n\nHmm, this is a problem. For a correct 2-opt with asymmetric costs, when we reverse segment [i..j], we need to:\n1. Change the boundary edges: (t[i-1]→t[i]) and (t[j]→t[j+1]) become (t[i-1]→t[j]) and (t[i]→t[j+1])\n2. Reverse all intermediate edges: (t[k]→t[k+1]) becomes (t[k+1]→t[k]) for k in [i, j-1]\n\nThe delta should be:\ndelta = Ec(a,c) + Ec(b,d) + sum_{k=i}^{j-1} Ec(t[k+1],t[k])\n      - Ec(a,b) - Ec(c,d) - sum_{k=i}^{j-1} Ec(t[k],t[k+1])\n\nFor symmetric costs: sum terms cancel. For asymmetric: they don\'t.\n\nSo my 2-opt is only approximate for asymmetric costs. This means it might not correctly find improvements or might apply "improvements" that actually increase cost.\n\nTo fix this, I\'d need to compute the full delta for 2-opt, which is O(j-i) per candidate move, making TwoOpt O(N^3) instead of O(N^2).\n\nAlternatively, I could make the cost matrix symmetric by taking the average: `C[i,j] = C[j,i] = (DV(i,j) + DV(j,i)) / 2`. This would make all the algorithms correct.\n\nLet me think about how asymmetric the DV matrix is. The main source of asymmetry is the plane change direction:\n- For a1 < a2: do plane change at apoapsis (a2)\n- For a2 < a1: do plane change at apoapsis (a1)\n\nSo DV(a1→a2) = dv1 + sqrt(vc2^2 + vT2^2 - 2*vc2*vT2*cos(di))\nAnd DV(a2→a1) = sqrt(vc2^2 + vT2^2 - 2*vc2*vT2*cos(di)) + dv1... wait that\'s the same!\n\nLet me recalculate for a1=7000, a2=42164, di=0.5 rad:\n- DV(7000→42164):\n  - dv1 = |vT1-vc1| (at periapsis a1=7000)\n  - dv2 = sqrt(vc2^2+vT2^2-2*vc2*vT2*cos(di)) (combined at apoapsis a2=42164)\n- DV(42164→7000):\n  - dv1 = sqrt(vc2^2+vT2^2-2*vc2*vT2*cos(di))... wait, no.\n  - Now a1=42164 and a2=7000, so a1>a2, use the else branch:\n  - dv1 = sqrt(vc1^2+vT1^2-2*vc1*vT1*cos(di)) where vc1=sqrt(MU/42164), vT1=sqrt(MU*(2/42164-1/aT))\n  - dv2 = |vT2-vc2| where vc2=sqrt(MU/7000), vT2=sqrt(MU*(2/7000-1/aT))\n  - Here vc1, vT1, vc2, vT2 are different from before (swapped roles)\n\nIn my DV function, when a1>a2:\n- aT = (a1+a2)/2 (same regardless of direction)\n- vc1 = sqrt(MU/a1) (circular velocity at a1=42164)\n- vc2 = sqrt(MU/a2) (circular velocity at a2=7000)\n- vT1 = sqrt(MU*(2/a1-1/aT)) (transfer velocity at a1=apoapsis)\n- vT2 = sqrt(MU*(2/a2-1/aT)) (transfer velocity at a2=periapsis)\n- Combined burn at a1 (apoapsis, source): sqrt(vc1^2+vT1^2-2*vc1*vT1*cos(di))\n- Simple burn at a2 (periapsis, destination): |vT2-vc2|\n\nFor di=0: DV(42164→7000) = |vc1-vT1| + |vT2-vc2| = |vc2_orig-vT1_orig| + |vT2_orig-vc1_orig| where orig means the original a1=7000, a2=42164 case... wait I\'m getting confused by variable reuse.\n\nLet me use r_lo=7000 and r_hi=42164:\n- vc_lo = sqrt(MU/r_lo), vc_hi = sqrt(MU/r_hi)\n- aT = (r_lo+r_hi)/2\n- vT_lo = sqrt(MU*(2/r_lo-1/aT)) (velocity at periapsis of transfer)\n- vT_hi = sqrt(MU*(2/r_hi-1/aT)) (velocity at apoapsis of transfer)\n\nDV(r_lo → r_hi):\n- a1=r_lo < a2=r_hi, so:\n- dv1 = |vT_lo - vc_lo| (burn at periapsis)\n- dv2 = sqrt(vc_hi^2+vT_hi^2-2*vc_hi*vT_hi*cos(di)) (burn at apoapsis, combined with plane change)\n- DV = dv1 + dv2\n\nDV(r_hi → r_lo):\n- a1=r_hi > a2=r_lo, so:\n- dv1 = sqrt(vc_hi^2+vT_hi^2-2*vc_hi*vT_hi*cos(di)) (burn at apoapsis=source, combined with plane change)\n- dv2 = |vT_lo - vc_lo| (burn at periapsis=destination)\n- DV = dv1 + dv2\n\nSo DV(r_lo → r_hi) = DV(r_hi → r_lo)! The cost matrix IS symmetric for Hohmann transfers with my formula.\n\nLet me verify mathematically:\n- DV(r_lo→r_hi) = |vT_lo-vc_lo| + sqrt(vc_hi^2+vT_hi^2-2*vc_hi*vT_hi*cos(di))\n- DV(r_hi→r_lo) = sqrt(vc_hi^2+vT_hi^2-2*vc_hi*vT_hi*cos(di)) + |vT_lo-vc_lo|\n- They\'re equal! ✓ (Just different order of addition)\n\nSo the cost matrix IS symmetric! This means my 2-opt formula is correct even for this asymmetric-looking case.\n\nPhysically, this makes sense: the cost of a Hohmann transfer + combined plane change is the same regardless of direction (from r_lo to r_hi or r_hi to r_lo), because the delta-V burns are at the same points in the orbit (periapsis and apoapsis), just in different orders.\n\nSo the cost matrix is symmetric, and all my 2-opt and OrOpt formulas are correct. ✓\n\nActually wait, let me double-check the asymmetric case: what if a1 and a2 are NOT in the ratio used by the formula?\n\nFor a1 = r1 and a2 = r2 with r1 < r2:\n- DV(r1→r2): a1<=a2 branch, uses vc1,vc2,vT1,vT2 computed from a1=r1,a2=r2\n- DV(r2→r1): a1>a2 branch (with a1=r2, a2=r1), uses vc1=sqrt(MU/r2), vc2=sqrt(MU/r1), vT1=sqrt(MU*(2/r2-1/aT)), vT2=sqrt(MU*(2/r1-1/aT))\n  - aT = (r2+r1)/2 (same)\n  - dv1 = sqrt(vc1^2+vT1^2-2*vc1*vT1*cos(di))\n  - dv2 = |vT2-vc2|\n\nNow:\n- In DV(r1→r2): vc2=sqrt(MU/r2), vT2=sqrt(MU*(2/r2-1/aT)). dv2=sqrt(vc2^2+vT2^2-2*vc2*vT2*cos(di))\n  Here vc2=sqrt(MU/r2) and vT2=sqrt(MU*(2/r2-1/aT))\n  \n- In DV(r2→r1): dv1=sqrt(vc1^2+vT1^2-2*vc1*vT1*cos(di)) where vc1=sqrt(MU/r2), vT1=sqrt(MU*(2/r2-1/aT))\n  This is the SAME as dv2 from DV(r1→r2)!\n\nAnd in DV(r2→r1): dv2=|vT2-vc2| where vc2=sqrt(MU/r1), vT2=sqrt(MU*(2/r1-1/aT)).\n- In DV(r1→r2): dv1=|vT1-vc1| where vc1=sqrt(MU/r1), vT1=sqrt(MU*(2/r1-1/aT)).\n- These are the same!\n\nSo DV(r1→r2) = |vT_r1-vc_r1| + combined(r2) and DV(r2→r1) = combined(r2) + |vT_r1-vc_r1|. They\'re equal. ✓ The cost matrix is symmetric.\n\nExcellent! This confirms that my 2-opt and OrOpt are correct.\n\nFinal thought: for the 2-opt, when we apply Array.Reverse, we reverse the middle edges but the costs are symmetric (C[a,b]=C[b,a] in terms of the TSP traversal). Since the cost matrix C[i,j] is symmetric (C[i,j]=C[j,i] for all i,j), the reversed traversal has the same edge costs. So the 2-opt is indeed correct. ✓\n\nActually wait: I said the cost matrix is symmetric. Let me verify: for two orbits with the same semi-major axis but different inclination, DV(1→2) = DV(2→1) (both give 2*vc*sin(di/2)). ✓\n\nFor two orbits with different SMAs and the same inclination: DV(r_lo→r_hi) = |vT_lo-vc_lo| + |vc_hi-vT_hi| = DV(r_hi→r_lo) = |vc_hi-vT_hi| + |vT_lo-vc_lo|. ✓ Same.\n\nFor two orbits with different SMAs AND different inclinations: I showed above they\'re equal. ✓\n\nSo C[i,j] = C[j,i] for all i,j. The 2-opt reversal doesn\'t change the cost of intermediate edges. ✓\n\nGreat, everything is consistent and correct.\n\nNow let me think about one more edge case: what if two stations are at exactly the same orbital state? Then DV(i,j) = 0. This should be handled correctly everywhere. ✓\n\nOkay, I\'m going to write the final code now. No more analysis! Here it is:\n\nI want to be careful about one thing: the SA applies `Array.Reverse(cur, a, b-a+1)` for 2-opt moves. This reverses the segment in-place. Since the cost matrix is symmetric, the reversed tour has the same intermediate edge costs as the original, so the delta is purely from the boundary edges. The formula D2 computes this correctly. ✓\n\nAnd when we compute `cc += d` (updating the running cost), we need the running cost to be accurate. Any accumulated floating-point error might cause drift. Let me add a periodic recalculation:\n\n```csharp\nif (k % 1000 == 0) cc = TC(cur); // periodic recalculation\n```\n\nBut this is O(N) every 1000 iterations, which is O(N/1000) overhead. For N=100 and 10M iterations per second: 10M/1000 * 100 = 1M operations per second just for recalculation. That\'s fine.\n\nHowever, for correctness, if the delta computations are exact (no floating point drift), recalculation is unnecessary. For practical purposes, let me add it every 100k iterations:\n\n```csharp\nif (iteration_count % 100000 == 0) cc = TC(cur);\n```\n\nActually, for this problem, I\'ll keep it simple and not add this. The floating point drift should be small enough for 100 stations over millions of iterations.\n\nOkay, truly final code coming up. Let me write it cleanly without further deliberation:\n\nActually, I realize I should also handle potential issues with the OR-opt when `B == node` (which I analyzed shouldn\'t happen, but let me double-check).\n\nIn OrOpt(t, sl=1):\n- i: position of node\n- For j: A=t[j], B=t[j+1]\n- We exclude j == i-1 (B=t[i]=node) and j == i (A=t[i]=node)\n- If j < i-1: A=t[j] ≠ node, B=t[j+1] ≠ node (since j+1 <= i-1 < i). ✓\n- If j >= i+1 (valid range): A=t[j], where j >= i+1 > i. Since tour has no duplicates, t[j] ≠ t[i]=node. B=t[j+1], where j+1 >= i+2 > i. So B ≠ node. ✓\n- j = -1: A=-1 (depot), B=t[0]. If i>0 (guaranteed since i=0 is excluded when j=-1): B=t[0] ≠ t[i]=node. ✓\n\nSo B != node in all valid cases. ✓\n\nAlso A != node in all valid cases (shown above). ✓\n\nOkay perfect. The final code:\n\n```csharp\nusing System;\nusing System.Linq;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\nusing System.Diagnostics;\nusing System.Globalization;\n\nclass Program\n{\n    static double MU;\n    static int N;\n    static double[,] C;\n    static readonly Stopwatch Sw = Stopwatch.StartNew();\n\n    static void Main()\n    {\n        // Parse\n        var f = (Console.ReadLine() ?? "").Trim()\n            .Split(new[] { \' \', \'\\t\' }, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);\n        N = int.Parse(f[0]);\n        MU = double.Parse(f[1], CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);\n        double[][] rv = new double[N + 1][];\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N; i++)\n            rv[i] = (Console.ReadLine() ?? "").Trim()\n                .Split(new[] { \' \', \'\\t\' }, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries)\n                .Select(s => double.Parse(s, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)).ToArray();\n\n        C = new double[N + 1, N + 1];\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N; i++)\n            for (int j = 0; j <= N; j++)\n                if (i != j) C[i, j] = DV(rv[i], rv[j]);\n\n        int[] ans = N == 1 ? new[] { 0 } : N <= 20 ? HK() : Large();\n        Console.WriteLine(string.Join(" ", ans));\n    }\n\n    static double SMA(double[] r)\n    {\n        double mag = Math.Sqrt(r[0] * r[0] + r[1] * r[1] + r[2] * r[2]);\n        double E = 0.5 * (r[3] * r[3] + r[4] * r[4] + r[5] * r[5]) - MU / mag;\n        return E < 0 ? -MU / (2 * E) : -1;\n    }\n\n    static double Inc(double[] r)\n    {\n        double hx = r[1] * r[5] - r[2] * r[4];\n        double hy = r[2] * r[3] - r[0] * r[5];\n        double hz = r[0] * r[4] - r[1] * r[3];\n        double h = Math.Sqrt(hx * hx + hy * hy + hz * hz);\n        return h > 1e-10 ? Math.Acos(Math.Max(-1.0, Math.Min(1.0, hz / h))) : 0;\n    }\n\n    static double DV(double[] r1, double[] r2)\n    {\n        double a1 = SMA(r1), a2 = SMA(r2);\n        if (a1 <= 0 || a2 <= 0)\n        {\n            double dx = r2[3] - r1[3], dy = r2[4] - r1[4], dz = r2[5] - r1[5];\n            return Math.Sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy + dz * dz);\n        }\n        double di = Math.Abs(Inc(r1) - Inc(r2));\n        double aT = (a1 + a2) / 2;\n        double vc1 = Math.Sqrt(MU / a1), vc2 = Math.Sqrt(MU / a2);\n        double vT1 = Math.Sqrt(MU * (2.0 / a1 - 1.0 / aT));\n        double vT2 = Math.Sqrt(MU * (2.0 / a2 - 1.0 / aT));\n        if (a1 <= a2)\n            return Math.Abs(vT1 - vc1) + Math.Sqrt(vc2 * vc2 + vT2 * vT2 - 2 * vc2 * vT2 * Math.Cos(di));\n        return Math.Sqrt(vc1 * vc1 + vT1 * vT1 - 2 * vc1 * vT1 * Math.Cos(di)) + Math.Abs(vT2 - vc2);\n    }\n\n    static double Ec(int a, int b)\n    {\n        if (b < 0) return 0;\n        return C[a < 0 ? 0 : a + 1, b + 1];\n    }\n\n    static double TC(int[] t)\n    {\n        double c = Ec(-1, t[0]);\n        for (int i = 1; i < t.Length; i++) c += Ec(t[i - 1], t[i]);\n        return c;\n    }\n\n    static int[] HK()\n    {\n        int full = 1 << N;\n        double[] dp = new double[full * N];\n        short[] par = new short[full * N];\n        for (int i = 0; i < dp.Length; i++) { dp[i] = double.MaxValue / 2; par[i] = -1; }\n        for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) dp[(1 << i) * N + i] = C[0, i + 1];\n        for (int mask = 1; mask < full; mask++)\n        {\n            int mN = mask * N;\n            for (int last = 0; last < N; last++)\n            {\n                if ((mask & (1 << last)) == 0) continue;\n                double d = dp[mN + last];\n                if (d >= double.MaxValue / 2) continue;\n                for (int nxt = 0; nxt < N; nxt++)\n                {\n                    if ((mask & (1 << nxt)) != 0) continue;\n                    double nd = d + C[last + 1, nxt + 1];\n                    int idx = (mask | (1 << nxt)) * N + nxt;\n                    if (nd < dp[idx]) { dp[idx] = nd; par[idx] = (short)last; }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        int fM = full - 1, fB = fM * N, best = 0;\n        for (int i = 1; i < N; i++) if (dp[fB + i] < dp[fB + best]) best = i;\n        int[] path = new int[N];\n        int cur = best, msk = fM;\n        for (int s = N - 1; s >= 0; s--)\n        {\n            path[s] = cur;\n            int p = par[msk * N + cur];\n            msk ^= (1 << cur);\n            cur = p;\n        }\n        return path;\n    }\n\n    static int[] Greedy(int first)\n    {\n        bool[] vis = new bool[N];\n        int[] t = new int[N];\n        int cur = first, s0 = 0;\n        if (first >= 0) { t[0] = first; vis[first] = true; s0 = 1; }\n        for (int s = s0; s < N; s++)\n        {\n            double best = double.MaxValue; int bj = 0;\n            for (int j = 0; j < N; j++)\n                if (!vis[j]) { double c = Ec(cur, j); if (c < best) { best = c; bj = j; } }\n            t[s] = bj; vis[bj] = true; cur = bj;\n        }\n        return t;\n    }\n\n    static void TwoOpt(int[] t)\n    {\n        bool imp = true;\n        while (imp)\n        {\n            imp = false;\n            for (int i = 0; i < N - 1; i++)\n                for (int j = i + 2; j < N; j++)\n                {\n                    int a = (i > 0) ? t[i - 1] : -1, b = t[i], c = t[j], d = (j < N - 1) ? t[j + 1] : -1;\n                    if (Ec(a, c) + Ec(b, d) < Ec(a, b) + Ec(c, d) - 1e-10)\n                    { Array.Reverse(t, i, j - i + 1); imp = true; }\n                }\n        }\n    }\n\n    static void OrOpt(int[] t, int sl)\n    {\n        bool imp = true;\n        while (imp)\n        {\n            imp = false;\n            for (int i = 0; i <= N - sl; i++)\n            {\n                int prev = (i > 0) ? t[i - 1] : -1, fs = t[i], ls = t[i + sl - 1], aft = (i + sl < N) ? t[i + sl] : -1;\n                double gR = Ec(prev, fs) + Ec(ls, aft) - Ec(prev, aft);\n                if (gR <= 1e-10) continue;\n                int bj = int.MinValue; double bg = 1e-10;\n                for (int j = -1; j < N; j++)\n                {\n                    if (j >= i - 1 && j < i + sl) continue;\n                    int A = j < 0 ? -1 : t[j], B = j + 1 < N ? t[j + 1] : -1;\n                    double g = gR + Ec(A, B) - Ec(A, fs) - Ec(ls, B);\n                    if (g > bg) { bg = g; bj = j; }\n                }\n                if (bj > int.MinValue) { ApplySeg(t, i, sl, bj); imp = true; break; }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    static void ApplySeg(int[] t, int from, int sl, int ia)\n    {\n        int[] seg = new int[sl];\n        Array.Copy(t, from, seg, 0, sl);\n        if (ia < from)\n        {\n            for (int k = from - 1; k >= ia + 1; k--) t[k + sl] = t[k];\n            for (int k = 0; k < sl; k++) t[ia + 1 + k] = seg[k];\n        }\n        else\n        {\n            for (int k = from; k <= ia - sl; k++) t[k] = t[k + sl];\n            for (int k = 0; k < sl; k++) t[ia - sl + 1 + k] = seg[k];\n        }\n    }\n\n    static double DS(int[] t, int i, int j)\n    {\n        if (i > j) { int tmp = i; i = j; j = tmp; }\n        if (j == i + 1)\n        {\n            int a = (i > 0) ? t[i - 1] : -1, b = t[i], c = t[j], d = (j < N - 1) ? t[j + 1] : -1;\n            return Ec(a, c) + Ec(c, b) + Ec(b, d) - Ec(a, b) - Ec(b, c) - Ec(c, d);\n        }\n        int pi = (i > 0) ? t[i - 1] : -1, ni = t[i + 1], pj = t[j - 1], nj = (j < N - 1) ? t[j + 1] : -1;\n        return Ec(pi, t[j]) + Ec(t[j], ni) + Ec(pj, t[i]) + Ec(t[i], nj)\n             - Ec(pi, t[i]) - Ec(t[i], ni) - Ec(pj, t[j]) - Ec(t[j], nj);\n    }\n\n    static double D2(int[] t, int i, int j)\n    {\n        int a = (i > 0) ? t[i - 1] : -1, b = t[i], c = t[j], d = (j < N - 1) ? t[j + 1] : -1;\n        return Ec(a, c) + Ec(b, d) - Ec(a, b) - Ec(c, d);\n    }\n\n    static double DR(int[] t, int from, int ia)\n    {\n        int nd = t[from], pv = (from > 0) ? t[from - 1] : -1, nx = (from < N - 1) ? t[from + 1] : -1;\n        double gR = Ec(pv, nd) + Ec(nd, nx) - Ec(pv, nx);\n        int A = ia < 0 ? -1 : t[ia], B = ia + 1 < N ? t[ia + 1] : -1;\n        return -(gR + Ec(A, B) - Ec(A, nd) - Ec(nd, B));\n    }\n\n    static void SA(int[] tour, ref double best, long ms, int seed = 42)\n    {\n        if (ms <= 0) return;\n        int[] cur = (int[])tour.Clone();\n        double cc = best;\n        Random rng = new Random(seed);\n        double T0 = best / N * 0.5, Tf = T0 * 1e-5;\n        if (T0 <= 1e-9) T0 = 0.01;\n        Tf = Math.Max(Tf, 1e-12);\n        long t0 = Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds, t1 = t0 + ms;\n        while (true)\n        {\n            long tn = Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds;\n            if (tn >= t1) break;\n            double prog = Math.Min(1.0, (double)(tn - t0) / ms);\n            double T = T0 * Math.Pow(Tf / T0, prog);\n            if (T < Tf) T = Tf;\n            for (int k = 0; k < 10000; k++)\n            {\n                int mt = rng.Next(3), a = rng.Next(N), b;\n                double d;\n                if (mt == 0)\n                {\n                    b = rng.Next(N); if (b == a) continue;\n                    d = DS(cur, a, b);\n                }\n                else if (mt == 1)\n                {\n                    b = rng.Next(N); if (b == a) continue;\n                    if (a > b) { int tmp = a; a = b; b = tmp; }\n                    d = D2(cur, a, b);\n                }\n                else\n                {\n                    b = rng.Next(N + 1) - 1;\n                    if (b == a - 1 || b == a) continue;\n                    d = DR(cur, a, b);\n                }\n                if (d <= 0 || rng.NextDouble() < Math.Exp(-d / T))\n                {\n                    if (mt == 0) { int tmp = cur[a]; cur[a] = cur[b]; cur[b] = tmp; }\n                    else if (mt == 1) Array.Reverse(cur, a, b - a + 1);\n                    else ApplySeg(cur, a, 1, b);\n                    cc += d;\n                    if (cc < best - 1e-10) { best = cc; Array.Copy(cur, tour, N); }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    static int[] Large()\n    {\n        int cores = Math.Min(64, Environment.ProcessorCount);\n        int ns = Math.Min(cores, N + 1);\n        var res = new (int[] t, double c)[ns];\n        Parallel.For(0, ns, new ParallelOptions { MaxDegreeOfParallelism = cores }, idx =>\n        {\n            int s = idx == 0 ? -1 : (idx - 1) % N;\n            int[] t = Greedy(s);\n            TwoOpt(t); Specifically:\n```csharp\nvar tt = saRes[idx].t;\nvar cc2 = saRes[idx].c;\nSA(tt, ref cc2, rem - 2000, 42 + idx * 7);\nsaRes[idx] = (tt, cc2);\n```\n\nThe `saRes` is an array of value-type tuples `(int[], double)`. When we do `saRes[idx] = (tt, cc2)`, we\'re updating the tuple at index `idx`. Since `(int[], double)` is a value type (struct), assigning `saRes[idx]` creates a new struct at that array slot.\n\nBut wait: `int[]` is a reference type (object reference). When SA modifies `tt` in place (via Array.Copy from inside SA), it modifies the array that both `tt` and `saRes[idx].t` point to.\n\nSo after SA, `saRes[idx].t` already points to the best array (modified in place). And `saRes[idx] = (tt, cc2)` just updates the cost value. ✓\n\nThis is thread-safe because each thread accesses a different `idx`. ✓\n\nOkay, I\'m going to write the final code now. Here\'s the final code:\n\nActually I realize there\'s a subtle bug in OrOpt: I skip `if (gR <= 1e-10) continue;` but this optimization might cause me to miss valid improvements where gR is small but gainInsert is large enough to compensate. Wait, no: gR represents the gain from removing the segment from its current position. If gR <= 0, then removing the segment doesn\'t help (it costs more to remove it). I should remove it.\n\nBut wait: gR = E(prev,fs) + E(ls,aft) - E(prev,aft). This is the "triangle inequality violation" for the current edges. If gR < 0, it means the detour through the segment is cheaper than the direct connection, so removing the segment would cost more (making the path longer). In that case, gR < 0 means the segment is "useful" in its current position from the perspective of the edges it connects.\n\nFor the total gain to be positive with gR < 0: gainInsert must be |gR| + epsilon positive. This means inserting the segment elsewhere gives a huge gain that more than compensates for the loss of removing it.\n\nThis is possible! For example:\n- Current: A -> [s1, s2] -> B -> ... -> C -> D (segment [s1,s2] is useful here, gR<0)\n- Alternative: A -> B -> ... -> C -> [s1, s2] -> D (inserting segment elsewhere gives big gain)\n\nSo my optimization `if (gR <= 1e-10) continue;` is incorrect and might miss improvements.\n\nLet me remove this optimization and compute the full gain for all positions:\n\n```csharp\nstatic void OrOpt(int[] t, int sl) {\n    bool imp = true;\n    while (imp) {\n        imp = false;\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N - sl; i++) {\n            int prev = (i>0)?t[i-1]:-1, fs = t[i], ls = t[i+sl-1], aft = (i+sl<N)?t[i+sl]:-1;\n            double gR = Ec(prev,fs)+Ec(ls,aft)-Ec(prev,aft);\n            // Note: gR can be negative\n            int bj = int.MinValue; double bg = 1e-10; // minimum gain threshold\n            for (int j = -1; j < N; j++) {\n                if (j >= i-1 && j < i+sl) continue;\n                int A = j<0?-1:t[j], B = j+1<N?t[j+1]:-1;\n                double g = gR + Ec(A,B) - Ec(A,fs) - Ec(ls,B);\n                if (g > bg) { bg = g; bj = j; }\n            }\n            if (bj > int.MinValue) { ApplySeg(t,i,sl,bj); imp = true; break; }\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\nThis is the correct version without the incorrect optimization. ✓\n\nFor performance: without the early continue, we compute `gR` for all positions even when gR is very negative. But the inner loop still computes the full gain. For N=100 and sl=1: O(N^2) per improvement, O(N^4) total in worst case. But in practice, converges quickly. ✓\n\nOkay let me finalize the code. Removing that optimization.\n\nActually, let me reconsider. The optimization `if (gR <= 1e-10) continue` is a heuristic shortcut. If gR < 0, it means the segment is well-integrated in its current position (removing it would increase cost). The question is: can the gain from inserting elsewhere be so large that it overcomes the removal cost?\n\nFor the Hohmann transfer metric: delta-V is always non-negative. E(a,b) >= 0 for all a,b. So the triangle inequality might or might not hold.\n\nIf the metric satisfies E(A,B) <= E(A,fs) + E(ls,B) (triangle inequality), then gainInsert <= 0. In that case, gR + gainInsert <= gR. If gR <= 0, total gain <= 0, so skip is valid.\n\nFor a metric satisfying triangle inequality: the optimization is valid.\nFor a metric not satisfying triangle inequality: the optimization might miss improvements.\n\nThe Hohmann transfer metric does NOT necessarily satisfy the triangle inequality. For example, going from orbit A to orbit C directly might be cheaper than going A→B→C if there\'s a favorable inclination alignment.\n\nSo the optimization is NOT valid in general. I should remove it.\n\nHowever, in practice, for the orbital TSP, triangle inequality violations are relatively rare, and the optimization might only miss a few improvements. For performance, it\'s worth keeping. But for correctness, I should remove it.\n\nI\'ll remove it for correctness. The performance impact is minimal for N <= 100.\n\nOkay, truly final code now:\n\nLet me write the complete final version:\n\n```csharp\nusing System;\nusing System.Linq;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\nusing System.Diagnostics;\nusing System.Globalization;\n\nclass Program {\n    static double MU;\n    static int N;\n    static double[,] C;\n    static readonly Stopwatch Sw = Stopwatch.StartNew();\n\n    static void Main() {\n        string[] f = (Console.ReadLine() ?? "").Trim().Split(new[]{\' \',\'\\t\'}, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);\n        N = int.Parse(f[0]);\n        MU = double.Parse(f[1], CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);\n        double[][] rv = new double[N+1][];\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N; i++)\n            rv[i] = (Console.ReadLine() ?? "").Trim().Split(new[]{\' \',\'\\t\'}, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries)\n                    .Select(s => double.Parse(s, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)).ToArray();\n        C = new double[N+1, N+1];\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N; i++)\n            for (int j = 0; j <= N; j++)\n                if (i != j) C[i,j] = DV(rv[i], rv[j]);\n        int[] ans = N==1 ? new[]{0} : N<=20 ? HK() : Large();\n        Console.WriteLine(string.Join(" ", ans));\n    }\n\n    static double SMA(double[] r) {\n        double mag = Math.Sqrt(r[0]*r[0]+r[1]*r[1]+r[2]*r[2]);\n        double E = 0.5*(r[3]*r[3]+r[4]*r[4]+r[5]*r[5]) - MU/mag;\n        return E<0 ? -MU/(2*E) : -1;\n    }\n    static double Inc(double[] r) {\n        double hx=r[1]*r[5]-r[2]*r[4],hy=r[2]*r[3]-r[0]*r[5],hz=r[0]*r[4]-r[1]*r[3];\n        double h=Math.Sqrt(hx*hx+hy*hy+hz*hz);\n        return h>1e-10 ? Math.Acos(Math.Max(-1.0,Math.Min(1.0,hz/h))) : 0;\n    }\n    static double DV(double[] r1, double[] r2) {\n        double a1=SMA(r1),a2=SMA(r2);\n        if (a1<=0||a2<=0) {\n            double dx=r2[3]-r1[3],dy=r2[4]-r1[4],dz=r2[5]-r1[5];\n            return Math.Sqrt(dx*dx+dy*dy+dz*dz);\n        }\n        double di=Math.Abs(Inc(r1)-Inc(r2)),aT=(a1+a2)/2;\n        double vc1=Math.Sqrt(MU/a1),vc2=Math.Sqrt(MU/a2);\n        double vT1=Math.Sqrt(MU*(2.0/a1-1.0/aT)),vT2=Math.Sqrt(MU*(2.0/a2-1.0/aT));\n        return a1<=a2\n            ? Math.Abs(vT1-vc1)+Math.Sqrt(vc2*vc2+vT2*vT2-2*vc2*vT2*Math.Cos(di))\n            : Math.Sqrt(vc1*vc1+vT1*vT1-2*vc1*vT1*Math.Cos(di))+Math.Abs(vT2-vc2);\n    }\n\n    static double Ec(int a, int b) {\n        if (b<0) return 0;\n        return C[a<0?0:a+1,b+1];\n    }\n    static double TC(int[] t) {\n        double c=Ec(-1,t[0]); for(int i=1;i<t.Length;i++) c+=Ec(t[i-1],t[i]); return c;\n    }\n\n    static int[] HK() {\n        int full=1<<N;\n        double[] dp=new double[full*N];\n        short[] par=new short[full*N];\n        for(int i=0;i<dp.Length;i++){dp[i]=double.MaxValue/2;par[i]=-1;}\n        for(int i=0;i<N;i++) dp[(1<<i)*N+i]=C[0,i+1];\n        for(int mask=1;mask<full;mask++) {\n            int mN=mask*N;\n            for(int last=0;last<N;last++) {\n                if((mask&(1<<last))==0) continue;\n                double d=dp[mN+last]; if(d>=double.MaxValue/2) continue;\n                for(int nxt=0;nxt<N;nxt++) {\n                    if((mask&(1<<nxt))!=0) continue;\n                    double nd=d+C[last+1,nxt+1];\n                    int idx=(mask|(1<<nxt))*N+nxt;\n                    if(nd<dp[idx]){dp[idx]=nd;par[idx]=(short)last;}\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        int fM=full-1,fB=fM*N,best=0;\n        for(int i=1;i<N;i++) if(dp[fB+i]<dp[fB+best]) best=i;\n        int[] path=new int[N]; int cur=best,msk=fM;\n        for(int s=N-1;s>=0;s--){path[s]=cur;int p=par[msk*N+cur];msk^=(1<<cur);cur=p;}\n        return path;\n    }\n\n    static int[] Greedy(int first) {\n        bool[] vis=new bool[N]; int[] t=new int[N]; int cur=first,s0=0;\n        if(first>=0){t[0]=first;vis[first]=true;s0=1;}\n        for(int s=s0;s<N;s++){double best=double.MaxValue;int bj=0;\n            for(int j=0;j<N;j++) if(!vis[j]){double c=Ec(cur,j);if(c<best){best=c;bj=j;}}\n            t[s]=bj;vis[bj]=true;cur=bj;}\n        return t;\n    }\n\n    static void TwoOpt(int[] t) {\n        bool imp=true; while(imp){imp=false;\n            for(int i=0;i<N-1;i++) for(int j=i+2;j<N;j++) {\n                int a=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,b=t[i],c=t[j],d=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n                if(Ec(a,c)+Ec(b,d)<Ec(a,b)+Ec(c,d)-1e-10){Array.Reverse(t,i,j-i+1);imp=true;}\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    static void OrOpt(int[] t, int sl) {\n        bool imp=true; while(imp){imp=false;\n            for(int i=0;i<=N-sl;i++) {\n                int prev=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,fs=t[i],ls=t[i+sl-1],aft=(i+sl<N)?t[i+sl]:-1;\n                double gR=Ec(prev,fs)+Ec(ls,aft)-Ec(prev,aft);\n                int bj=int.MinValue; double bg=1e-10;\n                for(int j=-1;j<N;j++) {\n                    if(j>=i-1&&j<i+sl) continue;\n                    int A=j<0?-1:t[j],B=j+1<N?t[j+1]:-1;\n                    double g=gR+Ec(A,B)-Ec(A,fs)-Ec(ls,B);\n                    if(g>bg){bg=g;bj=j;}\n                }\n                if(bj>int.MinValue){ApplySeg(t,i,sl,bj);imp=true;break;}\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    static void ApplySeg(int[] t, int from, int sl, int ia) {\n        int[] seg=new int[sl]; Array.Copy(t,from,seg,0,sl);\n        if(ia<from){for(int k=from-1;k>=ia+1;k--) t[k+sl]=t[k]; for(int k=0;k<sl;k++) t[ia+1+k]=seg[k];}\n        else{for(int k=from;k<=ia-sl;k++) t[k]=t[k+sl]; for(int k=0;k<sl;k++) t[ia-sl+1+k]=seg[k];}\n    }\n\n    static double DS(int[] t, int i, int j) {\n        if(i>j){int tmp=i;i=j;j=tmp;}\n        if(j==i+1){int a=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,b=t[i],c=t[j],d=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n            return Ec(a,c)+Ec(c,b)+Ec(b,d)-Ec(a,b)-Ec(b,c)-Ec(c,d);}\n        int pi=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,ni=t[i+1],pj=t[j-1],nj=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n        return Ec(pi,t[j])+Ec(t[j],ni)+Ec(pj,t[i])+Ec(t[i],nj)-Ec(pi,t[i])-Ec(t[i],ni)-Ec(pj,t[j])-Ec(t[j],nj);\n    }\n    static double D2(int[] t, int i, int j) {\n        int a=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,b=t[i],c=t[j],d=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n        return Ec(a,c)+Ec(b,d)-Ec(a,b)-Ec(c,d);\n    }\n    static double DR(int[] t, int from, int ia) {\n        int nd=t[from],pv=(from>0)?t[from-1]:-1,nx=(from<N-1)?t[from+1]:-1;\n        double gR=Ec(pv,nd)+Ec(nd,nx)-Ec(pv,nx);\n        int A=ia<0?-1:t[ia],B=ia+1<N?t[ia+1]:-1;\n        return -(gR+Ec(A,B)-Ec(A,nd)-Ec(nd,B));\n    }\n\n    static void SA(int[] tour, ref double best, long ms, int seed=42) {\n        if(ms<=0) return;\n        int[] cur=(int[])tour.Clone(); double cc=best;\n        Random rng=new Random(seed);\n        double T0=best/N*0.5,Tf=T0*1e-5; if(T0<=1e-9){T0=0.01;Tf=1e-11;}\n        long t0=Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds,t1=t0+ms;\n        while(true){\n            long tn=Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds; if(tn>=t1) break;\n            double prog=Math.Min(1.0,(double)(tn-t0)/ms);\n            double T=T0*Math.Pow(Tf/T0,prog); if(T<Tf) T=Tf;\n            for(int k=0;k<10000;k++){\n                int mt=rng.Next(3),a=rng.Next(N),b; if(cc<best-1e-10){best=cc;Array.Copy(cur,tour,N);}\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    static int[] Large() {\n        int cores=Math.Min(64,Environment.ProcessorCount);\n        int ns=Math.Min(cores,N+1);\n        var res=new (int[] t,double c)[ns];\n        Parallel.For(0,ns,new ParallelOptions{MaxDegreeOfParallelism=cores},idx=>{\n            int s=idx==0?-1:(idx-1)%N;\n            int[] t=Greedy(s); TwoOpt(t); OrOpt(t,1);OrOpt(t,2);OrOpt(t,3); TwoOpt(t);\n            res[idx]=(t,TC(t));\n        });\n        long rem=270000-Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds;\n        if(rem>5000){\n            var saRes=new (int[] t,double c)[ns];\n            for(int i=0;i<ns;i++) saRes[i]=((int[])res[i].t.Clone(),res[i].c);\n            Parallel.For(0,ns,new ParallelOptions{MaxDegreeOfParallelism=cores},idx=>{\n                var tt=saRes[idx].t; var cc2=saRes[idx].c;\n                SA(tt,ref cc2,rem-2000,42+idx*7);\n                saRes[idx]=(tt,cc2);\n            });\n            int bi=0; for(int i=1;i<ns;i++) if(saRes[i].c<saRes[bi].c) bi=i;\n            return saRes[bi].t;\n        }\n        int bi2=0; for(int i=1;i<ns;i++) if(res[i].c<res[bi2].c) bi2=i;\n        var bst=res[bi2].t; double bc=res[bi2].c;\n        if(rem>2000) SA(bst,ref bc,rem-1000);\n        return bst;\n    }\n}\n```\n\nThis looks good to me.
