I just realized there\'s a potential issue with the formula in the adjacents swap in DS:\n\n```csharp\nif(j==i+1){int a=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,b=t[i],c=t[j],d=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n    return Ec(a,c)+Ec(c,b)+Ec(b,d)-Ec(a,b)-Ec(b,c)-Ec(c,d);}\n```\n\nThis swaps adjacent elements b=t[i] and c=t[j]=t[i+1]. After swap:\n- a → c → b → d (where c=t[i+1], b=t[i])\n\nDelta = new_cost - old_cost = (Ec(a,c)+Ec(c,b)+Ec(b,d)) - (Ec(a,b)+Ec(b,c)+Ec(c,d)) ✓\n\nBut since the cost matrix is symmetric (Ec(c,b) = Ec(b,c)), this simplifies to:\nDelta = Ec(a,c) + Ec(c,b) + Ec(b,d) - Ec(a,b) - Ec(b,c) - Ec(c,d)\n      = Ec(a,c) + Ec(b,c) + Ec(b,d) - Ec(a,b) - Ec(b,c) - Ec(c,d)\n      = Ec(a,c) + Ec(b,d) - Ec(a,b) - Ec(c,d)\n      = D2(t, i, j)\n\nSo for adjacent swaps with symmetric costs, DS(i,i+1) == D2(i,i+1). The adjacent swap and 2-opt move produce the same result (both reverse a segment of length 2, which is equivalent to swapping the two elements). ✓\n\nThis is correct for our symmetric cost matrix.\n\nOkay, the code is correct. Final output coming up.\n\nActually, I want to reconsider one more time. The output format says "N integers: the visitation order of station indices (0..N-1)". So I output the order as a sequence of station indices. For example, if the optimal tour visits station 2, then 0, then 1, I output "2 0 1". This is what my code does: `Console.WriteLine(string.Join(" ", ans))` where `ans` is the array of station indices in visit order. ✓\n\nAlright, here is the final code. Let me write it out one more time cleanly:\n\nI want to pay attention to a few things:\n1. The LINQ `.Select` might not compile without `using System.Linq` - already included. ✓\n2. `StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries` - included in `using System`. ✓\n3. `Stopwatch` - needs `using System.Diagnostics`. ✓\n4. `Parallel.For` - needs `using System.Threading.Tasks`. ✓\n5. `CultureInfo.InvariantCulture` - needs `using System.Globalization`. ✓\n\nAll good. Here\'s the final code:', 'csharp_code': 'using System;\nusing System.Linq;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\nusing System.Diagnostics;\nusing System.Globalization;\n\nclass Program {\n    static double MU;\n    static int N;\n    static double[,] C;\n    static readonly Stopwatch Sw = Stopwatch.StartNew();\n\n    static void Main() {\n        string[] f = (Console.ReadLine() ?? "").Trim().Split(new[]{\' \',\'\\t\'}, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);\n        N = int.Parse(f[0]);\n        MU = double.Parse(f[1], CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);\n        double[][] rv = new double[N+1][];\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N; i++)\n            rv[i] = (Console.ReadLine() ?? "").Trim().Split(new[]{\' \',\'\\t\'}, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries)\n                    .Select(s => double.Parse(s, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)).ToArray();\n        C = new double[N+1, N+1];\n        for (int i = 0; i <= N; i++)\n            for (int j = 0; j <= N; j++)\n                if (i != j) C[i,j] = DV(rv[i], rv[j]);\n        int[] ans = N==1 ? new[]{0} : N<=20 ? HK() : Large();\n        Console.WriteLine(string.Join(" ", ans));\n    }\n\n    static double SMA(double[] r) {\n        double mag = Math.Sqrt(r[0]*r[0]+r[1]*r[1]+r[2]*r[2]);\n        double E = 0.5*(r[3]*r[3]+r[4]*r[4]+r[5]*r[5]) - MU/mag;\n        return E<0 ? -MU/(2*E) : -1;\n    }\n    static double Inc(double[] r) {\n        double hx=r[1]*r[5]-r[2]*r[4],hy=r[2]*r[3]-r[0]*r[5],hz=r[0]*r[4]-r[1]*r[3];\n        double h=Math.Sqrt(hx*hx+hy*hy+hz*hz);\n        return h>1e-10 ? Math.Acos(Math.Max(-1.0,Math.Min(1.0,hz/h))) : 0;\n    }\n    static double DV(double[] r1, double[] r2) {\n        double a1=SMA(r1),a2=SMA(r2);\n        if (a1<=0||a2<=0) {\n            double dx=r2[3]-r1[3],dy=r2[4]-r1[4],dz=r2[5]-r1[5];\n            return Math.Sqrt(dx*dx+dy*dy+dz*dz);\n        }\n        double di=Math.Abs(Inc(r1)-Inc(r2)),aT=(a1+a2)/2;\n        double vc1=Math.Sqrt(MU/a1),vc2=Math.Sqrt(MU/a2);\n        double vT1=Math.Sqrt(MU*(2.0/a1-1.0/aT)),vT2=Math.Sqrt(MU*(2.0/a2-1.0/aT));\n        if (a1<=a2)\n            return Math.Abs(vT1-vc1)+Math.Sqrt(vc2*vc2+vT2*vT2-2*vc2*vT2*Math.Cos(di));\n        return Math.Sqrt(vc1*vc1+vT1*vT1-2*vc1*vT1*Math.Cos(di))+Math.Abs(vT2-vc2);\n    }\n\n    static double Ec(int a, int b) {\n        if (b<0) return 0;\n        return C[a<0?0:a+1,b+1];\n    }\n    static double TC(int[] t) {\n        double c=Ec(-1,t[0]); for(int i=1;i<t.Length;i++) c+=Ec(t[i-1],t[i]); return c;\n    }\n\n    static int[] HK() {\n        int full=1<<N;\n        double[] dp=new double[full*N];\n        short[] par=new short[full*N];\n        for(int i=0;i<dp.Length;i++){dp[i]=double.MaxValue/2;par[i]=-1;}\n        for(int i=0;i<N;i++) dp[(1<<i)*N+i]=C[0,i+1];\n        for(int mask=1;mask<full;mask++) {\n            int mN=mask*N;\n            for(int last=0;last<N;last++) {\n                if((mask&(1<<last))==0) continue;\n                double d=dp[mN+last]; if(d>=double.MaxValue/2) continue;\n                for(int nxt=0;nxt<N;nxt++) {\n                    if((mask&(1<<nxt))!=0) continue;\n                    double nd=d+C[last+1,nxt+1];\n                    int idx=(mask|(1<<nxt))*N+nxt;\n                    if(nd<dp[idx]){dp[idx]=nd;par[idx]=(short)last;}\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        int fM=full-1,fB=fM*N,best=0;\n        for(int i=1;i<N;i++) if(dp[fB+i]<dp[fB+best]) best=i;\n        int[] path=new int[N]; int cur=best,msk=fM;\n        for(int s=N-1;s>=0;s--){path[s]=cur;int p=par[msk*N+cur];msk^=(1<<cur);cur=p;}\n        return path;\n    }\n\n    static int[] Greedy(int first) {\n        bool[] vis=new bool[N]; int[] t=new int[N]; int cur=first,s0=0;\n        if(first>=0){t[0]=first;vis[first]=true;s0=1;}\n        for(int s=s0;s<N;s++){double best=double.MaxValue;int bj=0;\n            for(int j=0;j<N;j++) if(!vis[j]){double c=Ec(cur,j);if(c<best){best=c;bj=j;}}\n            t[s]=bj;vis[bj]=true;cur=bj;}\n        return t;\n    }\n\n    static void TwoOpt(int[] t) {\n        bool imp=true; while(imp){imp=false;\n            for(int i=0;i<N-1;i++) for(int j=i+2;j<N;j++) {\n                int a=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,b=t[i],c=t[j],d=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n                if(Ec(a,c)+Ec(b,d)<Ec(a,b)+Ec(c,d)-1e-10){Array.Reverse(t,i,j-i+1);imp=true;}\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    static void OrOpt(int[] t, int sl) {\n        bool imp=true; while(imp){imp=false;\n            for(int i=0;i<=N-sl;i++) {\n                int prev=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,fs=t[i],ls=t[i+sl-1],aft=(i+sl<N)?t[i+sl]:-1;\n                double gR=Ec(prev,fs)+Ec(ls,aft)-Ec(prev,aft);\n                int bj=int.MinValue; double bg=1e-10;\n                for(int j=-1;j<N;j++) {\n                    if(j>=i-1&&j<i+sl) continue;\n                    int A=j<0?-1:t[j],B=j+1<N?t[j+1]:-1;\n                    double g=gR+Ec(A,B)-Ec(A,fs)-Ec(ls,B);\n                    if(g>bg){bg=g;bj=j;}\n                }\n                if(bj>int.MinValue){ApplySeg(t,i,sl,bj);imp=true;break;}\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    static void ApplySeg(int[] t, int from, int sl, int ia) {\n        int[] seg=new int[sl]; Array.Copy(t,from,seg,0,sl);\n        if(ia<from){\n            for(int k=from-1;k>=ia+1;k--) t[k+sl]=t[k];\n            for(int k=0;k<sl;k++) t[ia+1+k]=seg[k];\n        } else {\n            for(int k=from;k<=ia-sl;k++) t[k]=t[k+sl];\n            for(int k=0;k<sl;k++) t[ia-sl+1+k]=seg[k];\n        }\n    }\n\n    static double DS(int[] t, int i, int j) {\n        if(i>j){int tmp=i;i=j;j=tmp;}\n        if(j==i+1){\n            int a=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,b=t[i],c=t[j],d=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n            return Ec(a,c)+Ec(c,b)+Ec(b,d)-Ec(a,b)-Ec(b,c)-Ec(c,d);\n        }\n        int pi=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,ni=t[i+1],pj=t[j-1],nj=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n        return Ec(pi,t[j])+Ec(t[j],ni)+Ec(pj,t[i])+Ec(t[i],nj)\n             -Ec(pi,t[i])-Ec(t[i],ni)-Ec(pj,t[j])-Ec(t[j],nj);\n    }\n    static double D2(int[] t, int i, int j) {\n        int a=(i>0)?t[i-1]:-1,b=t[i],c=t[j],d=(j<N-1)?t[j+1]:-1;\n        return Ec(a,c)+Ec(b,d)-Ec(a,b)-Ec(c,d);\n    }\n    static double DR(int[] t, int from, int ia) {\n        int nd=t[from],pv=(from>0)?t[from-1]:-1,nx=(from<N-1)?t[from+1]:-1;\n        double gR=Ec(pv,nd)+Ec(nd,nx)-Ec(pv,nx);\n        int A=ia<0?-1:t[ia],B=ia+1<N?t[ia+1]:-1;\n        return -(gR+Ec(A,B)-Ec(A,nd)-Ec(nd,B));\n    }\n\n    static void SA(int[] tour, ref double best, long ms, int seed=42) {\n        if(ms<=0) return;\n        int[] cur=(int[])tour.Clone(); double cc=best;\n        Random rng=new Random(seed);\n        double T0=best/N*0.5,Tf=T0*1e-5;\n        if(T0<=1e-9){T0=0.01;Tf=1e-11;}\n        if(Tf<=0) Tf=1e-15;\n        long t0=Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds,t1=t0+ms;\n        while(true){\n            long tn=Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds; if(tn>=t1) break;\n            double prog=Math.Min(1.0,(double)(tn-t0)/ms);\n            double T=T0*Math.Pow(Tf/T0,prog); if(T<Tf) T=Tf;\n            for(int k=0;k<10000;k++){\n                int mt=rng.Next(3),a=rng.Next(N),b; double d;\n                if(mt==0){b=rng.Next(N);if(b==a)continue;d=DS(cur,a,b);}\n                else if(mt==1){b=rng.Next(N);if(b==a)continue;if(a>b){int tmp=a;a=b;b=tmp;}d=D2(cur,a,b);}\n                else{b=rng.Next(N+1)-1;if(b==a-1||b==a)continue;d=DR(cur,a,b);}\n                if(d<=0||rng.NextDouble()<Math.Exp(-d/T)){\n                    if(mt==0){int tmp=cur[a];cur[a]=cur[b];cur[b]=tmp;}\n                    else if(mt==1) Array.Reverse(cur,a,b-a+1);\n                    else ApplySeg(cur,a,1,b);\n                    cc+=d;\n                    if(cc<best-1e-10){best=cc;Array.Copy(cur,tour,N);}\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    static int[] Large() {\n        int cores=Math.Min(64,Environment.ProcessorCount);\n        int ns=Math.Min(cores,N+1);\n        var res=new (int[] t,double c)[ns];\n        Parallel.For(0,ns,new ParallelOptions{MaxDegreeOfParallelism=cores},idx=>{\n            int s=idx==0?-1:(idx-1)%N;\n            int[] t=Greedy(s); TwoOpt(t); OrOpt(t,1);OrOpt(t,2);OrOpt(t,3); TwoOpt(t);\n            res[idx]=(t,TC(t));\n        });\n        long rem=270000-Sw.ElapsedMilliseconds;\n        if(rem>5000){\n            var saRes=new (int[] t,double c)[ns];\n            for(int i=0;i<ns;i++) saRes[i]=((int[])res[i].t.Clone(),res[i].c);\n            Parallel.For(0,ns,new ParallelOptions{MaxDegreeOfParallelism=cores},idx=>{\n                var tt=saRes[idx].t; var cc2=saRes[idx].c;\n                SA(tt,ref cc2,rem-2000,42+idx*7);\n                saRes[idx]=(tt,cc2);\n            });\n            int bi=0; for(int i=1;i<ns;i++) if(saRes[i].c<saRes[bi].c) bi=i;\n            return saRes[bi].t;\n        }\n        int bi2=0; for(int i=1;i<ns;i++) if(res[i].c<res[bi2].c) bi2=i;\n        var bst=res[bi2].t; double bc=res[bi2].c;\n        if(rem>2000) SA(bst,ref bc,rem-1000);\n        return bst;\n    }\n}'}
